# physics.ins-det [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Measurements of the micro-spill structure of medical cyclotron and synchrotron beams and its impact on pulse pileup](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07508)
*Matthias Knopf,Simon Waid,Stefan Gundacker,Sebastian Onder,Daniel Radmanovac,Philipp Gaggl,Giulio Bordieri,Francesco Cordoni,Marta Missiaggia,Enrico Verroi,Giulio Magrin,Thomas Bergauer,Albert Hirtl*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本研究利用碳化硅（SiC）粒子传感器结合6 GHz高频读出系统，在亚纳秒时间尺度上测量了医用回旋加速器和同步加速器的束流微脉冲时间结构（micro-spill structure），为评估堆积效应（pileup）和设计下一代读出电子学提供了关键约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子物理实验需要单粒子分辨能力，堆积效应（pileup）会严重降低数据质量，因此精确掌握束流时间结构（beam time structure）对于选择适当的读出参数至关重要。然而，加速器设施通常不提供这类信息，且实验测定十分困难。

Method: 采用碳化硅（silicon carbide, SiC）粒子传感器耦合高频读出系统。SiC因其高载流子饱和速度（carrier saturation velocity）和耐受高偏压（bias voltage）能力，适用于快速读出和精确时间测量。研究使用6 GHz读出系统配合定制SiC二极管，在亚纳秒（sub-nanosecond）时间尺度上表征了回旋加速器（cyclotron）和同步加速器（synchrotron）束流的微脉冲结构（micro-spill structure）。

Result: 测得的到达时间分布（arrival-time distributions）呈现与加速器射频（RF）频率一致的调制模式，反映了束流提取过程（extraction process）的特征。分辨出的微脉冲结构使得堆积效应（pileup contributions）得以定量估算。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了束流时间结构表征对于精密读出系统开发的重要性，并为未来读出电子学（readout electronics）的设计提供了约束条件。

Abstract: Detector characterization and instrumentation testing are often performed at cyclotron and synchrotron facilities, many of which were originally developed for medical applications in cancer therapy. For particle physics experiments requiring a single-particle resolution, pileup can significantly degrade data quality, making precise knowledge of the beam time structure essential for selecting appropriate readout parameters. However, such information is often unavailable from the facilities and challenging to determine experimentally. Here, we report measurements of the spill time structure at two medical accelerator facilities using a silicon carbide (SiC) particle sensor coupled to a high-frequency readout system. Owing to its high carrier saturation velocity and the tolerance to large bias voltages, SiC is well suited for fast readout and measurements requiring precise timing. Using a 6 GHz readout with custom SiC diodes, we characterize the micro-spill structure of both cyclotron and synchrotron beams on a sub-nanosecond timescale. The measured arrival-time distributions exhibit modulation with the accelerator RF frequencies, reflecting features of the extraction process. The resolved micro-spill structure enables quantitative estimation of pileup contributions and provides design constraints for future readout electronics. The presented results emphasize the importance of the characterization of the beam time-structure characterization for the development of precise readout systems.

</details>


### [2] [Track and Vertex Reconstruction with the ATLAS Inner Detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07585)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文描述了ATLAS内部探测器（Inner Detector）中用于带电粒子重建（charged-particle reconstruction）和初级顶点重建（primary vertex reconstruction）的算法，并展示了在Run 2（2015–2018）和Run 3（2022–2026）部分数据（2022年起）及对应模拟数据上的性能表现。在高达80个同时发生的质子-质子对撞（proton-proton interaction）条件下，该方法保持了高效率、关键参数的良好分辨率以及低误重建率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电粒子重建是多用途高能物理探测器（multi-purpose high-energy physics detectors）中事件重建（event reconstruction）的基础环节。论文旨在系统描述ATLAS内部探测器（Inner Detector）中用于带电粒子和初级顶点重建的算法及其最新软件配置，并评估其在Run 2和Run 3数据条件下的实际性能。

Method: 论文介绍了ATLAS内部探测器（Inner Detector）中带电粒子重建和初级顶点重建所使用的算法，以及为数据采集部署的最新软件配置（software configuration）。重建性能通过对Run 2（2015–2018）数据、Run 3（2022–2026）中自2022年起的一部分数据以及相应模拟数据（simulated data）的处理结果进行评估。

Result: 在高达80个同时发生的质子-质子对撞（proton-proton interaction）条件下，该重建方法在Run 2和Run 3条件下均保持了高效率（high efficiency）、关键参数的良好分辨率（good resolution）以及低误重建率（low rates of mis-reconstructed candidates）。

Conclusion: ATLAS内部探测器的带电粒子和顶点重建算法在Run 2和Run 3的高对撞率条件下表现出稳健的性能，能够有效应对高亮度环境下的重建挑战。

Abstract: Charged-particle reconstruction is a fundamental part of the event reconstruction in modern multi-purpose high-energy physics detectors. This paper describes the algorithms used to reconstruct charged particles and primary vertices with the ATLAS Inner Detector. The most recent software configuration deployed for data-taking is described, and the performance obtained when this software is used to process Run 2 (2015-2018) data, a subset (from 2022) of Run 3 (2022-2026) data, and corresponding simulated data is presented. The ATLAS track and vertex reconstruction performance is shown for up to 80 simultaneous proton-proton interaction. It maintains a high efficiency, good resolution for key parameters, and low rates of mis-reconstructed candidates for Run 2 and Run 3 conditions.

</details>


### [3] [Optimisation of TES design for the CRESST experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07592)
*G. Angloher,S. Banik,A. Bento,A. Bertolini,R. Breier,C. Bucci,J. Burkhart,L. Burmeister,L. Canonica,E. Cipelli,S. Di Lorenzo,J. Dohm,F. Dominsky,A. Erb,E. Fascione,F. v. Feilitzsch,S. Fichtinger,D. Fuchs,V. M. Ghete,P. Gorla,P. V. Guillaumon,S. Gupta,D. Hauff,M. Ješkovský,J. Jochum,M. Kaznacheeva,H. Kluck,H. Kraus,B. von Krosigk,A. Langenkämper,M. Mancuso,B. Mauri,V. Mokina,C. Moore,P. Murali,M. Olmi,T. Ortmann,C. Pagliarone,L. Pattavina,F. Petricca,W. Potzel,P. Povinec,F. Pröbst,F. Pucci,F. Reindl,J. Rothe,K. Schäffner,J. Schieck,S. Schönert,C. Schwertner,M. Stahlberg,L. Stodolsky,C. Strandhagen,R. Strauss,I. Usherov,M. Zanirato,V. Zema*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文针对CRESST实验中用于亚GeV暗物质直接探测的W-TES传感器，研究了其声子收集器的厚度、尺寸与材料组成对探测器性能的影响，优化后显著提升了信噪比与整体性能，并建立了新的传感器基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CRESST实验旨在通过低温晶体靶上暗物质（dark matter）粒子与原子核的弹性散射，直接探测亚GeV质量的暗物质。为了进一步降低探测阈、提升信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio），需要对W-TES传感器进行系统优化。

Method: 方法上，本研究系统探讨了W-TES声子收集器（phonon collector）的厚度、尺寸和材料组成等几何与材料参数，并评估这些参数对探测器响应（detector response）的影响。研究基于实验数据进行性能对比分析。

Result: 优化后的W-TES传感器在信噪比与整体探测器性能方面取得了显著提升，并在CRESST所用传感器上建立了新的性能基准（benchmark）。

Conclusion: 研究证实，通过优化声子收集器的结构与材料参数可有效增强W-TES传感器性能，这有助于推动CRESST实验向更低暗物质质量（低至70 MeV/c²）的探测方向发展。

Abstract: The CRESST experiment aims at the direct detection of sub-GeV dark matter particles via elastic scattering off nuclei in different target crystals at cryogenic temperatures. The advancement in W-TES sensors allowed the CRESST detectors to reach energy thresholds of 10 eV and lower, opening the way to the exploration of dark matter masses as low as 70 MeV/c2. This work presents optimisation studies of W-TESs aimed at further improving the signal-to-noise ratio and overall detector performance. In particular, we investigate the thickness, dimensions and material composition of phonon collectors and assess their impact on detector response. The results demonstrate a significant performance enhancement and establish new benchmarks for the sensors used within CRESST.

</details>

# math.AP [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Asymptotic analysis of the energy for a ferroelectric nematic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06867)
*Dmitry Golovaty,Peter Sternberg*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明铁电向列（ferroelectric nematic）的变分模型在Γ-收敛（Γ-convergence）意义下趋向于高弹性各向异性（high elastic anisotropy）的向列相能量模型，揭示了两者在参数机制上的根本区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电向列的变分模型与微磁学（micromagnetics）中的标准能量模型在形式上高度相似，但两者描述的是截然不同的物理过程，且参数区间存在根本性差异。本文旨在澄清这一相似性背后的数学极限行为。

Method: 采用Γ-收敛（Γ-convergence）方法分析铁电向列能量泛函在特定参数极限下的渐近行为，并与高弹性各向异性向列相的能量模型进行比较。

Result: 建立了铁电向列能量泛函到高弹性各向异性向列相能量的Γ-收敛结果。

Conclusion: 尽管铁电向列与微磁学的能量模型在形式上类似，但两者处于根本不同的物理参数区间；通过Γ-收敛分析，铁电向列模型实际上趋近于高弹性各向异性的向列相能量。

Abstract: The variational model for a ferroelectric nematic bears close resemblance to the well-known energy model for micromagnetics. Despite this similarity, the two models operate in fundamentally distinct parameter regimes describing different physics. In this paper we establish that the ferroelectric nematic energy functional $Γ$-converges to the energy of a nematic with high elastic anisotropy.

</details>

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Rapid phase ordering of Ising dynamics on $\mathbb Z^2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08052)
*Reza Gheissari,Allan Sly*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明，在二维低温伊辛模型中，从有偏随机初始态出发的格劳伯动力学（Glauber dynamics）能够快速吸收到“全正”（all-plus）相。该结论通过一种时空多尺度耦合（spacetime multiscale coupling）方法推广至任意维度，将加性边界条件下混合时间的准多项式界提升为无边界条件下有偏初始化的快速相排序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在低温伊辛（Ising）模型中，从有偏且无序的初始态出发时，相排序（phase ordering）的收敛速度尚不明确。Fontes、Schonmann与Sidoravicius（2002）已证明零温情形下的快速吸收性质，但低温区域的行为仍需严格刻画。

Method: 采用时空多尺度耦合（spacetime multiscale coupling）方法，可在任意维度$d\ge 2$中，将加性边界条件下伊辛动力学混合时间（mixing time）的一致准多项式（uniform-in-$\beta$ quasi-polynomial）界，提升为无边界条件下有偏初始化的快速相排序结果。

Result: 在二维情形下，存在阈值$p_0<1$，使得当初始自旋（spin）独立同分布且$+1$概率$p>p_0$时，在任意低温$\beta>\beta_c$下运行的伊辛格劳伯动力学快速收敛到正相测度（plus phase measure）$\pi^+$。

Conclusion: 低温伊辛模型的快速相排序行为在整个低温柔区域均成立，且该结论可通过多尺度耦合方法推广到更高维度。

Abstract: We consider the phase ordering problem for the low-temperature Ising dynamics initialized from a biased and disordered initialization. Work of Fontes, Schonmann, Sidoravicius (2002) showed that at zero-temperature, Ising Glauber dynamics on $\mathbb Z^d$ for $d\ge 2$ initialized from i.i.d. spins on each vertex that are $+1$ with sufficiently large probability, absorbs into the all-plus configuration quickly. We prove that analogous behavior holds throughout the low-temperature regime of the Ising model in two dimensions. Namely, there exists $p_0 <1$ such that Ising Glauber dynamics initialized from i.i.d. spins that are $+1$ with probability $p>p_0$, run at any low temperature $β>β_c$ converges rapidly to the plus phase measure $π^+$.
  The result is proved using a spacetime multiscale coupling valid in any $d\ge 2$, that boosts a uniform-in-$β$ quasi-polynomial bound on the mixing time of Ising dynamics with plus boundary conditions, into rapid phase ordering from biased initializations with no boundary conditions.

</details>

# math-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [A Note on the Construction of Trial States for the Dilute Bose Gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06844)
*Morris Brooks,Jakob Oldenburg,Diane Saint Aubin*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文回顾了如何利用[11]中引入的局域粒子数截断（local particle number cutoff）来构造稀薄玻色气体（dilute Bose gas）的尝试态，这些态能够捕捉热力学极限下基态的实质性关联结构，并给出了李-黄-杨修正（Lee-Huang-Yang correction）作为基态能量上界的简化推导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确描述稀薄玻色气体在热力学极限下的基态关联结构是统计力学中的关键问题。此前对Lee-Huang-Yang修正的理论推导较为复杂，需要一种更简洁的方法来建立其上界估计。

Method: 采用[11]中提出的局域粒子数截断（local particle number cutoff）方法构造尝试态（trial states），并在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下利用该态进行能量上界的变分估计。

Result: 成功给出了Lee-Huang-Yang修正作为稀薄玻色气体基态能量上界的简化推导，验证了该尝试态能有效捕捉热力学极限下的基态关联结构。

Conclusion: 局域粒子数截断的尝试态方法为描述稀薄玻色气体的基态关联提供了一种有效途径，并使得Lee-Huang-Yang修正的上界证明得以简化。

Abstract: We review how the local particle number cutoff introduced in [11] is used to build trial states for the dilute Bose gas that capture the substantial correlation structure of the ground state in the thermodynamic limit. In particular, we provide a simplified derivation of the Lee-Huang-Yang correction as an upper bound for the ground state energy.

</details>


### [7] [Quantitative propagation of chaos for Lindblad dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06973)
*Nina H. Amini,Sofiane Chalal*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了由N体林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation）描述的开量子系统（open quantum system）的平均场极限（mean-field limit），证明了在量子相对熵（quantum relative entropy）意义下，N粒子动力学收敛到极限非线性方程的积分解，并建立了阶数为1/N的相对熵显式上界，从而提供了混沌传播（propagation of chaos）的定量刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在开放量子多体系统中，平均场极限的严格数学分析尚不充分，特别是在量子相对熵框架下的定量收敛结果缺乏。本文旨在填补这一空白，为N体林德布拉德方程的平均场行为提供严格的定量理论。

Method: 采用量子相对熵作为度量工具，研究N体开放量子系统的平均场极限。通过推导N粒子密度算符（density operator）与对应乘积态（product state）之间相对熵的显式边界，建立收敛速率为1/N的定量混沌传播结果。

Result: 证明了N粒子动力学在量子相对熵意义下收敛到极限非线性方程的积分解（tensorized solution），且收敛速率为1/N的显式上界。该结果为开放量子系统中的混沌传播提供了定量性保证。

Conclusion: 本文首次在量子相对熵框架下，为N体林德布拉德方程的平均场极限建立了1/N量级的定量混沌传播结果，从数学上严格刻画了开放量子系统在平均场极限下的渐近行为。

Abstract: We consider an open quantum system governed $N$-body Lindblad equation and study mean-field limits in this setting. We prove that the $N$-particle dynamics converges, in the sense of quantum relative entropy, to the tensorized solution of the limiting nonlinear equation. More precisely, we establish explicit bounds of order $1/N$ on the relative entropy between the $N$-particle density operator and the corresponding product state, thereby providing a quantitative propagation of chaos.

</details>


### [8] [Volume-Independent Spectral Stability of Energy-Truncated Effective Hamiltonians in Quantum Spin Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07410)
*Ayumi Ukai*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对有界有限程量子自旋系统（bounded finite-range quantum spin systems）证明了一个体积极限一致有效哈密顿量定理（volume-uniform effective-Hamiltonian theorem）。通过构造能量截断哈密顿量并建立体积极限一致的谱重叠界（volume-uniform spectral-overlap bound），该定理在有限体积下保证了低能本征值的稳定性，在无限体积的热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下则通过GNS表示（GNS representation）给出了相应的谱重叠估计。该工作推广并强化了Arad、Kuwahara和Landau先前的有效哈密顿量机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子多体系统中，有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）方法常用于将高能自由度“积分掉”，从而简化低能物理的描述。然而，以往的构造（如Arad, Kuwahara和Landau的工作）主要依赖于有限体积下的算子范数（operator-norm）表述，无法直接推广到热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下的无限体积系统。本文旨在建立一种体积极限一致的谱重叠表述，使得有效哈密顿量方法在无限体积下仍然成立。

Method: 首先，对任意有限目标区域构造一个能量截断哈密顿量（energy-truncated Hamiltonian）。然后，证明一个体积极限一致的谱重叠界（volume-uniform spectral-overlap bound），该界控制了截断哈密顿量的低能谱子空间（low-energy spectral subspace）渗漏（leakage）到原始哈密顿量高能谱子空间（high-energy spectral subspace）的程度。该界允许包含非指数型的谱窗项（non-exponential spectral-window terms），但其截断相关的余项呈指数衰减（exponentially decaying in the cutoff）。在无限体积情形下，该估计在无穷体积基态（infinite-volume ground state）的GNS表示（GNS representation）中建立。

Result: 在有限体积下，该构造保证了低能本征值（low-lying eigenvalues）的稳定性，且本征值误差受控于指数小的截断相关余项。在无限体积下，在GNS表示中证明了相应的谱重叠估计。因此，本文通过将有限体积的算子范数表述替换为适用于热力学极限的体积极限一致谱重叠表述，扩展并强化了Arad、Kuwahara和Landau的有效哈密顿量机制。

Conclusion: 本文为有界有限程量子自旋系统提供了一个在热力学极限下仍然适用的有效哈密顿量框架。该结果建立了体积极限一致的谱重叠控制，使得有效哈密顿量方法能够从有限体积严格推广到无限体积系统，为量子多体系统的低能有效理论研究提供了更强大的数学工具。

Abstract: We prove a volume-uniform effective-Hamiltonian theorem for bounded finite-range quantum spin systems on possibly infinite lattices. For any finite target region, we construct an energy-truncated Hamiltonian and prove a volume-uniform spectral-overlap bound controlling the leakage of its low-energy spectral subspace into the high-energy spectral subspace of the original Hamiltonian. The bound may contain non-exponential spectral-window terms, but its cutoff-dependent remainder decays exponentially in the cutoff.
  In finite volume, this yields stability of low-lying eigenvalues, with eigenvalue errors controlled by the exponentially small cutoff-dependent remainder. In infinite volume, we prove the corresponding spectral-overlap estimate in the GNS representation of an infinite-volume ground state. Thus, for bounded finite-range interactions, we extend and strengthen the effective-Hamiltonian mechanism of Arad, Kuwahara, and Landau by replacing the finite-volume operator-norm formulation with a volume-uniform spectral-overlap formulation applicable in the thermodynamic limit.

</details>


### [9] [Superintegrability in the interaction of two particles with spin: First-order pseudo-scalar integrals of motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07659)
*Fatih Turkkan,O. Ogulcan Tuncer,I. Yurdusen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从最一般的旋转不变哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）出发，将最一般的赝标量算符（pseudo-scalar operator）构造为动量（momenta）的矩阵多项式形式；通过施加该算符与哈密顿量的对易关系（commutativity），导出确定方程组（system of determining equations）并求解，从而完成分类。

Result: 获得了此类超可积系统的完整分类，并确定了相应的赝标量运动积分；结果提供了具有自旋依赖相互作用的新族超可积系统，丰富了与核子-核子相互作用（nucleon–nucleon interactions）相关的可积模型。

Conclusion: 该分类为超可积量子自旋系统的更广泛分类计划做出了贡献；对选定的情况进一步构造了运动积分生成的多项式对称代数（polynomial symmetry algebras），加深了对系统代数结构的理解。

Abstract: In recent work, we initiated a research program aimed at the systematic investigation of quantum superintegrable systems describing the interaction of two non-relativistic spin-$1/2$ particles in three-dimensional Euclidean space. In that study, we classified all such superintegrable systems admitting additional first-order scalar integrals of motion. In the present paper, we continue this program by focusing on systems that admit additional pseudo-scalar integrals of motion. Starting from the most general rotationally invariant Hamiltonian for two interacting spin-$1/2$ particles, we construct the most general first-order pseudo-scalar operator in the form of a matrix polynomial in the momenta. Imposing the commutativity of this operator with the Hamiltonian leads to a system of determining equations. By solving these equations, we obtain a complete classification of such superintegrable systems and determine the corresponding pseudo-scalar integrals of motion. The resulting classification provides new families of superintegrable systems with spin-dependent interactions. These systems enrich the class of integrable models relevant to nucleon--nucleon interactions and contribute to the broader program of classifying superintegrable quantum systems with spin. For selected cases, we further construct the associated polynomial symmetry algebras generated by the integrals of motion, providing additional insight into the algebraic structure of the systems.

### [10] [Hamiltonian formulation of the supersymmetric KdV equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08065)
*Ali Pazarci,Nadir Ghazanfari,Ilmar Gahramanov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文对超对称KdV（supersymmetric Korteweg-de Vries）方程进行了约束哈密顿量（constrained Hamiltonian）形式化研究，发现该系统与其经典版本类似，是一个受约束系统。通过选取自由参数 $a=2$，获得了非平凡拉格朗日量描述，并运用狄拉克-贝尔格曼算法（Dirac-Bergmann algorithm）确定了完整的初级与次级约束，构建了总哈密顿量（total Hamiltonian）。研究揭示了涉及费米子场（fermionic fields）的非平凡约束以及哈密顿量密度中的非局域贡献（nonlocal contribution），最终在分量形式和超空间表示（superspace representation）中验证了形式化的自洽性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典KdV方程在哈密顿体系中已被广泛研究，但其超对称扩展版本的约束结构尚待澄清。本文旨在填补这一空白，为超对称KdV方程建立系统的约束哈密顿量形式化框架。

Method: 采用狄拉克-贝尔格曼算法分析超对称KdV方程的约束结构；选取超对称扩展中的自由参数 $a=2$ 以得到非平凡拉格朗日量描述；从退化拉格朗日量出发，依次确定初级约束与次级约束，并构建总哈密顿量；通过一致性条件（consistency conditions）推导约束体系中的非局域贡献。

Result: 明确了完整的初级与次级约束集合，构建了总哈密顿量；发现除涉及费米子场的非平凡约束外，一致性条件还引入了哈密顿量密度中的非局域贡献；推导出的哈密顿运动方程（Hamilton equations of motion）以分量形式正确再现了超对称KdV系统；最终获得的超空间表示与分量层面形式化结果一致。

Conclusion: 超对称KdV方程具有与经典版本类似的约束系统结构，但其超对称扩展带来了新的非局域特征。本文建立的约束哈密顿量形式化和超空间表示为该系统的进一步量子化与可积性研究提供了基础。

Abstract: We studied the constrained Hamiltonian formulation of a supersymmetric Korteweg-de Vries (KdV) equation, which is observed to be a constrained system similar to its classical version. We found a nontrivial Lagrangian description, where we select $a=2$ for the free parameter $a$ in the supersymmetric extension. The corresponding degenerate Lagrangian requires an exclusive consideration and the utilization of the Dirac-Bergmann algorithm. We explicitly determined the full set of primary and secondary constraints and constructed the total Hamiltonian governing the dynamics of the system. In this analysis, in addition to a nontrivial constraint involving the fermionic fields, the consistency conditions give rise to a nonlocal contribution to the Hamiltonian density. This highlights a distinctive feature of this supersymmetric extension. We showed that the resulting Hamilton equations of motion reproduce the supersymmetric KdV system in the component form. Finally, we derived a compact superspace representation of the Hamiltonian and demonstrated its consistency with the component-level formulation.

### [11] [Learning Minimal-Deviation Corrections for Multi-Dimensional Mismodelling in HEP Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07460)
*Matthias Schott,Lucie Flek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种基于神经网络的蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo, MC）修正方法，在仅有一维（1D）目标分布信息且无法获取完整多维相关性的约束下，通过最小偏离原则学习模拟事件的变换，从而修正误建模特征并保持全局相关结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理中精确的蒙特卡罗模拟面临挑战，尤其在复杂场景中模拟无法复现观测数据；实际实验信息常局限于一个维度（one-dimensional, 1D）的分布，而误建模（mismodelling）却发生在多维特征空间中，传统的一维重加权（reweighting）方法忽略特征间相关性，而全多维方法需要大量目标数据集，在实际中难以实现。

Method: 提出一种基于神经网络的方法，在仅能获取一维目标分布的约束下，学习对模拟事件的一种变换（transformation），使得变换后的分布与可用的一维目标分布一致，同时尽可能保持与原始模拟的接近。该方法遵循最小偏离原则（minimal-deviation principle），在修正误建模特征的同时保留基线模型（baseline model）的全局相关结构。

Result: 通过基于模拟伪数据（pseudo-data）的控制研究（controlled studies）表明，该方法能够改善与目标分布的一致性，并维持一致的多维结构（multidimensional structure）。

Conclusion: 该方法专为传统技术无法胜任的复杂高维分析场景设计，提供了一种在有限信息条件下可扩展的蒙特卡罗模拟增强方案。

Abstract: Accurate Monte Carlo (MC) modelling in high-energy physics is challenging, particularly in complex scenarios where simulations fail to reproduce observed data. In practice, experimental information is often limited to one-dimensional (1D) distributions, while mismodelling arises in a multidimensional feature space. This restricts traditional correction methods, as one-dimensional reweighting ignores correlations and fully multidimensional approaches require large target datasets. We propose a neural network-based method that operates under these constraints by learning a transformation of simulated events that reproduces the available 1D target distributions while remaining close to the original simulation. This minimal-deviation principle preserves the global correlation structure of the baseline model while enabling targeted corrections of mismodelled features. Using controlled studies with simulated pseudo-data, we show that the method improves agreement with target distributions and maintains a consistent multidimensional structure. The approach is designed for complex, high-dimensional analyses where traditional techniques are insufficient, providing a scalable way to enhance MC modelling under limited information.

### [12] [Uncovering Hidden Systematics in Neural Network Models for High Energy Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07470)
*Lucie Flek,Philipp Alexander Jungs,Akbar Karimi,Timo Saala,Alexander Schmid,Matthias Schott,Philipp Soldin,Christopher Wiebusch,Ulrich Willemsen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对高能物理（HEP）中神经网络（NN）模型系统不确定性（systematic uncertainty）难以估计的问题，受对抗攻击（adversarial-attack）研究启发，展示输入观测量的微小扰动（在实验不确定性允差范围内）可显著改变网络输出，并据此提出一种量化框架以探测和评估NN对实验变化的隐藏敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理分析中，神经网络（neural network, NN）对输入特征的微小变化高度敏感，导致系统不确定性的传播与估计成为开放挑战；现有方法（如控制区域导出或标称变化）可能低估真实模型不确定性，使偏差未被充分计入。

Method: 受机器学习对抗攻击（adversarial-attack）的启发，在实验不确定性允差范围内对输入观测量施加微妙扰动，保持其一维分布和相关分布几乎不变，然后在代表性HEP任务（事件分类与对象识别）及多种网络架构上测试扰动对输出的影响。

Result: 在设定的不确定性包络（uncertainty envelope）内，神经网络可以被系统地、以显著比例地“欺骗”（fooled），即输出发生大幅变化。

Conclusion: 基于上述观察，引入一个定量框架用于探测和度量神经网络对现实实验变化的隐藏敏感性（hidden sensitivity），从而在物理分析中提供一条评估与控制系统不确定性的实用路径。

Abstract: Neural networks (NNs) are inherently multidimensional classifiers that learn complex, non-linear relationships among input observables. While their flexibility enables unprecedented performance in high-energy physics (HEP) analyses, it also makes them sensitive to small variations in their inputs. Consequently, the propagation and estimation of systematic uncertainties in NN-based models remain an open challenge. There are indications that uncertainties derived in control regions or from nominal variations of input features can underestimate the true model uncertainty, potentially leaving biases unaccounted for. Inspired by insights from adversarial-attack studies in machine learning, we explore how subtle perturbations, fully consistent with the experimental uncertainties on the input observables, can lead to substantial changes in NN outputs, while keeping the one-dimensional and correlated input distributions nearly unchanged. Using a set of representative HEP tasks, including event classification and object identification, and testing across a variety of network architectures, we demonstrate that networks can be systematically "fooled" at significant rates within the allowed uncertainty envelopes. Building on this observation, we introduce a quantitative framework to probe and measure the hidden sensitivity of neural networks to realistic experimental variations, providing a practical path to evaluate and control their systematic uncertainty in physics analyses.

### [13] [Transfer Learning Across Fast- and Full-Simulation Domains in High-Energy Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07471)
*Matthias Schott,Lucie Flek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了高能物理中基于快速模拟（fast simulation）预训练模型向全模拟（full simulation）数据迁移学习的效果，发现预训练模型在所有任务中均优于独立训练的基线模型，并可将所需目标域数据量减少约一半。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理（high-energy physics）中的机器学习模型通常依赖模拟数据训练，但全模拟样本计算成本高昂，而快速模拟虽能提供大量统计量但保真度较低。本文旨在系统研究如何利用迁移学习（transfer learning）将快速模拟训练的表征迁移到全模拟数据，以降低计算成本并提升数据效率。

Method: 在真实LHC（Large Hadron Collider）环境下，选取信号-背景分类（signal-background classification）、夸克-胶子喷注标记（quark-gluon jet tagging）和缺失横动量重建（missing transverse energy reconstruction）三个代表性任务，采用密集神经网络（dense neural network, DNN）、图神经网络（graph neural network, GNN）和基于Transformer的架构。模型先在ATLAS类快速模拟上预训练，再适配至CMS类快速模拟和全模拟ATLAS Open Data。

Result: 在所有任务中，预训练模型均持续优于独立训练的基线模型（independently trained baselines），且显著减少对目标域训练数据的需求，通常可将所需统计量降低约一半。

Conclusion: 快速模拟可用于学习鲁棒且可复用的表征（robust, reusable representations），这为将训练好的模型作为可复用的科学资产（reusable scientific assets）发布提供了支持，其意义不仅限于大型基础模型。

Abstract: Machine-learning models in high-energy physics are often trained on simulated data, where fully simulated samples are computationally expensive while fast simulation provides large statistics at reduced realism. In this work, we systematically study transfer learning between fast-simulated and fully simulated datasets in a realistic LHC environment. We consider three representative tasks, signal-background classification, quark-gluon jet tagging, and missing transverse energy reconstruction, using dense neural networks, graph neural networks, and transformer-based architectures. Models are pretrained on ATLAS-like fast simulation and adapted to CMS-like fast simulation and to fully simulated ATLAS Open Data. Across all tasks, pretrained models consistently outperform independently trained baselines and require significantly less target-domain training data, typically reducing the needed statistics by about a factor of two. These results demonstrate that fast simulation can be used to learn robust, reusable representations and motivate publishing trained models as reusable scientific assets beyond large foundation models.

</details>


### [14] [Susceptibilities and Patterning: A Primer on Linear Response in Bayesian Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07980)
*Chris Elliott,Daniel Murfet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文基于统计力学（statistical mechanics）中的磁化率（susceptibility）理论，将其推广到神经网络（neural networks）解释中，定义了观测量对数据扰动的磁化率，并建立了其与后验协方差、影响矩阵（influence matrix）以及结构磁化率矩阵（structural susceptibility matrix）之间的联系。该框架通过置换矩阵的伪逆提供了数据扰动与结构变化之间的线性化解，并从统计力学基础和损失景观（loss landscape）几何角度给出了详尽阐述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将统计力学中成熟的磁化率（susceptibility）理论引入神经网络解释领域，以建立数据扰动与模型结构变化之间的量化关联，并统一此前在贝叶斯影响函数（Bayesian influence function）和模式化问题（patterning problem）中的分散结果。

Method: 定义一个观测量（observable）φ 对数据扰动的磁化率为后验期望（posterior expectation）的导数；利用涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation–dissipation theorem）将其等价为后验协方差（posterior covariance）。通过选择不同的 φ 得到不同对象：每样本损失对应影响矩阵（influence matrix），分量局域观测量对应结构磁化率矩阵（structural susceptibility matrix）。该矩阵（在因子 nβ 下）是从数据分布（data distributions）到结构坐标（structural coordinates）映射的雅可比矩阵（Jacobian），其伪逆提供模式化问题的线性化解。

Result: 建立了磁化率理论在神经网络解释中的完整形式体系：定义了磁化率及其经验估计量（empirical estimators），揭示了其与损失景观（loss landscape）几何的联系，并给出了从统计力学基础到具体应用的系统性推导。

Conclusion: 磁化率理论为神经网络解释提供了一种具有统计力学根基的统一框架，能够通过数据扰动定量分析模型结构变化，并为模式化问题提供线性化解。

Abstract: These notes introduce the theory of susceptibilities as developed in [arXiv:2504.18274, arXiv:2601.12703] for interpreting neural networks. The susceptibility of an observable $φ$ to a data perturbation is defined as a derivative of a posterior expectation, which by the fluctuation--dissipation theorem equals a posterior covariance. Different choices of $φ$ yield different objects: per-sample losses give the influence matrix (the Bayesian influence function of [arXiv:2509.26544]), while component-localized observables give the structural susceptibility matrix that pairs model components with data patterns. The susceptibility matrix is (up to a factor of $nβ$) the Jacobian of the map from data distributions to structural coordinates; its pseudo-inverse provides a linearized solution to the patterning problem of [arXiv:2601.13548]: finding data perturbations that produce a desired structural change. We motivate the theory from its statistical-mechanical foundations, then give a detailed exposition of susceptibilities, their empirical estimators, and their connection to the geometry of the loss landscape.

</details>

### [15] [Breaking the Trade-off: Bulk 2D Ising Superconductivity with High Tc and Giant Interlayer Spacing via a Unique Chain Intercalation in (BaS)1/3TaS2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07336)
*Ziyi Zhu,Leiming Chen,Xiangqi Liu,Haonan Wang,Chen Xu,Ze Yan,Zhengyang Li,Wei Xia,Jiawei Luo,Na Yu,Xia Wang,Ke Qu,Zhenzhong Yang,Yanfeng Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过一种独特的链状插层策略，在(BaS)1/3TaS2中实现了大层间距与高超导转变温度(Tc)的兼得，打破了传统二维过渡金属硫族化物(TMD)超导体中层间距与Tc之间的长期折中关系，并获得了鲁棒的二维伊辛超导性(2D Ising superconductivity)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统插层体系中，要实现高超导转变温度(Tc)往往必须以减小层间距、削弱二维(2D)特性为代价，这种长期存在的折中关系限制了低维超导体的设计与性能提升。

Method: 采用链状插层策略，合成了一种新的多晶型物(BaS)1/3TaS2，在TaS2双层之间插入独特的Ba-S-S-Ba链状结构；通过结构演化抑制层间电子耦合，使得单个TaS2层内的局域反演对称性破缺(local inversion symmetry breaking)占据主导，从而防止体心对称相中伊辛自旋轨道场(Ising spin-orbit fields)的抵消效应。

Result: (BaS)1/3TaS2的双层间距达到12.75 Å，是原始2H-TaS2的三倍以上；在保持超大层间距的同时实现了增强的Tc，打破了传统上大层间距/高各向异性与高Tc不可兼得的矛盾；综合输运、磁性和热力学测量确认了其稳健的超导态。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种通用的插层框架，用于设计体材料(bulk-like)二维伊辛超导体，为调和相互竞争的材料需求提供了新路径，并拓展了伊辛超导性(Ising superconductivity)的研究范围。

Abstract: Two-dimensional (2D) transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) are promising platforms for low dimensional superconductivity. However, in conventional intercalated systems, achieving a high superconducting transition temperature (Tc) often comes at the expense of reduced interlayer spacing and weakened 2D character. Here, we overcome this long-standing compromise through a unique chain-like intercalation strategy. We report the synthesis and properties of a new polymorph, (BaS)1/3TaS2, in which a distinctive Ba-S-S-Ba chain structure is inserted between TaS2 bilayers. This unique configuration breaks the bulk c axis mirror symmetry while achieving exceptional interlayer decoupling, with an inter-bilayer spacing of 12.75 Å-more than three times that of pristine 2H-TaS2. By suppressing interlayer electronic coupling, this structural evolution allows local inversion symmetry breaking within individual TaS2 layers to dominate. This prevents compensation of the Ising spin-orbit fields typical of centrosymmetric bulk phases, enabling robust 2D Ising superconductivity. Remarkably, the compound exhibits an enhanced Tc without sacrificing its large interlayer spacing, thereby breaking the conventional trade-off between large spacing/high anisotropy and high Tc. Comprehensive transport, magnetic, and thermodynamic measurements confirm its robust superconducting state. Our work establishes a versatile intercalation framework for designing bulk-like 2D Ising superconductors, providing a new route to reconcile competing material demands and expanding the scope of Ising superconductivity research.

</details>


### [16] [Finite temperature pair density wave superconductivity in $d$-wave altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07656)
*Amrutha N Madhusuthanan,Madhuparna Karmakar*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过非微扰静态路径近似蒙特卡洛方法，证明二维d波交变磁体（altermagnet）可在无外磁场条件下稳定有限动量超导（finite-momentum superconductivity），并展现出鲁棒的配对密度波（pair-density-wave, PDW）相，同时识别了相相干、能隙闭合和赝能隙（pseudogap）形成的不同热力学尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索无需泽曼场（Zeeman field）即可实现有限动量超导的物理机制，解决传统方案依赖外加磁场或强自旋轨道耦合的限制。

Method: 采用非微扰静态路径近似蒙特卡洛（static path approximation Monte Carlo）方法，对二维d波交变磁体模型进行数值模拟。

Result: 1) d波交变磁体在有限温度窗口内支持鲁棒的PDW相；2) 动量依赖的自旋劈裂（momentum-dependent spin splitting）增强了有限质心动量下的配对不稳定性；3) 识别出相相干、能隙闭合和赝能隙形成三种不同的热力学尺度。

Conclusion: 交变磁体为热稳定性有限动量超导提供了一种无需外场的鲁棒实现路径，并在能谱和实空间特征上给出了可供实验检验的独特信号。

Abstract: We demonstrate that altermagnetism provides a field-free mechanism for stabilizing finite-momentum superconductivity in two dimensions. Using a non-perturbative static path approximation Monte Carlo approach, we show that a d-wave altermagnet supports a robust pair-density-wave (PDW) phase that persists over a finite temperature window despite strong thermal fluctuations. The underlying mechanism originates from momentum-dependent spin splitting, which effectively enhances pairing instabilities at finite center-of-mass momentum without Zeeman fields. We identify distinct thermal scales associated with phase coherence, gap closing, and pseudogap formation, and establish characteristic spectroscopic and real-space signatures of the PDW state. Our results reveal altermagnetism as a robust route to thermally stable finite-momentum superconductivity and provide experimentally testable signatures for altermagnetic materials.

</details>

### [17] [On the single-Hessian Gaussian wavepacket dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07440)
*Davide Barbiero,Jiří J. L. Vaníček*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了单海森高斯波包动力学（single-Hessian GWD）的辛几何推导，证明其守恒非正则辛结构并避免能量漂移；同时实现了高阶时间步进几何积分器，在保持精度可比的前提下大幅降低计算负担，并通过多个数值实验验证了其几何性质的守恒性和光谱计算的高效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 降低Heller局域谐波高斯波包动力学（local harmonic GWD）的计算负担，同时保持相近的光谱近似精度；进一步消除局域谐波版本中存在的能量漂移问题，并建立更严格的几何守恒性质。

Method: （1）给出单海森GWD运动方程的辛几何（symplectic）推导；（2）引入高阶时间步进几何积分器（geometric integrators），具有时间可逆性（time-reversible），并精确守恒波包范数和辛结构；（3）推导一般势能下高斯波包宽度的精确演化表达式，以及全局谐波势下整个波包的精确演化表达式；（4）在氨的第一激发态势能面上进行on-the-fly从头算高斯波包动力学数值验证。

Result: 单海森GWD守恒非正则辛结构，在光滑势中的有界动力学下避免了能量漂移；其渐近误差为$\mathcal{O}(\hbar)$量级，与局域谐波版本相同；高阶几何积分器在保持守恒性的同时提升了精度和计算效率；在二氟卡宾负离子的光电子谱和甲胺的吸收谱计算中，单海森GWD优于全局谐波模型，精度与局域谐波GWD相当。

Conclusion: 单海森GWD是一种兼具高计算效率和光谱精度的近似方法，其辛结构和能量守恒性质优于局域谐波版本；高阶几何积分器可进一步加速数值模拟；部分光谱特征对参考海森（reference Hessian）的选择敏感。

Abstract: Single-Hessian Gaussian wavepacket dynamics (GWD) significantly reduces the computational burden of Heller's local harmonic GWD, while maintaining comparable accuracy in approximating vibronic spectra. Here, we provide a new, symplectic derivation of the equations of motion of single-Hessian GWD and show that, unlike the local harmonic version, this method conserves the non-canonical symplectic structure on the manifold of Gaussian wavepackets and$-$for bounded dynamics in smooth potentials$-$avoids the drift of energy. Our numerical results suggest that, despite being much more efficient than the local harmonic variant, the single-Hessian GWD exhibits the same $\mathcal{O}(\hbar)$ asymptotic error in averages of observables. To further accelerate numerical simulations, we implement high-order time-stepping geometric integrators that are time-reversible and conserve the norm and symplectic structure exactly, regardless of the time step. In addition, we present explicit expressions for the exact evolution of the width of a single-Hessian Gaussian wavepacket in a general potential, as well as for the exact evolution of the whole wavepacket in a global harmonic potential. Using on-the-fly ab initio Gaussian wavepacket dynamics on the first excited-state surface of ammonia, we numerically confirm the conservation of geometric properties by these integrators and demonstrate that high-order integrators can enhance both accuracy and computational efficiency. We also compute the photoelectron spectrum of the difluorocarbene anion and the absorption spectrum of methylamine, and find that, in comparison with experiment, single-Hessian GWD outperforms global harmonic models and matches the accuracy of local harmonic GWD. Finally, we identify which spectral features are sensitive to the choice of reference Hessian.

</details>

### [18] [Functoriality of the KSGNS Construction for Intertwiners of Strict Positive $C^*$-Correspondences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08004)
*Lucus Brady,Ryan Grady*

Main category: math.OA

TL;DR: 本文证明了KSGNS构造可视为从固定C*-代数出发的正C*-对应（positive C*-correspondence）范畴上的一个自函子（endofunctor），并在此基础上为C*-动力系统（C*-dynamical systems）的严格正等变C*-对应（strict positive equivariant C*-correspondence）提供了函子化视角，证明该类对应在KSGNS构造下可唯一酉膨胀（unitarily dilates）为动力系统的等变C*-对应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将KSGNS构造重新解释为固定C*-代数上正C*-对应范畴的自函子，并引入交织子（intertwiner）来处理固定C*-代数的自同构（automorphism），将膨胀过程纳入函子化视角。

Result: 证明了每个严格正等变C*-对应在KSGNS构造下可以被唯一地酉膨胀为动力系统的等变C*-对应。

Conclusion: 该工作为KSGNS构造提供了范畴论基础，并揭示了正等变对应与等变对应之间通过膨胀的结构关系。

Abstract: We prove that the KSGNS construction can be viewed as an endofunctor on a category whose objects are positive $C^*$-correspondences from a fixed $C^*$-algebra and morphisms are given by intertwiners which account for automorphisms of the fixed $C^*$-algebra. Using this perspective, we provide a functorial perspective for strict positive equivariant $C^*$-correspondences of $C^*$-dynamical systems and show every strict positive equivariant $C^*$-correspondence of $C^*$-dynamical systems unitarily uniquely dilates under the KSGNS construction to an equivariant $C^*$-correspondence of the dynamical systems.

### [19] [Diffusive transport from spatially correlated random phase kicks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06701)
*Pei Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维晶格上单粒子波包在有限空间关联长度的周期性随机相位敲击下的动力学，发现相位敲击会抑制弹道输运并诱导长期扩散，推导了扩散系数与关联长度的解析表达式，为周期性驱动晶格系统中的扩散提供了可定量检验的预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 驱动量子系统（driven quantum systems）中的退相干（dephasing）机制尚缺乏可控的理论模型，特别是空间关联相位噪声如何影响量子输运行为尚未被清晰揭示。

Method: 采用动量空间表述（momentum-space formulation）分析一维晶格上受周期性随机相位敲击（stroboscopic random phase kicks）的单粒子波包演化，推导累积相位的结构对波包扩散的控制作用，并得到扩散系数（diffusion coefficient）关于关联长度（correlation length）的解析表达式。

Result: 相位敲击强烈抑制弹道输运（ballistic transport），并在长时间尺度下诱导扩散行为；推导出的扩散系数解析表达式与数值模拟结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 空间关联的相位噪声通过一种简单机制控制量子输运，为周期性驱动晶格系统中的扩散提供了可定量检验的理论预测，并讨论了在冷原子（cold-atom）平台上的实验实现可能性。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of a single-particle wave packet on a one-dimensional lattice subject to periodic random phase kicks with finite spatial correlation length. This stroboscopic setting provides a controllable model of dephasing in driven quantum systems. Using a momentum-space formulation, we show that the evolution is governed by an accumulated phase whose structure determines the spreading of the wave packet. We find that the phase kicks strongly suppress ballistic transport and induce diffusion at long times. We derive an explicit analytical expression for the diffusion coefficient as a function of the correlation length, in excellent agreement with numerical simulations. Our results uncover a simple mechanism by which spatially correlated phase noise controls quantum transport, and provide a quantitatively testable prediction for diffusion in periodically driven lattice systems. Possible experimental realizations in cold-atom platforms are discussed.

### [20] [Majorana bound states in chiral ferromagnet-superconductor heterostructures revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06828)
*A. S. Slobodskoi,S. S. Apostoloff,I. S. Burmistrov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本论文针对超导薄膜中手性铁磁体与磁斯格明子（magnetic skyrmion）耦合超导涡旋（superconducting vortex）构成的异质结构，提出了马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）的低能准粒子束缚态（low-energy quasiparticle bound states）分析理论框架。在Bogoliubov-de Gennes方法下推导了马约拉纳波函数的解析表达式，明确揭示了自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）在稳定马约拉纳模式中的关键作用，并评估了矢量势和杂散磁场等现实效应的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 马约拉纳零模是实现容错拓扑量子计算（fault-tolerant topological quantum computation）的核心要素，传统上在一维混合纳米线中寻找，而基于超导体与非共线磁体（noncollinear magnets）异质结构的鲁棒替代方案正受到关注。斯格明子-涡旋对（skyrmion-vortex pairs）已在实验中实现，理论上被认为可容纳局域化的马约拉纳态（localized Majorana states），为编织操作（braiding operations）提供潜在路径。

Method: 基于Bogoliubov-de Gennes方法，对异质结构中的低能准粒子束缚态进行全面的理论分析。在先前研究基础上，发展了马约拉纳波函数以及其他低能态波函数与能谱的解析框架，并推导了有/无斯格明子伴随下局域于涡旋的低能态的近似解析表达式。通过数值模拟验证了解析结果的准确性，并进一步分析了矢量势（vector potentials）和杂散磁场（stray magnetic fields）引起的纹理扰动（texture perturbations）等现实效应。

Result: 解析结果明确展示了自旋-轨道耦合对稳定马约拉纳模式（Majorana modes）的关键作用；推导的解析表达式与数值模拟结果具有良好的一致性；量化了矢量势和杂散磁场纹理扰动等现实因素对系统的影响。

Conclusion: 该解析框架为理解斯格明子-涡旋对异质结构中的马约拉纳零模提供了系统理论工具，确认了自旋-轨道耦合在稳定马约拉纳态中的核心作用，并评估了实际实验条件下若干现实效应对系统行为的影响。

Abstract: Majorana zero modes are central to the pursuit of fault-tolerant topological quantum computation. While traditionally sought in one-dimensional hybrid nanowires, a robust alternative platform involves heterostructures combining superconductors with noncollinear magnets. This work focuses on a particularly promising system: a chiral ferromagnet hosting a magnetic skyrmion coupled to a superconducting film containing a superconducting vortex. Such skyrmion-vortex pairs have recently been realized experimentally and are theorized to harbor localized Majorana states, offering a potential pathway for braiding operations. We present a comprehensive theoretical analysis of the low-energy quasiparticle bound states in these heterostructures. Extending previous studies, we develop an analytical framework for the Majorana wavefunctions as well as the wavefunctions and spectrum of other lowlying states within a Bogoliubov-de Gennes approach. Our analytical results explicitly demonstrate the critical role of spin-orbit coupling for the stabilization of Majorana modes and provides approximate analytical expressions for low-lying states localized at the vortex, both with and without an accompanying skyrmion. The derived analytical results show excellent agreement with numerical simulations. We further elucidate the role of realistic effects, including vector potentials and texture perturbations from stray magnetic fields, to assess their impact.

### [21] [Nonadiabatic Theory of Phonon Magnetic Moments in Insulators and Metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06983)
*Haoran Chen,Wenqin Chen,Kaijie Yang,Ting Cao,Di Xiao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个适用于绝缘体和金属的非绝热声子磁矩理论，通过力-速度响应与规范协变Wigner展开推导出规范不变的表达式，揭示了费米海与费米面的贡献，并在Pb1-xSnxTe中验证了费米面贡献对声子磁矩的显著增强效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的声子磁矩理论主要局限于绝热近似（adiabatic approximation），无法完整描述金属体系中费米面附近电子态对声子磁矩的影响，且缺乏适用于绝缘体和金属的统一框架。

Method: 将声子磁矩关联至离子在磁场中的力-速度响应（force-velocity response），并利用规范协变Wigner展开（gauge-covariant Wigner expansion）推导出规范不变（gauge-invariant）的表达式，该形式自然分离了费米海（Fermi-sea）与费米面（Fermi-surface）贡献，完整保留了对声子频率的全部依赖关系。

Result: 在带隙系统中，新理论在低频极限下回归至已有的绝热表达式；超出该极限时，揭示了来自共振带间过程（resonant interband processes）和费米面的额外贡献。在Pb1-xSnxTe中的应用表明，费米面贡献显著增强了声子磁矩，其量级与实验观测一致。

Conclusion: 该理论为描述绝热极限之外的声子磁矩提供了统一框架，可同时适用于绝缘体和金属体系。

Abstract: We develop a nonadiabatic theory of phonon magnetic moments applicable to both insulators and metals. By relating the phonon magnetic moment to the force-velocity response of ions in a magnetic field, we derive a gauge-invariant expression using a gauge-covariant Wigner expansion. The formalism naturally separates Fermi-sea and Fermi-surface contributions and captures the full dependence on phonon frequency. In gapped systems, our theory reduces to previous adiabatic expressions in the low-frequency limit. Beyond this limit, it reveals additional contributions arising from resonant interband processes and the Fermi surface. Applying our theory to Pb$_{1-x}$Sn$_x$Te, we find that the Fermi-surface contribution substantially enhances the phonon magnetic moment, reproducing the same order of magnitude as the experimental observation. Our results provide a unified framework for describing phonon magnetic moments beyond the adiabatic regime.

### [22] [Coherent Nonreciprocal Valley Transport in Dirac/Weyl Semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07189)
*Can Yesilyurt*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发现，在狄拉克（Dirac）或外尔（Weyl）通道中，仅凭单个形状缺乏反演对称性的静电势垒即可驱动相干非互易输运，无需磁性、超导等传统内置对称性破缺要素。该机制源于几何效应：通过两个不同折射界面（垂直与倾斜）的势垒时，正反向传播的波包经历不同的费米面失配顺序。数值模拟显示，反演不对称的三角形势垒可产生强电荷模式整流，而添加狄拉克锥倾斜则将其转化为谷分辨二极管。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统非互易电子输运（nonreciprocal electronic transport）通常依赖于材料的本征反演对称性破缺或外加场（如磁序、磁手性耦合、极性晶格畸变或超导态）。本文旨在探索是否可以在不依赖这些传统要素的情况下，仅通过几何结构设计实现相干非互易输运。

Method: 采用相干分裂算符狄拉克波包模拟（split-operator Dirac wave-packet simulations），并结合实际器件参数，在具有各向同性（无倾斜）能量色散的通道中研究反演不对称的直角三角形势垒，以及引入狄拉克锥倾斜（Dirac-cone tilt）后的情形。

Result: 反演不对称的直角三角形势垒在两个不同折射界面（一个垂直、一个倾斜）作用下产生强电荷模式整流，证实其纯几何起源。添加狄拉克锥倾斜后，同一形状转变为相干谷分辨二极管（valley-resolved diode），其二向色结构在狄拉克点处翻转符号。而镜像对称的等腰三角形虽有两个倾斜面，但保持严格互易，仅呈现谷极化透射。

Conclusion: 机制的本质是几何效应：正反向波包在势垒入口和出口面经历不同的费米面失配（Fermi-surface-mismatch）序列。倾斜界面与锥倾斜本身并不充分，关键在于具有几何上不同界面类型的序列组合。

Abstract: Nonreciprocal electronic transport, defined as a directional asymmetry between the forward and backward two-terminal responses, typically requires a built-in inversion-breaking feature of the host material or an applied field, such as magnetic order, magnetochiral coupling, polar lattice distortion, or a superconducting state. Here, we show that a single electrostatic barrier whose shape lacks inversion symmetry can drive coherent nonreciprocal transport in a Dirac or Weyl channel without any of these ingredients. The mechanism is geometric: across a barrier with two qualitatively distinct refraction interfaces (one vertical and one oblique), forward- and backward-propagating wave packets experience different Fermi-surface-mismatch sequences at the entrance and exit faces. Using coherent split-operator Dirac wave-packet simulations with realistic device parameters, we show that in a channel with isotropic (untilted) energy dispersion, an inversion-asymmetric (right-angle) triangular barrier produces strong charge-mode rectification, establishing its purely geometric origin. Adding a Dirac-cone tilt turns the same shape into a coherent valley-resolved diode whose dichroic structure flips sign across the Dirac point. Strikingly, a mirror-symmetric (isosceles) triangle with two oblique faces exhibits valley-polarized transmission while remaining exactly reciprocal. Oblique interfaces and tilt together do not suffice; the essential ingredient is a sequence of geometrically distinct interface types.

</details>


### [23] [Floquet second-order topological insulator in strained graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07190)
*Yu-Wen Xu,Xiaolin Wan,Zi-Ming Wang,Rui Wang,Dong-Hui Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本论文展示了一种通过单轴应变（uniaxial strain）和可调入射角的非共振圆偏振光在石墨烯中实现Floquet高阶拓扑相（Floquet higher-order topological phase）的可控路径，证明了应变压制石墨烯可作为实现Floquet二阶拓扑绝缘体（second-order topological insulator）的现实可调谐平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯为Floquet能带工程（Floquet band engineering）提供了典型体系，但现有研究主要关注圆偏振光在Dirac点处动态打开拓扑带隙并产生非平衡霍尔响应。作者希望探索在应变和斜入射圆偏振光的联合作用下，能否在石墨烯中实现更丰富的高阶拓扑相（higher-order topology）。

Method: 采用带有Peierls耦合（Peierls coupling）的应变化蜂巢紧束缚模型（strained honeycomb tight-binding model），并结合高频展开（high-frequency expansion）得到有效Floquet哈密顿量（effective Floquet Hamiltonian）。通过陈数（Chern number）和晶体对称性量子化的极化不变量（crystalline-symmetry-quantized polarization invariant）刻画相图，并利用第一性原理（first-principles）信息构建紧束缚模型验证拓扑演化。

Result: 应变将Dirac锥驱动至Dirac合并（Dirac-merging, semi-Dirac）临界区域，使光诱导质量出现强各向异性。在斜入射条件下，投影驱动场等效为椭圆偏振光，与应变协同稳定了一种边缘有带隙但有限几何结构中存在稳健带隙角态（corner modes）的相，实现了Floquet二阶拓扑绝缘体。第一性原理支持的紧束缚计算证实了应变化石墨烯纳米结构中的拓扑演化。

Conclusion: 研究结果将受驱动的应变化石墨烯（driven strained graphene）确立为一种现实且可调谐的平台，用于实现和诊断Floquet高阶拓扑相（Floquet higher-order topological phases）。

Abstract: Graphene provides a canonical setting for Floquet band engineering, where circularly polarized light can dynamically open topological gaps at Dirac points and generate nonequilibrium Hall responses. Here we show that uniaxial strain and off-resonant circularly polarized light with tunable incidence angle enable a controllable route to Floquet higher-order topology in graphene. Using a strained honeycomb tight-binding model with Peierls coupling and a high-frequency expansion for the effective Floquet Hamiltonian, we find that strain drives the Dirac cones toward the Dirac-merging (semi-Dirac) critical regime, where the light-induced mass becomes strongly anisotropic. For oblique incidence, the projected drive is effectively elliptically polarized and, in combination with strain, stabilizes a phase with gapped edges but robust in-gap corner modes in finite geometries, realizing a Floquet second-order topological insulator. We characterize the phase diagram via the Chern number and a crystalline-symmetry-quantized polarization invariant. Finally, first-principles-informed tight-binding calculations corroborate the predicted topological evolution in strained graphene nanostructures. Our results identify driven strained graphene as a realistic and tunable platform for realizing and diagnosing Floquet higher-order topological phases.

</details>


### [24] [Hybrid-order topology in two-dimensional nonsymmorphic antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07206)
*Wei Xiong,Zi-Ming Wang,Xin-Mei Wei,Rui Wang,Dong-Hui Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证明，在二维非对称性（nonsymmorphic）反铁磁体中存在一种杂化阶拓扑（hybrid-order topology）：单一的体绝缘相可同时展现由终止面几何唯一决定的一阶（first-order）边缘态和二阶（second-order）角态，从而实现了受终止面控制的一阶与二阶拓扑之间的对偶性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在反铁磁体系中同时实现一阶与二阶拓扑边界态的可能性，并揭示体相与边界几何之间的耦合机制。

Method: 采用一个通用的反铁磁狄拉克模型（antiferromagnetic Dirac model），引入对称性允许的动量依赖自旋密度波（spin-density-wave, SDW）质量项；通过分析不同终止面几何（screw兼容边与45°菱形终止）下对称性的变化，研究拓扑边界态的涌现。

Result: 对于screw兼容边缘，非对称性螺旋对称性（screw symmetry）保护无能隙的一阶边缘态；对于45°菱形终止，边界破缺螺旋对称性，但磁镜对称性（magnetic mirror symmetries）\(\mathcal{M}_x\mathcal{T}\)和\(\mathcal{M}_y\mathcal{T}\)仍被有限几何保留，强制边缘质量交替排列，束缚出零维角态（zero-dimensional corner states）。该二阶相（second-order phase）由量子化的四极矩（quantized quadrupole moment）表征，角态因手征对称性（chiral symmetry）钉扎在零能。此外，显式晶格微扰可选择性地使一阶边缘模打开能隙而稳健地保留角态。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种基于对称性的路径，在磁性非对称性体系中实现了受终止面控制的一阶与二阶拓扑之间的对偶性。

Abstract: We theoretically demonstrate hybrid-order topology in a two-dimensional nonsymmorphic antiferromagnet. Utilizing a generic antiferromagnetic Dirac model with a symmetry-allowed, momentum-dependent spin-density-wave (SDW) mass, we show that a single bulk insulating phase exhibits distinct topological boundary manifestations governed solely by the termination geometry. For screw-compatible edges, nonsymmorphic screw symmetry protects gapless first-order edge states. In contrast, for a $45^\circ$ diamond-shaped termination, the screw symmetry is broken at the boundary, resulting in gapped edges. However, the finite geometry still preserves magnetic mirror symmetries $\mathcal{M}_x\mathcal{T}$ and $\mathcal{M}_y\mathcal{T}$, which enforce an alternating pattern of edge masses, thereby binding zero-dimensional corner states. This second-order phase is characterized by a quantized quadrupole moment, with corner states pinned to zero energy by the chiral symmetry. We further demonstrate that explicit lattice perturbations can selectively gap the first-order edge modes while robustly preserving the corner states. Our work establishes a symmetry-based route to a termination-controlled duality between first- and second-order topology in magnetic nonsymmorphic systems.

</details>


### [25] [Topological Characterization of Discrete-Time Classical Stochastic Processes: Dual Role of Point-Gap Topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07231)
*Masaya Nakagawa,Masahito Ueda*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文对由格点上的离散时间马尔可夫链（discrete-time Markov chain）描述的经典随机过程进行了拓扑表征，发现随机矩阵的点隙拓扑（point-gap topology）围绕不同参考点具有不同的物理意义：围绕一般参考点的拓扑与输运方向相关，而围绕复谱原点的非平凡拓扑则意味着由反馈控制等因素导致的非马尔可夫性（non-Markovianity）。基于此，研究者在麦克斯韦妖实验中识别出定向输运的拓扑起源，并发现反馈控制的拓扑本质；此外，他们还展示了拓扑强制的非马尔可夫经典随机过程可由马尔可夫量子主方程（Markovian quantum master equation）模拟，揭示了量子优势的一种拓扑形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典随机过程的拓扑性质尚未被系统刻画，尤其是在离散时间马尔可夫链的背景下，点隙拓扑的物理含义仍不明确。本文旨在建立随机矩阵的点隙拓扑与定向输运、非马尔可夫性之间的严格联系，并揭示其在麦克斯韦妖（Maxwell’s demon）实验及反馈控制中的拓扑起源。

Method: 采用点隙拓扑（point-gap topology）分析离散时间马尔可夫链的随机矩阵，依据参考点的不同将拓扑效应区分为两类：一般参考点对应输运方向；复谱原点对应非马尔可夫性。进一步将这一拓扑框架应用于S. Toyabe等人的经典麦克斯韦妖实验，并构建马尔可夫量子主方程模拟拓扑强制的非马尔可夫过程。

Result: 识别出麦克斯韦妖实验中定向输运的拓扑起源，发现反馈控制具有超越热力学解释的拓扑本质（topological nature）。证明了拓扑强制的非马尔可夫经典随机过程可由马尔可夫量子主方程实现，从而展示了一种拓扑形式的量子优势（topological form of quantum advantage）。

Conclusion: 点隙拓扑为经典随机过程的定向输运与非马尔可夫性提供了统一的拓扑框架；量子系统在模拟拓扑强制的非马尔可夫经典过程方面具有天然优势，这构成了量子优势的一种新形态。

Abstract: We present topological characterization of classical stochastic processes described by discrete-time Markov chains on lattices. We point out that point-gap topology of stochastic matrices entails two distinct physical consequences that hinge on the choice of the reference point. The point-gap topology around a generic reference point is related to the direction of transport, and nontrivial topology around the origin of the complex spectrum of a stochastic matrix implies non-Markovianity caused by, e.g., feedback control. On the basis of this characterization, we identify the topological origin of directed transport in a classic experiment of Maxwell's demon [S. Toyabe et al., Nat. Phys. 6, 988 (2010)] and find the topological nature of feedback control beyond thermodynamic interpretation. We demonstrate that a topologically enforced non-Markovian classical stochastic process can be simulated by a Markovian quantum master equation, indicating a topological form of quantum advantage.

</details>


### [26] [Effective Gilbert damping in the stochastic Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07416)
*Mexx. E. Y. Regout,Bertrand Dupé,Matthieu J. Verstraete*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过一维自旋链（1D spin chain）的原子自旋动力学（atomistic spin dynamics）模拟，研究了温度和自旋波相互作用对有效阻尼（effective damping）的影响，发现有效阻尼随温度和晶格动量（crystal momentum）的变化与初始常数吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）存在显著差异，并从与吉尔伯特热浴的相互作用和局域磁序变化导致的自旋波散射等机制进行了解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准粒子方法（如玻尔兹曼方程）研究自旋波输运时，通常假设散射率遵循η=αω的简单形式，其中α为吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）。该工作旨在检验当引入温度和自旋波相互作用时，原子自旋动力学中观测到的有效阻尼α_eff,T=η/ω是否仍符合这一简单形式。

Method: 利用随机朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特方程（stochastic Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation）传播自旋轨迹，从中提取动态关联函数（dynamical correlation functions），并通过拟合动态结构因子（dynamical structure factor）获得宽温度范围内的色散关系（dispersion）和散射率（scattering rates）。

Result: 得到的有效阻尼与初始设定的常数吉尔伯特阻尼值差异很大；有效阻尼表现出对温度和晶格动量的依赖性。

Conclusion: 有效阻尼的温度和晶格动量标度关系可通过与吉尔伯特热浴（Gilbert bath）的相互作用以及局域磁序变化引起的自旋波散射来解释。

Abstract: Quasi particle based (e.g. Boltzmann equation) studies of spin wave transport often assume that their scattering rates follow the simple form $η=αω$, with the Gilbert damping $α$ and frequency $ω$. In this work, we examine the effective damping $α_{eff,T}=η/ω$ observed in atomistic spin dynamics, when temperature and spin wave interactions are introduced for a 1D spin chain. We extract the dynamical correlation functions from spin trajectories propagated using the stochastic Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation, and fit the dynamical structure factor, yielding the dispersion and scattering rates for a wide range of temperatures. The resulting effective damping can be very different from the initially constant Gilbert value. It exhibits a temperature and crystal momentum scaling which we explain based on interactions with the Gilbert bath and spin wave scattering by changes in local magnetic order.

### [27] [Point-gap topology of damped magnon excitations in skyrmion strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07435)
*Yusuke Koyama,Yuki Kawaguchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过结合自旋波理论与微扰论，理论研究了吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）导致有限寿命磁振子的非厄米拓扑（non-Hermitian topology）。研究解析计算了点能隙的谱绕数（spectral winding number），发现非厄米趋肤效应（NHSE）可存在于无非局域阻尼的情形下，并通过磁振子传播动力学验证了绕数的非平庸性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究具有有限寿命的磁振子（magnons）在吉尔伯特阻尼影响下的非厄米拓扑性质，特别是非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect, NHSE）的存在条件及其与阻尼形式的关系。

Method: 结合自旋波理论（spin-wave theory）与针对包含非局域阻尼项的朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特方程（Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation）的微扰论，解析计算了点能隙（point gaps）的谱绕数（spectral winding number）；并以稳态为斯格明子弦晶格（skyrmion-string lattice）的模型进行数值验证。

Result: 非厄米趋肤效应可在没有非局域阻尼的情况下出现。当存在沿单一方向的非局域阻尼时，具有唯一极小值（unique minimum）的能带的绕数由该极小值处的波数符号决定。磁脉冲激发的自旋波传播方向在不同能带间发生剧烈变化，其行为与局域/非局域阻尼的存在性及非平庸绕数一致。

Conclusion: 吉尔伯特阻尼诱导的有限寿命磁振子可承载非厄米拓扑，其谱绕数与非厄米趋肤效应依赖于局域与非局域阻尼的配置；自旋波传播动力学实验可用于探测此类拓扑特征。

Abstract: We theoretically study the non-Hermitian topology of magnons with finite lifetimes due to Gilbert damping. By incorporating the spin-wave theory and perturbation theory for the Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation including nonlocal damping terms, we analytically evaluate the spectral winding number for point gaps, which indicates the existence of the non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE). We find that the NHSE can occur even in the absence of nonlocal damping. In the presence of nonlocal damping along one direction, we show that the winding number for an energy band with a unique minimum is determined from the sign of the wave number at the band minimum. We demonstrate these results using a model that hosts a skyrmion-string lattice as a steady state. We further investigate spin-wave propagation dynamics excited by a magnetic-field pulse and show that the propagation direction changes drastically from band to band depending on the presence of local and nonlocal damping, consistent with the nontrivial winding numbers.

### [28] [Exciton-mediated optical control of liquid-solid friction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07539)
*Timur Pryadilin,Alexey Kavokin,Baptiste Coquinot*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于激子（exciton）的微观理论，解释了纳米流体（nanofluidic）系统中固体-液体摩擦的激子中介机制。该理论区分静态与动态激子，推导了可调谐的摩擦解析公式，并在无拟合参数的情况下定量复现了碳纳米管中光致扩散降低的实验观测，从而将激子确立为光学调控纳米流体输运的新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米流体系统中的界面摩擦可源于液体电荷涨落与固体内部激发之间的涨落诱导耦合。已有实验观察到光照可影响纳米通道内的液体输运，但缺乏相应的微观理论解释。本文旨在建立激子中介的固-液摩擦微观理论，以解释和预测光控纳米流体输运现象。

Method: 基于激子与水的电荷涨落之间的耦合，分别针对由无序或官能团局域化的静态激子（static exciton）以及通过极化涨落（polarization fluctuation）与水相互作用的动态激子（dynamic exciton），推导了各自的激子摩擦（excitonic friction）解析公式。

Result: 所推导的激子摩擦在实验上可调谐，能显著减小滑移长度（slip length），从而降低纳米通道的水力渗透性（hydraulic permeability）。将框架应用于碳纳米管，无需拟合参数即定量复现了Kistwal等人最新测量中光照条件下纳米管扩散减小的结果。

Conclusion: 激子是一种能够实现光学调控纳米流体输运的机制；激子光致发光（excitonic photoluminescence）有望作为纳米通道内流速的光学探针。

Abstract: Interfacial friction in nanofluidic systems can arise from fluctuation-induced coupling between liquid charge fluctuations and the internal excitations of the confining solid. Here, we develop a microscopic theory of exciton-mediated solid-liquid friction based on the coupling between optically generated excitons and charge fluctuations in water. We distinguish between static excitons, localized by disorder or functionalization, and dynamic excitons, which interact with water through polarization fluctuations. In both cases, we derive analytical formulas for the excitonic friction, which is experimentally tunable and can significantly reduce the slip length and thereby the hydraulic permeability of nanochannels. Applying our framework to carbon nanotubes, we quantitatively reproduce the recent measurements of Kistwal et al., showing a reduction of nanotube diffusion under optical excitation, without fitting parameters. More broadly, our results establish excitons as a mechanism to optically control nanofluidic transport and suggest that excitonic photoluminescence could provide an optical probe of flow velocity inside nanochannels.

Method: 设计、制备了铁磁（FM）和合成反铁磁（SAF）多层膜，并将其与SAF偏置系统（SAF bias system）集成；结合定量高灵敏度磁力显微镜（MFM）和微磁模拟（micromagnetic modeling）进行表征。

Abstract: Synthetic antiferromagnetic skyrmions (SAFsk) are nanoscale, topologically protected spin textures with strong potential for spintronic technologies because of their high stability and the absence of the skyrmion Hall effect. However, robust zero field stabilization remains a central challenge. Here, a synthetic antiferromagnetic (SAF) bias system is introduced as a novel strategy to stabilize both ferromagnetic skyrmions (FMsk) and SAFsk at zero field. Ferromagnetic (FM) and SAF multilayers are designed, fabricated and integrated with the SAF bias system to enable controlled skyrmion stabilization and polarity setting via multilayer design and a preparatory field cycle. Combining quantitative and high-sensitivity magnetic force microscopy (MFM) with micromagnetic modeling, reliable zero field skyrmion formation is demonstrated and sub 20nm SAFsk are directly observed, the smallest SAFsk reported to date. Moreover, the SAF bias system concept introduced here offers a robust and scalable route to bias future skyrmion multilayers, as its compensated nature suppresses domain formation and preserves a uniform exchange field.

### [30] [Finite-q photon-drag shift current in two-dimensional massive chiral Dirac fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07856)
*Rofii,Eddwi Hasdeo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过直接计算有限动量传递 q 下的非垂直响应，发现各向同性二维有质量手性狄拉克模型中，手性指标 J 会定性重构光拖拽位移电流（photon-drag shift current）的符号拓扑结构：J=1 时光电流保持正值，J≥2 时则在运动学允许区域内出现零电流等高线和符号反转；同时光电流受对称性约束完全为横向（transverse），且在中心对称系统中严格垂直跃迁极限 q=0 下消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有位移电流研究多局限于微扰小 q 近似下的垂直跃迁（vertical transition）框架，忽略了有限动量传递 q 对非垂直响应（non-vertical response）的贡献；本文旨在通过直接计算全有限 q 响应，揭示手性（chirality）对光拖拽位移电流符号拓扑的定量影响。

Method: 采用各向同性的二维有质量手性狄拉克模型（massive chiral Dirac model），手性指标 J=1,2,3；直接评估全有限 q 非垂直响应，而非微扰小 q 近似；结合对称性分析与运动学截断（kinematic cutoff）和泡利阻塞（Pauli blocking）效应。

Result: (1) 手性定性重构有限 q 光电流 j(q) 的符号拓扑：J=1 时光电流整体为正，J≥2 则在运动学允许区域内出现内部零电流等高线（zero-current contours）和符号反转；(2) 光电流受对称性约束严格横向，j(q) ∝ ẑ×q；(3) 在中心对称系统中，严格垂直跃迁极限 q=0 下光电流消失；(4) Pauli 阻塞通过选择共振等高线（resonance contour）的活动部分来塑造响应，大 Δ 或大 q 下响应因运动学截断而消失。

Conclusion: 各向同性有质量手性狄拉克问题可作为研究手性依赖的有限 q 位移电流的对称性控制的基准模型（symmetry-controlled benchmark）。

Abstract: We investigate the photon-drag shift current in an isotropic single-valley two-dimensional massive chiral Dirac model with chirality index $J=1,2,3$ by directly evaluating the full finite-$q$ non-vertical response beyond the perturbative small-$q$ regime. Our central result is that chirality qualitatively reorganizes the sign topology of the finite-$q$ photocurrent $\mathbf{ j}(\mathbf{ q})$. For $J=1$, the photocurrent remains broadly positive, whereas higher-chirality sectors ($J \ge 2$) generically develop internal zero-current contours and sign reversals within the kinematically allowed region. We further show that the photocurrent is symmetry-constrained to be purely transverse, $\mathbf{j}(\mathbf{q}) \propto \hat{\mathbf{z}}\times\mathbf{q}$, and vanishes in the strictly vertical-transition limit $q=0$ in centrosymmetric systems. Pauli blocking further shapes the response by selecting the active portion of the resonance contour, while its extinction at large $Δ$ or $q$ follows from a simple kinematic cutoff. These results establish the isotropic massive chiral Dirac problem as a symmetry-controlled benchmark for chirality-dependent finite-$q$ shift currents.

### [31] [Energy-Resolved Quantum Geometry from Středa Response: Driven-Dissipative Bosonic Lattices and Disordered Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07948)
*Anaïs Defossez,Baptiste Bermond,Lucila Peralta Gavensky,Nathan Goldman*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出在驱动-耗散玻色子晶格中，利用均匀泵浦和随机相位激励，可同时实现积分型和能量分辨型Středa响应的直接测量，从而将Středa公式从朗道能级的拓扑响应推广至一般色散能带，并应用于强无序下拓扑安德森绝缘体中量子几何结构的表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Středa公式将绝缘体的霍尔电导（Hall conductivity）与其粒子密度对磁场的响应联系起来，提供了拓扑陈数（Chern number）的局域普适探针。然而，除积分型响应外，能量分辨的Středa标记（energy-resolved Středa marker）虽能从态密度的磁响应中揭示布洛赫带（Bloch bands）的量子几何（quantum geometry）细节，但其在实验上的可获取性尚未解决。因此，需要寻找能够直接测量这两种Středa响应的物理平台。

Method: 利用驱动-耗散玻色子晶格（driven-dissipative bosonic lattices），通过在晶格上施加具有均匀强度和随机相位的受控泵浦（controlled pumping with uniform strength and random phases），并引入均匀损耗（uniform loss），从而对特征模占据数施加洛伦兹滤波（Lorentzian filter），使得系统在稳态下能够直接得到积分型和能量分辨型的Středa响应。

Result: 对于一般的色散能带（dispersive bands），该方案能够重建粗粒化的能量分辨Středa响应，从而将驱动-耗散玻色子晶格确立为反常谱流（anomalous spectral flow）和能量分辨量子几何的多功能探针。进一步，将该标记应用于强无序下的拓扑带，成功捕捉了拓扑安德森绝缘体（topological Anderson insulators）中潜在的量子几何结构。

Conclusion: 驱动-耗散玻色子晶格是实现Středa响应的通用实验平台，不仅可重现其拓扑量子化的积分响应，还能通过能量分辨标记解析能带中量子几何的精细结构。该方法在强无序体系中仍能有效运作，为研究拓扑安德森绝缘体等无序拓扑相提供了新的探测手段。

Abstract: The Středa formula links the Hall conductivity of an insulator to the magnetic-field response of its particle density, providing a local and universal probe of the topological Chern number. Beyond this quantized response, an energy-resolved Středa marker can be defined from the magnetic response of the density of states, revealing detailed features of the quantum geometry of Bloch bands. We show that driven-dissipative bosonic lattices provide direct access to both the integrated and energy-resolved Středa responses. Our scheme uses controlled pumping with uniform strength and random phases across the lattice, together with uniform loss, to yield a Lorentzian filter of eigenmode occupations. For generic dispersive bands, this enables reconstruction of a coarse-grained energy-resolved Středa response, establishing these platforms as versatile probes of anomalous spectral flow and energy-resolved quantum geometry. As a striking application, we show that this marker elucidates the fate of topological bands under strong disorder, capturing the quantum-geometric structure underlying topological Anderson insulators.

</details>

### [32] [Quantum spin liquid on a 3D bipartite lattice of spin trimers stabilized by enhanced effective anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06752)
*M. Gomilšek,L. Mangin-Thro,T. Arh,S. Petit,B. Grenier,V. Simonet,M. Pregelj,A. Zorko,B. Koteswararao,B. -G. Jeon,B. Sana,Y. Furukawa,Y. Inagaki,T. Asano,C. Repellin,B. Fåk,J. Ollivier,F. Fauth,C. V. Colin,E. Pachoud,V. Pomjakushin,J. S. Lord,H. Luetkens,K. -H. Kim,P. Khuntia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究在三维双分子格点（bipartite lattice）材料KBa$_3$Ca$_4$Cu$_3$V$_7$O$_{28}$中，通过实验与理论结合的手段，发现了一种由弱微观各向异性经三聚体（trimer）放大效应稳定存在的无隙量子自旋液体（gapless quantum spin liquid）态，从而为在双分子体系中实现各向异性稳定的量子纠缠态提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然理论预测键各向异性（bond anisotropy）可在双分子晶格上稳定量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid, QSL），但迄今尚无材料被确证在真实基态中实现这一状态，因此亟需寻找实际材料平台。

Method: 通过块体热力学测量、中子散射（neutron scattering）、μSR（muon spin rotation）和核磁共振（NMR）等实验手段，结合蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）和精确对角化（exact diagonalization）计算，对三维自旋三聚体磁体KBa$_3$Ca$_4$Cu$_3$V$_7$O$_{28}$进行系统的结构和磁性表征。

Result: 实验未检测到自旋冻结或对称性破缺相变直至20 mK，观察到具有代数自旋关联（algebraic spin autocorrelations）的无隙动力学基态。理论计算表明，弱微观Cu-Cu交换各向异性（约15%）在三聚体层级被放大为60–100%的有效赝自旋间相互作用各向异性（anisotropy），从而稳定该量子自旋液体态。

Conclusion: 三聚体网络是构建各向异性稳定量子纠缠态（anisotropy-stabilized quantum entangled states）的有效平台，即便在仅具有弱微观各向异性的三维双分子体系中亦可实现。

Abstract: Quantum spin liquids (QSLs) represent highly entangled states of matter in which frustration-induced quantum fluctuations suppress any symmetry-breaking phase transition down to absolute zero, giving rise to fractionalized excitations and emergent gauge fields. Theoretically, bond anisotropy can stabilize QSLs even on bipartite lattices, as exemplified by the Kitaev honeycomb model; however, no material has so far been established to realize such a state as its true ground state. Here we identify the three-dimensional spin-trimer magnet KBa$_3$Ca$_4$Cu$_3$V$_7$O$_{28}$ as a promising candidate for a bipartite quantum spin liquid persisting to the lowest temperatures. Strongly coupled Cu$^{2+}$ trimers form effective pseudospin-1/2 degrees of freedom upon cooling, which in turn constitute a three-dimensional bipartite network. Bulk thermodynamic measurements, neutron scattering, $μ$SR, and NMR detect no spin freezing or symmetry-breaking phase transition down to 20 mK, but instead reveal a gapless dynamical ground state with algebraic spin autocorrelations. Complementary Monte Carlo and exact-diagonalization calculations show that this state is stabilized by a strong enhancement of effective anisotropy: a weak microscopic Cu-Cu exchange anisotropy of approximately 15 percent is generically amplified at the trimer level, producing effective pseudospin-pseudospin interaction anisotropies of 60 to 100 percent. Our results establish trimer-based networks as a promising platform for realizing anisotropy-stabilized quantum entangled states, even in three-dimensional bipartite systems with only weak microscopic anisotropy.

</details>


### [33] [Does a Fractional Quantum Hall Edge Have a Protected Intrinsic Dipole Moment?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06801)
*Domagoj Perković,Konstantinos Vasiliou,S. A. Parameswaran,Steven H. Simon*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）数值方法，检验了Park和Haldane关于分数量子霍尔（FQH）边缘电偶极矩具有内禀保护值的论断，发现该内禀值仅在ν=1/3边缘成立，而在ν=2/3边缘以及Pfaffian/反Pfaffian界面中并不存在，并通过复合费米子（composite fermion）图像解释了层级态（hierarchy states）缺乏内禀保护的物理原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证Park和Haldane [Phys. Rev. B 90, 045123 (2014)]提出的分数量子霍尔系统物理边缘处电偶极矩具有内禀保护值的论断是否普遍成立，并澄清此前数值研究中存在的局限性。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法精确计算基态偶极矩，针对三个代表性系统（ν=1/3-真空边缘、ν=2/3-真空边缘以及Pfaffian与反Pfaffian相之间的界面）进行数值研究，同时基于复合费米子（composite fermion）理论给出解析论证。

Result: 内禀偶极矩的预期值仅在ν=1/3边缘出现；ν=2/3边缘以及Pfaffian/反Pfaffian界面均未表现出所声称的内禀值。

Conclusion: 层级态（hierarchy states）通常不具有内禀保护偶极矩，这一发现对分数量子霍尔态的边缘结构及能量学具有重要启示。

Abstract: We investigate the claims by Park and Haldane [Phys. Rev. B 90, 045123 (2014)] of an intrinsic protected value of the electric dipole moment at the physical edge of fractional quantum Hall (FQH) systems. Contrary to prevailing expectations, we find that the edge dipole takes the expected intrinsic value only in certain very special cases. We identify key limitations in earlier numerical studies and employ density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) methods to accurately compute the ground-state dipole. We focus on three representative systems: the $ν=1/3$-vacuum edge, the $ν=2/3$-vacuum edge, and the interface between Pfaffian and anti-Pfaffian phases. We find that the expected intrinsic dipole value occurs only at $ν=1/3$, whereas the other systems do not exhibit the claimed intrinsic value. We give arguments based on composite fermions as to why hierarchy states should generally not have protected intrinsic dipoles. These results have important implications for the energetics and edge structure of FQH states.

</details>


### [34] [Fluctuation-driven chiral ferromagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06852)
*Rokas Veitas,Ahmed Khalifa,Francisco Machado,Shubhayu Chatterjee*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明，在铁磁材料中，磁化不守恒耦合（magnetization-non-conserving couplings）可以改变量子涨落被抑制的常规图景，从而稳定一个具有轨道手性（orbital chirality）的手性铁磁态（chiral ferromagnet）。通过超越经典相图分析，作者发现了由量子涨落稳定化的手性条纹相（chiral stripe regime）等新相，并阐明了这些相的热霍尔效应（thermal Hall effect）等输运特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁磁材料通常具有简单无阻挫（unfrustrated）的基态，导致量子涨落被抑制，从而极大限制了可观测现象的多样性。作者旨在突破这一限制，探索如何通过磁化不守恒耦合引入手性序，从而扩展铁磁体的物理现象范围。

Method: 作者展示了自旋-轨道相互作用（spin-orbit interactions）如何修正经典相图；经典分析仅预言共线态（collinear states），而通过考虑量子涨落，作者观测到了涨落稳定的新相，包括具有大轨道手性的铁磁相和手性条纹相。该机制自发产生标量轨道手性（scalar orbital chirality），区别于传统依赖场致矢量子（vector chiral order）倾斜的机制。

Result: 磁化不守恒耦合在手性铁磁体中稳定了量子涨落主导的新相，不同于经典分析给出的共线态。这些手性态表现出增强的热霍尔效应等独特的输运特征，并且与莫尔异质结构（moiré heterostructures）、里德伯原子阵列（Rydberg-atom arrays）以及含非克拉默自旋（non-Kramers spins）的固态材料直接相关。

Conclusion: 手性铁磁体可以通过量子涨落而非经典机制实现稳定，该发现不仅拓展了对铁磁材料中量子现象的理解，也对相关低维和固态系统具有实际指导意义。

Abstract: In general, quantum fluctuations are suppressed in ferromagnetic materials because they admit a simple unfrustrated ground state, greatly limiting the scope of phenomena that can be observed in these materials. In this work, we show how magnetization-non-conserving couplings fundamentally alter this paradigm by demonstrating the existence of a chiral ferromagnet that is stabilized by quantum fluctuations. More specifically, we show how these spin-orbit interactions modify the classical phase diagram; whereas a classical analysis predicts only collinear states, we observe fluctuation-stabilized phases, including a ferromagnet with large orbital chirality and a chiral stripe regime. We elucidate how such couplings spontaneously generate a scalar orbital chirality, in contrast to conventional mechanisms which rely upon a field-induced canting of vector chiral order. The resultant chiral states exhibit distinct transport signatures, namely an enhanced thermal Hall effect, and are of direct relevance to moiré heterostructures, Rydberg-atom arrays, and solid-state materials featuring non-Kramers spins.

</details>

*T. Vibert,D. Sénéchal*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索扭曲铜氧化物双层体系中非平庸拓扑（nontrivial topology）的出现条件，揭示掺杂水平（doping level）对拓扑特性的调控作用。

Method: 基于弱相互作用（weak-interaction regime）下的Hubbard模型，计算陈数（Chern number）以表征拓扑特性；在有限宽度几何（finite-width geometry）中分析关联边缘态（edge states）及其手征性（chirality），同时保持全关联（full correlations）。

Result: 在U/t=3.85条件下，电子掺杂（electron-doped）时陈数为±8，而空穴掺杂（hole-doped）时陈数为0。

Conclusion: 扭曲铜氧化物双层体系的拓扑特性敏感依赖于掺杂水平，电子掺杂可诱导非平庸拓扑，而空穴掺杂则不能；边缘态分析进一步支持了非平庸拓扑的存在。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of nontrivial topology in a twisted cuprate bilayer described by the Hubbard model in the weak-interaction regime. Our results show that the topological character depends sensitively on the doping level. For $U/t=3.85$, the Chern number assumes a value of $\pm 8$ in the electron-doped case, whereas it vanishes (0) in the hole-doped regime. The presence of nontrivial topology is further supported by an analysis the associated edge states and their chirality in a finite-width geometry, while keeping full correlations.

### [36] [Anomalous Phase-Coherence Scaling in a Quantum-Critical Dirac Semimetal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07085)
*Sana Nakamichi,Ryotaro Kobara,Yoshinari Unozawa,Yoshitaka Kawasugi,Sakura Hiramoto,Koki Funatsu,Toshio Naito,Masafumi Tamura,Reizo Kato,Yutaka Nishio,Naoya Tajima*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过加压调控狄拉克半金属α-(BEDT-TTF)₂I₃，测量其弱反局域化（weak antilocalization, WAL）行为，提取了相相干长度（phase coherence length）L_φ及其温度标度指数（temperature exponent）p。高压区呈现典型的二维退相干行为（p≈1/2），而接近临界压力P_c≈1.2 GPa时，温度指数被抑制至p≈0.3，表明量子临界点附近狄拉克电子的非弹性散射机制异常。WAL在相变过程中持续存在，支持无能隙或近无能隙的量子相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索关联驱动的量子相变（quantum phase transition）中，狄拉克半金属的量子相干输运性质如何演化，特别是弱反局域化（WAL）行为及相相干长度（L_φ）的温度标度规律如何受压力调控。

Method: 对加压的狄拉克半金属α-(BEDT-TTF)₂I₃进行低温磁导率测量，从弱反局域化（WAL）效应提取相相干长度L_φ及其温度标度指数p，并在不同压力下系统分析其变化。

Result: 高压区呈现常规二维退相干行为，L_φ ∝ T^{-p} 且 p≈1/2，符合扩散导体中电子-电子散射机制；接近临界压力P_c≈1.2 GPa时，温度指数降至p≈0.3，而L_φ仍保持较大值（0.5 K时约700–800 nm）。WAL在相变过程中持续存在。

Conclusion: 量子临界点（quantum critical point）附近出现异常的温度标度指数（p≈0.3），暗示狄拉克电子的非弹性散射机制不同于常规扩散导体；WAL的持续存在支持该关联驱动的相变为无能隙或近无能隙（gapless or nearly gapless）的量子相变。

Abstract: We have investigated the weak antilocalization (WAL) in the pressurized Dirac semimetal $α$-(BEDT-TTF)$_2$I$_3$ across a correlation-driven quantum phase transition to a charge-ordered insulating state and evaluated the phase coherence length $L_φ$ and its temperature scaling under various pressures from the low-temperature magnetoconductivity. In the high-pressure regime, the system exhibits the conventional two-dimensional dephasing behavior ($L_φ \propto T^{-p}$ with $p \approx 1/2$), characteristic of electron-electron scattering in diffusive conductors. As the pressure approaches the critical pressure ($P_c \sim 1.2$ GPa), the temperature exponent is suppressed to $p \sim 0.3$, while $L_φ$ remains large ($700\text{-}800$ nm at 0.5 K). This anomalous scaling suggests nontrivial inelastic scattering associated with Dirac electrons near the quantum critical point. The persistence of WAL across the transition supports a gapless or nearly gapless quantum phase transition.

</details>


### [37] [Revisiting magnetoelectric response in collinear antiferromagnetic zigzag chains: A downfolding approach beyond conventional low-energy models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07118)
*Shuhei Kanda,Satoru Hayami*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过多轨道紧束缚模型研究共线反铁磁锯齿链中的磁电效应，发现其微观机制来源于s-p杂化激活的轨道自由度，而非自旋贡献；低能有效模型需通过顶点修正和重整化Kubo公式才能正确描述该效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁体中的磁电（magnetoelectric, ME）效应为探索对称性驱动的交叉关联响应提供了丰富平台，但其微观起源尚不明确，且常被简化低能描述所掩盖。

Method: 采用包含s和p轨道自由度的多轨道紧束缚（tight-binding）模型，基于Kubo公式进行解析和数值计算；利用Schur补导出投影到s轨道子空间的有效哈密顿量；引入顶点修正和准粒子重整化方案构建重整化Kubo公式。

Result: ME响应由s-p杂化激活的轨道自由度主导，自旋贡献因自旋守恒而消失；在低能有效模型中直接应用Kubo公式无法捕捉ME响应，需通过顶点修正纳入轨道杂化效应；重整化Kubo公式能准确重现完整多轨道计算结果。

Conclusion: ME效应源于顶点修正所编码的虚轨道间过程（virtual interorbital processes），而非裸低能哈密顿量；所发展的有效框架提供了轨道驱动ME响应的统一微观理解，并给出了超越简单低能模型系统性地纳入杂化效应的途径。

Abstract: Magnetoelectric (ME) effects in antiferromagnets provide a fertile platform for exploring symmetry-driven cross-correlated responses. However, their microscopic origin remains elusive and is often obscured in simplified low-energy descriptions. In this study, we revisit the microscopic mechanism of the ME effect in a collinear antiferromagnetic zigzag chain by employing a multi-orbital tight-binding model that explicitly includes both $s$- and $p$-orbital degrees of freedom. Using analytical and numerical calculations based on the Kubo formula, we demonstrate that the ME response is governed by orbital degrees of freedom activated through $s$--$p$ hybridization, while the spin contribution vanishes due to spin conservation. To elucidate the low-energy description, we derive an effective Hamiltonian projected onto the $s$-orbital subspace using the Schur complement. We show that a naive application of the Kubo formula within this effective model fails to capture the ME response. This issue is resolved by systematically incorporating vertex corrections in terms of orbital hybridization into the response functions. Furthermore, by introducing a quasiparticle renormalization scheme, we formulate a renormalized Kubo formula that preserves conservation laws and accurately reproduces the full multi-orbital results. Our analysis revisits the conventional low-energy perspective and reveals that the ME effect originates from virtual interorbital processes encoded in vertex corrections, rather than from the bare low-energy Hamiltonian. The effective framework developed here provides a unified microscopic understanding of orbital-driven ME responses and offers a systematic route to incorporate hybridization effects beyond simple low-energy models.

</details>


### [38] [Frustration of harmonic and solitonic helimagnetism on the body-centered tetragonal lattice of GdAlSi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07294)
*Ryota Nakano,Rinsuke Yamada,Oleg I. Utesov,Masaki Gen,Akiko Kikkawa,Hajime Sagayama,Hironori Nakao,Yasujiro Taguchi,Masashi Tokunaga,Taka-hisa Arima,Yoshinori Tokura,Se Kwon Kim,Max Hirschberger*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出体心四方晶格（body-centered tetragonal lattice, BCTL）可实现螺旋磁序谐波与非谐波态之间的阻挫竞争，并在四方磁性韦尔半金属 GdAlSi 中通过共振弹性 X 射线散射实验验证了这一机制，为 BCTL 材料中的阻挫物理提供了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三角格点反铁磁体（triangular lattice antiferromagnet, TLAF）中简并的螺旋磁波及其高次谐波产生了非谐（"上-上-下"）与谐波磁态之间的竞争。本文旨在探索体心四方晶格（BCTL）是否能实现类似的谐波与非谐螺旋磁态阻挫，并寻找具体的材料实现。

Method: 在施加外磁场的条件下，利用共振弹性 X 射线散射（resonant elastic X-ray scattering）技术测量四方磁性韦尔半金属 GdAlSi 的磁结构，并将实验结果与平均场计算（mean-field calculations）进行对比。

Result: 实验观测到谐波摆线态（harmonic cycloidal）与孤子双 Q 态（solitonic double-Q states）之间存在竞争，与平均场计算结果高度吻合。

Conclusion: 体心四方晶格（BCTL）能够实现类似于三角格点反铁磁体中的谐波与非谐螺旋磁态阻挫，GdAlSi 作为具体材料实例验证了该场景。这项工作为 BCTL 材料中的阻挫物理（frustration physics）提供了新范式。

Abstract: The triangular lattice antiferromagnet (TLAF) with nearest-neighbor exchange interaction is a model platform in the field of frustrated magnetism. Here, anharmonic ('up-up-down') and harmonic magnetic states compete, because a helimagnetic wave and its higher harmonic are degenerate in energy. We show that a body-centered tetragonal lattice (BCTL) can realize a similar frustration of harmonic and anharmonic helimagnetic states, and that the tetragonal magnetic Weyl semimetal GdAlSi realizes this scenario. In an applied magnetic field, resonant elastic X-ray scattering reveals a competition of harmonic cycloidal and solitonic double-Q states, well consistent with mean-field calculations. Our work provides a new paradigm for frustration physics in BCTL materials.

</details>
