Abstract: CrRhAs was theoretically proposed to be a kagome metal with unusual magnetic ground states; however, little is known about its magnetic structure and physical properties experimentally. Here, we present an experimental investigation of CrRhAs with ZrNiAl-type structure and a distorted Cr kagome lattice. CrRhAs is an antiferromagnet with TN = 149 K. Combined with the results of heat capacity measurements, a large Kadowaki-Woods ratio α = 33.9 μΩ cm mol2 K2/J2 is obtained. The above results suggest CrRhAs is a strongly correlated kagome metal with multiband and noncollinear magnetic structure features.

### [40] [Emergent Dynamic Magnetic Ground State in a Mixed 3d/5d Heavy Fermion System CaCu3Ir4O12](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07602)
*J. Ming,Abhisek Bandyopadhyay,G. B. G. Stenning,M. T. F. Telling,N. N. Wang,G. Wang,J. -G. Cheng,D. T. Adroja*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: CaCu₃Ir₄O₁₂被确立为一种有前景的三维量子无序磁体（3D quantum-disordered magnet），为在关联3d/5d氧化物中研究涨落主导的磁态提供了一个经过充分表征的平台。

Abstract: Quantum-disordered magnetic ground states are challenging to identify in three-dimensional (3D) oxides, where strong exchange pathways typically favour long-range magnetic order or spin freezing. The quadruple perovskite $\mathrm{CaCu_3Ir_4O_{12}}$, crystallizing in the cubic $Im\bar{3}$ structure, provides a 3D lattice where $\mathrm{Cu^{2+}}$ $3d$ moments are coupled to an extended Ir $5d$ network, offering a rare platform for probing quantum-disordered magnetism in a mixed $3d/5d$ electron system. Here, we combine bulk probes, including DC and AC magnetic susceptibility, and heat capacity measurements (down to $50~\mathrm{mK}$), along with the local microscopic probe muon spin relaxation ($μ$SR) (down to $40~\mathrm{mK}$), to investigate the true magnetic ground state of $\mathrm{CaCu_3Ir_4O_{12}}$. Despite strong antiferromagnetic interactions ($θ_{\mathrm{W}} \sim -200~\mathrm{K}$, with an applied-field dependence), no signature of long-range magnetic ordering or spin freezing is detected down to the lowest measured temperatures. Furthermore, our in-depth zero-field (ZF) and longitudinal-field (LF) $μ$SR characterizations confirm strong quantum spin fluctuations and the truly dynamic nature of the local moments down to $40~\mathrm{mK}$. These results establish $\mathrm{CaCu_3Ir_4O_{12}}$ as a promising 3D quantum-disordered magnet and a well-characterized platform for exploring fluctuation-dominated states in correlated $3d/5d$ oxides.

### [41] [Ground states of quantum XY dipoles on the Archimedean lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07685)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用大规模密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）数值计算，在11种阿基米德晶格中的9种上求解基态性质；对有序态进一步计算流体力学参数（磁化强度、磁化率、刚度）并与线性自旋波理论（linear spin wave theory）进行对比。

Conclusion: 阿基米德晶格的几何结构显著影响偶极XY模型的基态相图；长程偶极相互作用在三角晶格等体系中导致丰富的竞争相，而kagome晶格可能支持狄拉克自旋液体，为后续理论研究提供了重要基准。

Abstract: We report numerical ground states for the dipolar XY spin model, which describes extended antiferromagnetic interactions in two-dimensional arrays of polar molecules and two-level Rydberg atoms. Carrying out large-scale density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) calculations, we compute ground state properties on nine of the eleven Archimedean lattices--tilings of the plane by regular polygons. Four of these host trivial paramagnets, while another four develop collinear Neel magnetic order, as was found previously for the square lattice. For the ordered states, we calculate the hydrodynamic parameters (magnetization, susceptibility, and stiffness) and compare to linear spin wave theory. We also investigate the triangular lattice, for which we find several competing phases including coplanar magnetism, stripe density wave order, and a possible spin liquid; their relative stability is sensitive to the long-range couplings present in our dipolar model. Finally, the Archimedean classification is completed by the kagome lattice, which we argue in a companion work is likely to be a Dirac spin liquid.

Method: 采用动力学顶点近似（dynamical vertex approximation）对Emery模型进行数值计算，系统考察了包含近邻和次近邻氧-氧跳迁在内的多跳迁参数对超导相图的影响。

Conclusion: Emery模型虽能定性捕捉铜氧化物超导体的超导穹顶行为，但为达到定量精度并正确描述d波配对对称性，必须包含更多远程跳迁项。

Abstract: The Emery model is the quintessential model for cuprate superconductors. In his eponymous paper, Emery only considered the next-nearest-neighbor oxygen-copper hopping. Later, also the relevance of nearest- and next-nearest oxygen-oxygen hoppings has been pointed out. Using dynamical vertex approximation, we find a superconducting dome consistent with cuprates. However, long-range hoppings beyond the three conventional hopping parameters are necessary for the quantitatively correct phase diagram and for a proper d-wave order parameter.

### [43] [Probabilistic denoising for reliable signal extraction in spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07819)
*Younsik Kim,Changyoung Kim*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种概率去噪框架，能够从含噪声数据中同时提取去噪信号和逐元素预测不确定性（element-wise predictive uncertainties）。将该方法应用于三维角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）数据和二维X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）数据。

Conclusion: 该工作将具有不确定性意识的深度学习（uncertainty-aware deep learning）从单纯的“可视化工具”提升为科学数据分析的严谨框架（rigorous framework），为深度学习在科学研究中的定量可靠应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: While deep learning offers powerful capabilities for scientific research, its application is often hindered by a lack of quantitative reliability. To address this, we introduce a probabilistic denoising framework that simultaneously extracts denoised signals and element-wise predictive uncertainties from noisy data. We demonstrate this approach on three-dimensional angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy data, showing that the model reliably recovers the spectral features of a cuprate superconductor from Poisson-distributed noise with an average count of only 0.02 electrons per voxel. Crucially, we show that these predicted uncertainties can be propagated into subsequent superconducting gap analyses, enabling quantitative parameter extraction with scientifically meaningful error bars. Furthermore, we validate the broad applicability of our approach by successfully extending it to two-dimensional X-ray diffraction data. Ultimately, this approach establishes uncertainty-aware deep learning not merely as a visualization tool, but as a rigorous framework for scientific data analysis.

Abstract: SrCu2(BO3)2 (SCBO) is a paradigmatic realization of the Shastry-Sutherland model, hosting geometrically frustrated spin dimers and a variety of quantum magnetic phases and phenomena. Although its magnetic properties have been extensively studied, the high-energy electronic excitations that determine the crystal-field environment and Cu-O hybridization have remained largely unexplored. Here we combine Cu L3-edge resonant inelastic x-ray scattering (RIXS), broadband optical spectroscopy, and electronic-structure calculations to determine the relevant local and interband excitation energy scales in SCBO. In contrast, optical spectroscopy identifies charge-transfer excitations with an absorption onset near 1.2-1.6 eV and a broader higher-energy structure around 4.5 eV, which are qualitatively captured by DFT+U calculations. Taken together, these results define the characteristic energy scales of d-d and CT excitations, offering quantitative benchmarks for computational frameworks and providing essential input for refining superexchange-based magnetic models of this prototypical frustrated quantum antiferromagnet.

Motivation: 对新型手性四方穹顶（chiral square-cupola）反铁磁体 Pb(TiO)Cu₄(PO₄)₄ 的微观超精细和局域场参数尚未有系统表征，且其与同族 Ba/Sr 类似物之间的差异机制尚不明确。本文旨在通过核磁共振（NMR）填补这一空白，从原子尺度理解该系列材料的磁性行为差异。

Method: 采用 ³¹P 和 ⁶³,⁶⁵Cu 核磁共振（NMR）技术，测量转移超精细耦合（transferred hyperfine coupling）、内部场（internal field）和四极频率（quadrupole frequency）；结合点电荷电场梯度（point-charge electric-field-gradient）计算和 Sternheimer 修正，提取 Cu 位空穴占据数。

Result: (1) 高于尼尔温度（T_N ≈ 6.7 K）时，³¹P Knight 位移跟随体磁化率，给出近各向同性的转移超精细耦合 H_hf^(010)=6.77(3) kOe/μ_B 和 H_hf^(001)=6.19(3) kOe/μ_B；(2) 低于 T_N 时，³¹P 谱分裂为三条谱线（BaTCPO 为四条线），线间距与静态内部场 onset 一致，临界指数 β≈0.23 符合准二维临界性（quasi-two-dimensional criticality）；(3) 零场 ⁶³,⁶⁵Cu NMR 给出 Cu 位内部场 B_int=14.50(6) T 和四极频率 ν_Q=32.72(5) MHz，计算得到 Cu 空穴占据数 n_d=0.20(4)；(4) PbTCPO 的有序态 ³¹P 内部场（69.5 mT）远高于 BaTCPO（35.6 mT）和 SrTCPO（34.6 mT）。

Conclusion: PbTCPO 的有序态 ³¹P 内部场显著增强无法仅由偶极项（dipolar terms）解释，表明转移贡献（transferred contributions）和堆叠依赖抵消（stacking-dependent cancellation）共同起了关键作用。此外，跨系列转移超精细耦合 H_hf 的差异反映了局域 Cu-O-P 共价性的变化，而 Cu 空穴占据数结果与配体空穴主导的电荷转移特性一致。

Abstract: We report a comprehensive NMR study of the chiral square-cupola antiferromagnet Pb(TiO)Cu$_4$(PO$_4$)$_4$ and compare its microscopic hyperfine and local-field parameters with the Ba/Sr analogues in the $A$(TiO)Cu$_4$(PO$_4$)$_4$ family. Above $T_{\rm N}\simeq 6.7$ K, the $^{31}$P Knight shift tracks the bulk susceptibility and yields nearly isotropic transferred hyperfine couplings $H_{\rm hf}^{[010]}=6.77(3)$ and $H_{\rm hf}^{[001]}=6.19(3)$ kOe/$μ_{\rm B}$. Below $T_{\rm N}$, the frequency-swept $^{31}$P spectrum splits into three lines, in contrast to the four-line pattern reported for BaTCPO. The line separation tracks the onset of the static $^{31}$P internal field with a power-law exponent $β\simeq 0.23$, consistent with quasi-two-dimensional criticality. Crystal-rotation $^{31}$P NMR in the ordered state resolves all eight symmetry-related P sites and their site-dependent anisotropy. In the ordered state, zero-field $^{63,65}$Cu NMR gives a Cu-site internal field $B_{\rm int}=14.50(6)$ T and a quadrupole frequency $ν_Q=32.72(5)$ MHz, while point-charge electric-field-gradient calculations including Sternheimer corrections yield an on-site Cu hole occupancy $n_d=0.20(4)$, consistent with a ligand-hole-dominated charge-transfer character. Comparing PbTCPO with BaTCPO and SrTCPO, we find that the transferred hyperfine coupling $H_{\rm hf}$ varies across the series, reflecting changes in local Cu-O-P covalency, whereas the ordered-state $^{31}$P internal field in PbTCPO is $69.5$ mT, considerably higher than in BaTCPO ($35.6$ mT) and SrTCPO ($34.6$ mT). This enhancement is not captured by dipolar terms alone and points to the combined effects of transferred contributions and stacking-dependent cancellation.

</details>


### [47] [Light-driven octupolar inverse Faraday effect and multipolar order in Mott insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08049)
*Saikat Banerjee,Tara Steinhöfel,Florian Lange,Matthias Eschrig,Holger Fehske*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过Floquet Schrieffer-Wolff展开方法，证明了圆偏振光可以在具有边共享八面体结构的$4d^2/5d^2$体系中产生两种新的光驱动多极项：一个与磁八极矩线性耦合的有效静态场（即八极逆法拉第效应），以及一个在平衡态中不存在的依赖于键的各向异性交换相互作用。这两种耦合使得研究者能够光学调控隐藏的八极序、扩展Kitaev-like多极液体相，并诱导可逆的晶格畸变，从而建立了光学生成、控制和检测隐藏多极量子态的一般机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋-轨道耦合Mott绝缘体（spin-orbit-coupled Mott insulators）中隐藏的多极序（hidden multipolar orders）为关联量子物质（correlated quantum matter）提供了有前景的研究平台，但如何控制和检测这些隐藏序态仍是重大挑战。本文旨在探索利用圆偏振光（circularly polarized light）实现对多极序的光学操控。

Method: 对一个受驱动的Hubbard-Kanamori模型（driven Hubbard-Kanamori model）进行Floquet Schrieffer-Wolff展开（Floquet Schrieffer-Wolff expansion），推导出低能多极哈密顿量（low-energy multipolar Hamiltonian），其中包含两种定性的新光驱动项。

Result: 获得的两种新耦合项分别是：（1）一个与磁八极矩线性耦合的有效静态场，实现了八极逆法拉第效应（octupolar inverse Faraday effect）；（2）一种依赖于键的各向异性交换相互作用（bond-dependent anisotropic exchange interaction），在平衡态中不存在。这两种耦合的光学调控使得体系可以在反铁八极、铁八极、部分极化铁四极、Ising八极和多极液体相等多种多极相之间调谐。此外，诱导的多极序还产生可逆的三方和四方晶格畸变（trigonal and tetragonal distortions），可作为泵浦-探测实验（pump-probe experiments）中的结构指纹。

Conclusion: 本文建立了光学生成、控制和检测隐藏多极量子态（hidden multipolar quantum states）的一般机制，为利用光场操控关联量子物质中的隐藏序提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Hidden multipolar orders in spin-orbit-coupled Mott insulators provide a promising setting for correlated quantum matter, yet their control and detection remain major challenges. Here, we demonstrate that circularly polarized light enables both in $4d^2/5d^2$ systems with edge-sharing octahedra. Using a Floquet Schrieffer-Wolff expansion of a driven Hubbard-Kanamori model, we derive a low-energy multipolar Hamiltonian with two qualitatively new light-driven terms. One is an effective static field that couples linearly to the magnetic octupole, realizing an octupolar inverse Faraday effect. The other is a bond-dependent anisotropic exchange interaction absent in equilibrium. These two couplings are the key result of this work: the first provides a direct optical handle on hidden octupolar order, while the second reorganizes the multipolar exchange landscape and opens an enlarged Kitaev-like multipolar liquid regime. Their interplay produces a nonequilibrium multipolar phase space inaccessible in equilibrium, enabling optical tuning among antiferro-octupolar, ferro-octupolar, partially polarized ferro-quadrupolar, Ising octupolar, and multipolar liquid phases. We further show that the induced multipolar order couples to the lattice, generating reversible trigonal and tetragonal distortions that provide structural fingerprints in pump-probe experiments. Our work establishes a general mechanism for the optical generation, control, and detection of hidden multipolar quantum states.

</details>


### [48] [Gapped 1/9 Magnetization Plateau in the Anisotropic Kagome Antiferromagnet Y-kapellasite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08067)
*Dipranjan Chatterjee,Paul A. Goddard,Ewan R. P. Thomas,Katharina M. Zoch,Hank C. H. Wu,Benjamin M. Huddart,Cornelius Krellner,Edwin Kermarrec,Mladen Horvatić,Steffen Krämer,Pascal Puphal,John Singleton,Stephen J. Blundell,Fabrice Bert*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过脉冲磁场磁化测量和核磁共振（NMR）技术，在kagome反铁磁体Y-kapellasite中观测到包括1/9和1/3在内的分数磁化平台，揭示了1/9平台伴随的有序自旋构型、低能自旋涨落的强烈抑制和能隙行为，表明该平台对应于有能隙的分数化（fractional）量子态，且该态对材料磁性细节的变化具有鲁棒性（robustness）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数磁化平台（fractional magnetization plateaus）是研究受挫量子磁体中多体自旋态（many-body spin states）的灵敏探针，但kagome反铁磁体中分数平台的微观起源尚未解决，尤其是理论上预测但实验中极少观测到的1/9平台，其形成机制亟需阐明。

Method: 对S=1/2各向异性kagome反铁磁体Y-kapellasite（Y₃Cu₉(OH)₁₉Cl₈）的单晶进行脉冲磁场磁化测量（pulsed-field magnetization measurements）以及高场³⁵Cl核磁共振（NMR）实验。

Result: 观测到包括1/3和1/9平台在内的场致分数特征（field-induced fractional features）以及一个较弱的低场特征；进一步分析1/9平台上的NMR谱和磁化率，发现该平台伴随着有序局域自旋构型（ordered local spin configuration）、低能自旋涨落的强烈抑制以及激活行为（activated behavior），符合有能隙的分数化态（gapped fractional state）的特征；这些特征与另一同平台材料YCu₃(OH)₆Br₂[Br₁−y(OH)y]中的表现不同，表明1/9态对磁性细节具有显著鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 在kagome反铁磁体Y-kapellasite中确认了1/9分数磁化平台的存在，并证明该平台对应一个有能隙的分数化量子态；不同材料中1/9态的相似性暗示该态对磁性相互作用的细节不敏感，具有物理上的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Fractional magnetization plateaus provide a sensitive probe of many-body spin states in frustrated quantum magnets, yet their microscopic origin in kagome antiferromagnets remains unresolved. This is particularly true of the mysterious $1/9$ plateau, which is predicted by theory but infrequently observed in experiment. Here, we investigate this problem in the $S = 1/2$ anisotropic kagome antiferromagnet Y-kapellasite, Y$_3$Cu$_9$(OH)$_{19}$Cl$_8$, using pulsed-field magnetization measurements on single crystals and high-field $^{35}$Cl NMR. We identify a hierarchy of field-induced fractional features, including $1/3$ and $1/9$ plateaus, as well as a weaker low-field feature. Analysis of the NMR spectra and the magnetic susceptibility across the $1/9$ plateau demonstrate that it is accompanied by an ordered local spin configuration, a strong suppression of low-energy spin fluctuations and activated behavior, consistent with a gapped fractional state. These features differ from those in the only other material YCu$_3$(OH)$_6$Br$_2$[Br$_{1-y}$(OH)$_y$] in which this plateau is observed, implying a surprising robustness of the $1/9$ state to the details of the underlying magnetism.

</details>

Zhao,Y. L. Zhao,Y. P. Zhao,Y. X. Zhao,Z. G. Zhao,A. Zhemchugov,B. Zheng,B. M. Zheng,J. P. Zheng,W. J. Zheng,W. Q. Zheng,X. R. Zheng,Y. H. Zheng,B. Zhong,C. Zhong,H. Zhou,J. Q. Zhou,S. Zhou,X. Zhou,X. K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器收集的约27.1亿psi(3686)事件，首次联合测量了Xi(1530)^{-}衰变至Xi^{0} pi^{-}和Xi^{-} pi^{0}的绝对分支比（branching fraction），并更新了psi(3686)至反Xi^{+} Xi(1530)^{-} + c.c.的分支比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Xi(1530)^{-}的两个主要衰变模式Xi^{0} pi^{-}和Xi^{-} pi^{0}的绝对分支比此前尚未被实验直接测量，因此需要利用大统计量的psi(3686)数据样本进行精确测定。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器收集的(2712.4±14.3)×10^6个psi(3686)事件，通过psi(3686) → 反Xi^{+} Xi(1530)^{-} + c.c.过程联合分析两个衰变道；在同位旋对称性（isospin symmetry）假设下，将两个衰变模式视为完全关联（fully correlated），并结合关联效应进行拟合。

Result: 首次测得Xi(1530)^{-} → Xi^{0} pi^{-}的分支比为(61.4±4.5±4.6)%，Xi(1530)^{-} → Xi^{-} pi^{0}的分支比为(29.7±2.2±2.2)%，两者联合分支比为(91.1±6.7±6.8)%；同时更新psi(3686) → 反Xi^{+} Xi(1530)^{-} + c.c.的分支比为(8.67±0.52±0.58±0.57)×10^{-6}。

Conclusion: 上述结果首次提供了Xi(1530)^{-}两个主要衰变模式的绝对分支比实验数据，并提高了psi(3686)相关衰变分支比的测量精度，对理解重子谱及强相互作用具有参考价值。

Abstract: Based on (2712.4+-14.3)*10^{6} psi(3686) events collected with the BESIII detector, the decays Xi(1530)^{-} to Xi^{0} pi^{-} and Xi(1530)^{-} to Xi^{-} pi^{0} are investigated jointly via the process psi(3686) to anti-Xi^{+} Xi(1530)^{-} + c.c. Under the assumption of isospin symmetry, the two decay modes are treated as fully correlated, and we report the first measurement of their absolute branching fractions. The results are B(Xi(1530)^{-} to Xi^{0} pi^{-})=(61.4+-4.5+-4.6)% and B(Xi(1530)^{-} to Xi^{-} pi^{0}) =(29.7+-2.2+-2.2)%. The combined branching fraction of the two decays is B(Xi(1530)^{-} to (Xi pi)^{-})=(91.1+-6.7+-6.8)%, with uncertainties accounting for the correlations between the two modes. Here, the first uncertainties are statistical, while the second are systematic. Additionally, we update the branching fraction of the decay psi(3686) to anti-Xi^{+} Xi(1530)^{-} + c.c. The updated measurement is B(psi(3686) to anti-Xi^{+} Xi(1530)^{-} + c.c.)=(8.67+-0.52+-0.58+-0.57)*10^{-6}, where the first uncertainty is statistical, the second is systematic related to event selection and the fit model, and the third is associated with the interference effect.

</details>


### [50] [Search for Sub-GeV Axion-Like Particles at EBES Pilot Run Using 4 GeV Positron Beam at KEK LINAC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07108)
*Takahiro Fusayasu,Tomoya Iizawa,Fumihito Ikeda,Akimasa Ishikawa,Masako Iwasaki,Hiroshi Iwase,Takahiro Kawahara,Aoi Masaki,Fusashi Miyahara,Yu Morikawa,Yuichi Okayasu,Toshiyuki Ono,Hidetoshi Otono,Yasuhito Sakaki,Takumi Seino,Yuta Shimasaki,Taikan Suehara,Yosuke Takubo,Shusaku Tsumura,Kosuke Uemura,Yifu Zhang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 利用KEK LINAC Switching Yard 3 (EBES)的电子束-束靶实验（Electron Beam-dump Experiment）导引运行数据，搜索亚GeV级类轴子粒子（axion-like particles, ALPs）。基于$1.3\times10^{14}$个4 GeV正电子轰击钨靶的数据，未观测到信号事件，在ALP质量-耦合参数空间导出90%置信水平的上限，拓展了此前实验未覆盖的区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 填补亚GeV能区类轴子粒子（ALPs）实验搜索的空白，探索此前实验未触及的参数空间区域。

Method: 利用KEK LINAC Switching Yard 3的电子束-束靶实验（EBES）导引运行数据，使用4 GeV正电子束与钨束靶（beam dump）及单个PbO量热器（calorimeter）。ALP通过轫致辐射（bremsstrahlung）光子在束靶中引发Primakoff过程产生，随后衰变为两个光子（$a\toγγ$）。采用数据驱动方法（data-driven method）估计本底，定义信号区域使预期本底产额低于0.1个事件。

Result: 揭盲后未观测到任何事件。在ALP质量-耦合参数平面导出了90%置信水平（confidence level）的上限，扩展了实验覆盖范围至此前搜索未探索的参数空间区域。

Conclusion: 基于EBES导引运行数据，未发现亚GeV类轴子粒子（ALPs）存在的证据，但所导出的上限约束填补了该能区实验空白。

Abstract: We report the results of a search for sub-GeV axion-like particles (ALPs) using pilot run data from the Electron Beam-dump Experiment at KEK LINAC Switching Yard 3 (EBES). The data were collected in December 2023 with a 4 GeV positron beam and correspond to $1.3\times10^{14}$ positrons on target. In the pilot run setup, a tungsten beam dump and a single PbO calorimeter were used. We consider ALP production via the Primakoff process induced by bremsstrahlung photons in the beam dump, followed by the decay $a\toγγ$. The background was estimated with a data-driven method, and a signal region was defined such that the expected background yield is below 0.1 events. No events were observed after unblinding. Upper limits at the 90% confidence level were derived in the ALP mass-coupling plane, extending the experimental coverage into a region of parameter space not explored by previous searches.

</details>

Zhang,Z. Y. Zhang,Zh. Zh. Zhang,G. Zhao,J. -P. Zhao,J. Y. Zhao,J. Z. Zhao,L. Zhao,L. Zhao,M. G. Zhao,R. P. Zhao,S. J. Zhao,Y. B. Zhao,Y. L. Zhao,Y. P. Zhao,Y. X. Zhao,Z. G. Zhao,A. Zhemchugov,B. Zheng,B. M. Zheng,J. P. Zheng,W. J. Zheng,W. Q. Zheng,X. R. Zheng,Y. H. Zheng,B. Zhong,C. Zhong,H. Zhou,J. Q. Zhou,S. Zhou,X. Zhou,X. K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究基于BESIII探测器收集的7.33 fb⁻¹数据，首次测量了Dₛ⁺→K*(892)⁰μ⁺ν_μ衰变并改进了电子道测量，给出了分支比、强子形状因子参数以及微分衰变率与轻子前后不对称性系数，并检验了轻子味普适性，未发现违背。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Dₛ⁺介子的半轻衰变（semileptonic decay）有助于检验非微扰量子色动力学（QCD）理论计算；此前Dₛ⁺→K*(892)⁰μ⁺ν_μ从未被测量，且电子道分支比和形状因子（form factor）参数精度有限，强子形状因子A₁(0)此前未被直接测量。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的质心能量4.128–4.226 GeV范围内的7.33 fb⁻¹ e⁺e⁻湮灭数据，对Dₛ⁺→K*(892)⁰μ⁺ν_μ和Dₛ⁺→K*(892)⁰e⁺ν_e两个衰变道进行同时分析，提取分支比、形状因子参数及微分分布。

Result: 测得分支比B(Dₛ⁺→K*(892)⁰μ⁺ν_μ)=(2.07±0.22_stat±0.10_syst)×10⁻³，B(Dₛ⁺→K*(892)⁰e⁺ν_e)=(2.14±0.18_stat±0.10_syst)×10⁻³；形状因子比值r_V=V(0)/A₁(0)=1.63±0.14_stat±0.08_syst，r₂=A₂(0)/A₁(0)=0.60±0.13_stat±0.06_syst，A₁(0)=0.56±0.02_stat±0.01_syst（首次测量）；在完整与分区间q²检验中均未发现轻子味普适性（lepton flavor universality）破坏。

Conclusion: 该工作首次完成了Dₛ⁺→K*(892)⁰跃迁动力学完整研究，显著提高了形状因子参数r_V与r₂的精度，首次给出A₁(0)的实验值，并为非微扰理论计算提供了严格检验；轻子味普适性在误差范围内成立。

Abstract: We report the first measurement of the semileptonic decay $D^+_s \rightarrow K^*(892)^0μ^+ν_μ$ and an improved measurement of the decay $D^+_s \rightarrow K^*(892)^0 e^+ν_{e}$ using a sample of $7.33~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ of $e^+e^-$ annihilation data collected at center-of-mass energies between 4.128 to 4.226~GeV with the BESIII detector at the BEPCII collider. We measure the branching fractions to be $\mathcal B({D^+_s\rightarrow K^*(892)^0 μ^+ν_μ})=(2.07\pm0.22_{\rm stat}\pm0.10_{\rm syst})\times10^{-3}$ and $\mathcal B({D^+_s\rightarrow K^*(892)^0 e^+ν_{e}})=(2.14\pm0.18_{\rm stat}\pm0.10_{\rm syst})\times10^{-3}$. Based on a simultaneous study of the dynamics in two semileptonic decays, the hadronic form factor parameters in the $D^+_s\rightarrow K^{*}(892)^0$ transition are determined to be $r_{V} = V(0)/A_1(0) = 1.63 \pm 0.14_{\rm stat} \pm 0.08_{\rm syst}$, $r_{2} = A_2(0)/A_1(0) = 0.60 \pm 0.13_{\rm stat} \pm 0.06_{\rm syst}$, and $A_1(0)=0.56 \pm 0.02_{\rm stat} \pm 0.01_{\rm syst}$, where $V(0)$ is the vector form factor and $A_{1,2}(0)$ are the axial-vector form factors evaluated at $q^2=0$. The precision of $r_V$ and $r_2$ is improved by twofold and $A_1(0)$ is measured for the first time. We also report the first model-independent measurements of the differential decay rates and the lepton forward-backward asymmetries for $D^+_s\rightarrow K^{*}(892)^0\ell^+ν_{\ell}$ decays. Based on these measurements, we perform a test of lepton flavor universality in full and separate $q^2$ intervals with $D^+_s\rightarrow K^{*}(892)^0\ell^+ν_{\ell}$ decays. No violation is found within uncertainties. Our results present for the first time a complete study of the dynamics in the $D_s^+\rightarrow K^*(892)^0$ transition, and provide stringent tests of various non-perturbative theoretical calculations.

</details>


### [52] [NEXT Simulation Dataset for AI Summer School UC Irvine 2026](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07566)
*K. Mistry*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文档发布了模拟的0νββ（无中微子双β衰变）事件以及来自高压氙气中$^{214}$Bi衰变的本底事件数据集，这些事件模拟了NEXT探测器中产生的信号；该数据集作为2026年6月20-21日在加州大学尔湾分校举办的0νββ AI暑期学校的一部分发布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为0νββ AI暑期学校提供模拟数据集，支持参与者开发和测试基于人工智能（artificial intelligence）的0νββ事件与放射性本底事件的区分方法。

Method: 通过模拟高压氙气中0νββ衰变事件以及来自$^{214}$Bi衰变的本底事件来生成数据集，事件特征与NEXT探测器中的信号类似。

Result: 成功生成了模拟的0νββ事件和$^{214}$Bi本底事件数据集，可作为暑期学校的标准数据资源。

Conclusion: 该数据集的发布为0νββ研究领域的AI方法开发提供了标准化数据基础，有助于推动基于机器学习的稀有事件识别技术。

Abstract: This document details the dataset release of simulated $0νββ$ and background events originating from the decay of $^{214}$Bi in high-pressure xenon gas, describing events similar to those produced in the NEXT detector. This release is part of the Neutrinoless Double Beta Decay ($0νββ$) AI Summer School held on June 20-21 2026 at the University of California, Irvine.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于LHCb实验8.4 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，利用全角分布对$\overline{B}^0 \to \overline{K}^{*0}μ^+μ^-$衰变过程进行$C\!P$破坏搜索，通过无分箱最大似然拟合提取弱有效理论中的复数Wilson系数，将$C\!P$破坏观测量精度提升一个数量级，未发现显著$C\!P$破坏，结果与标准模型一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在味改变中性流（flavour-changing neutral-current, FCNC）过程$\overline{B}^0 \to \overline{K}^{*0}μ^+μ^-$中搜索$C\!P$破坏（$C\!P$ violation），以检验标准模型（Standard Model, SM）并探寻可能的新物理信号。

Method: 利用LHCb实验在Run 1与Run 2期间收集的质心能量为8.4 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据，对$\overline{B}^0 \to \overline{K}^{*0}μ^+μ^-$衰变的全角分布（full angular distribution）进行分析；在弱有效理论（Weak Effective Theory, WET）框架下，通过无分箱最大似然拟合（unbinned maximum-likelihood fit）确定复数Wilson系数（complex Wilson coefficients），并纳入全双缪子质量谱上的非定域强子振幅（nonlocal hadronic amplitudes）。

Result: $C\!P$破坏观测量（$C\!P$-violation observables）的测量精度较此前结果提升了一个数量级（an order of magnitude）；Wilson系数的虚部（imaginary parts）的测定精度高于实部（real parts）；未观测到显著的$C\!P$破坏信号。

Conclusion: 测量结果与标准模型预言一致，表明在当前统计精度下该衰变通道中不存在显著的$C\!P$破坏新物理效应。

Abstract: A search for $C\!P$ violation in the $\overline{B}^0 \to \overline{K}^{*0}μ^+μ^-$ decay is performed using proton--proton collision data collected by the LHCb experiment during Run 1 and Run 2, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 8.4 fb$^{-1}$. The analysis exploits the full angular distribution of the decay, providing sensitivity to $C\!P$-violating effects in both vector and axial-vector contributions to this flavour-changing neutral-current process. The complex Wilson coefficients are determined within the Weak Effective Theory through an unbinned maximum-likelihood fit to the angular observables, incorporating nonlocal hadronic amplitudes across the full dimuon mass spectrum. The precision of the $C\!P$-violation observables is improved by an order of magnitude relative to previous measurements, with the imaginary parts of the Wilson coefficients now determined more precisely than the real parts. No significant $C\!P$ violation is observed, and the results are consistent with Standard Model.

</details>

Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于LHCb实验采集的9 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，以3.5σ显著性首次获得B⁰_s→φη′衰变的证据，并测定了其相对于B⁰_s→φφ的分支比及绝对分支比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找B⁰_s介子到φη′的稀有衰变过程，检验粒子物理标准模型（Standard Model）的预测，并探索可能的新物理（new physics）信号。

Method: 利用LHCb实验在2011至2018年间收集的质子-质子对撞数据，总积分亮度对应9 fb⁻¹，通过统计显著性分析测量B⁰_s→φη′衰变信号，并与B⁰_s→φφ衰变进行分支比相对比较。

Result: 以3.5σ显著性发现B⁰_s→φη′衰变证据；相对分支比R=(3.56±0.79±0.18±0.06)×10⁻²；绝对分支比B(B⁰_s→φη′)=(0.66±0.15±0.03±0.02)×10⁻⁶，其中不确定度依次对应统计（statistical）、系统（systematic）及外部分支比贡献。

Conclusion: 该结果为B⁰_s→φη′衰变的存在提供了实验证据，测量精度受限于当前数据统计量，后续需更多数据以提升显著性并检验标准模型预言。

Abstract: Using a dataset corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $9 \,\textrm{fb}^{-1}$ collected in proton-proton collisions between 2011 and 2018 by the LHCb experiment, evidence is found for the decay $B^0_s\toφη'$ with $3.5 σ$ significance. The branching ratio relative to the $B^0_s\toφφ$ decay is determined to be $R=(3.56 \pm 0.79\pm 0.18\pm 0.06)\times10^{-2}$. This corresponds to a branching fraction, $B(B^0_s\toφη')=(0.66 \pm 0.15 \pm 0.03 \pm 0.02) \times 10^{-6}$ where, in both cases, the first uncertainty is statistical, the second systematic, and the third due to external branching fractions.

</details>

### [55] [Physics inspired quantum algorithm for QCD splitting functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06789)
*Gabriel Rouxinol,Yacine Haddad,Cenk Tüysüz,Sofia Vallecorsa,Michele Grossi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种模块化量子电路基本单元，用于模拟QCD部分子分裂中的纠缠动力学，并以此作为数据驱动、物理一致的即插即用事件生成构件。在纯胶子通道中，推导了分裂顶点处手征性纠缠的解析表达式（以并发度量化），构建了双量子比特电路，其测量结果编码出射胶子间的动量分配并复现QCD预测的纠缠结构。通过将电路参数校准至LHC喷注子结构数据，重构的动量分配分数与电路旋转角直接关联。多个分裂基本单元的组合生成多支动量分配分布；三支和四支情况与实验数据吻合良好。针对三支构型，在超导量子硬件上执行电路，经标准质量截断后结果与模拟一致。该工作为编码分裂动力学层面量子关联的量子原生部分子簇射模块提供了具体框架，并为未来QCD量子算法提供了物理启发的拟设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前高能物理蒙特卡罗事件生成器难以在分裂动力学层面精确刻画量子纠缠效应，而量子计算有望提供原生编码量子关联的新范式。本文旨在弥合QCD理论预测与LHC实验数据之间的差距，利用量子电路直接模拟部分子分裂中的纠缠结构。

Method: 提出模块化量子电路基本单元，以双量子比特电路建模纯胶子通道的分裂过程；推导并发度（concurrence）作为纠缠度量，并将电路旋转角映射到动量分配分数。通过校准至LHC喷注子结构数据确定电路参数，并组合多个基本单元构建多支构型。

Result: 双量子比特电路能准确复现QCD预言的纠缠结构；三支和四支动量分配分数分布与实验数据吻合良好；三支构型在超导量子硬件上的执行结果经标准质量截断后与模拟一致，得益于低量子比特数和浅电路深度。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了量子原生部分子簇射模块的具体框架，使得在分裂动力学层面编码量子关联成为可能，并为未来面向QCD的量子算法提供了物理启发的拟设（physics-informed ansatz）。

Abstract: We introduce a modular quantum circuit primitive to model entanglement dynamics in QCD parton splitting and use it as a composable building block for data-driven, physics-consistent event generation. For the pure-gluon channel, we derive an analytic expression for the helicity entanglement generated at the splitting vertex, quantified via the concurrence, and construct a two-qubit circuit whose measurement outcomes encode the momentum shared between outgoing gluons while reproducing the QCD-predicted entanglement structure. Calibrating the circuit parameters to LHC jet substructure data maps, reconstructed momentum-sharing fractions are directly related to circuit rotation angles. Composing multiple splitting primitives yields multi-prong momentum-fraction distributions; we validate the three- and four-prong cases against experimental data and find good agreement. For the three-prong configuration, we execute the circuit on superconducting quantum hardware and obtain results consistent with simulation after standard quality cuts, enabled by the low qubit count and shallow circuit depth. This work provides a concrete framework for quantum-native parton-shower modules that encode quantum correlations at the level of splitting dynamics, and offers physics-informed ansätze for future quantum algorithms for QCD.

### [56] [Giant-atom-enabled quantum optics with valley-polarized photons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06771)
*Marcel A. Pinto,Giovanni Luca Sferrazza,Silvia Casulleras,Alejandro Gonzalez-Tudela,Daniele De Bernardis,Francesco Ciccarello*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出在量子光学中利用非局域耦合的“巨型原子”（giant atom）选择性激发光子晶格中的谷自由度（valley degree of freedom），实现谷偏振发射（valley-polarized emission）和手性发射（chiral emission），无需破坏时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 谷电子学（valleytronics）和谷光子学（valley photonics）利用谷自由度进行信息编码与操控。现有方法在量子光学层面实现对光子谷的选择性激发仍面临挑战，尤其是如何在不破坏电磁介质时间反演对称性的条件下实现手性发射。

Method: 考虑一个两能级量子比特（qubit）作为巨型原子，其与工程化的蜂窝状谐振器晶格（honeycomb lattice of resonators）在多个耦合点（coupling points）非局域耦合，该晶格子晶格频率（sublattice frequencies）失谐。通过调整耦合点的几何结构，使巨型原子选择性地发射到单一谷中；进一步将量子比特置于相反子晶格失谐区域之间的畴壁（domain wall）附近，其界面支持谷偏振边缘模（valley-polarized edge modes）。

Result: 巨型原子能够选择性地发射到单一光子谷，发射光子获得明确的谷特征（valley character）并继承相应的贝里曲率（Berry curvature）；在畴壁附近，发射变为沿畴壁的手性发射（chiral emission）。

Conclusion: 该方案为在电路量子电动力学（circuit QED）等平台上实现单光子级别的抗无序手性发射（disorder-robust chiral emission）提供了可行路径，无需破坏电磁介质的时间反演对称性。

Abstract: Valleytronics and valley photonics exploit the valley degree of freedom to encode and manipulate information. Here we show that photonic valleys can be selectively addressed in quantum optics using a simple two-level emitter, provided it is coupled nonlocally to the field, thereby realizing a so-called giant atom. Specifically, we consider a qubit coupled at multiple points to an engineered honeycomb lattice of resonators with detuned sublattice frequencies. By tailoring the geometry of the coupling points, the giant atom can be made to emit selectively into a single valley. The emitted photons thereby acquire a well-defined valley character and inherit the associated Berry curvature. By placing the qubit near a domain wall between regions of opposite sublattice detuning, whose interface supports valley-polarized edge modes, emission becomes chiral along the domain wall. This provides a promising route toward implementation of single-photon disorder-robust chiral emission without breaking time-reversal symmetry of the electromagnetic medium in platforms such as circuit QED.

</details>


### [57] [Quantum Annealing: Optimisation, Sampling, and Many-Body Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06857)
*Steven Abel,Andrei Constantin,Luca A. Nutricati*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了量子退火（quantum annealing）的计算范式、硬件平台、算法技术及应用场景，指出其作为受物理启发的启发式方法，在离散优化、采样任务以及非平衡多体量子动力学实验平台方面具有独特价值，并与经典算法和门基量子计算形成互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子退火提供了一种受物理启发的启发式方法，用于探索科学和工程领域中崎岖的能量景观，尽管无法在最坏情况下多项式求解NP难问题，但其在近期量子计算（near-term quantum computing）中具有重要的实际意义。

Method: 将优化问题映射到相互作用量子系统的能量景观上，通过连续变换初始哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）使其基态编码目标解；系统借助量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）、隧穿过程（tunnelling）和耗散动力学（dissipative dynamics）穿越复杂景观。

Result: 现代量子退火器实现了包含数千量子比特（qubits）的可编程自旋系统，是当前规模最大的可控量子设备之一；其计算性能受隧穿效应、能隙（spectral gaps）和开放系统效应（open-system effects）的影响。

Conclusion: 量子退火在优化、机器学习、量子模拟和多体物理等领域有广泛应用，其作为优化、随机采样和可编程量子动力学之间的独特框架，与经典算法和门基量子计算（gate-based quantum computing）形成互补角色。

Abstract: Quantum annealing is a computational paradigm in which optimisation problems are mapped onto the energy landscape of an interacting quantum system and explored through its dynamical evolution. By continuously transforming a simple initial Hamiltonian into one whose ground state encodes the solution, the system traverses a complex landscape via a combination of quantum fluctuations, tunnelling processes, and dissipative dynamics. Unlike gate-based quantum computing, quantum annealing is a specialised and near-term approach aimed primarily at discrete optimisation and sampling tasks. While it is not expected to provide polynomial-time solutions to NP-hard problems in the worst case, it offers a physically motivated heuristic for navigating rugged energy landscapes that arise across science and engineering. Modern quantum annealers realise programmable spin systems with thousands of qubits, placing them among the largest controllable quantum devices currently available. As a result, their significance extends beyond optimisation: they also function as experimental platforms for studying non-equilibrium many-body quantum dynamics in regimes that are difficult to access using classical simulation. In this review we present an accessible introduction to the principles of quantum annealing, describe the main hardware platforms and algorithmic techniques, and analyse how tunnelling, spectral gaps, and open-system effects shape computational performance. We survey applications ranging from optimisation and machine learning to quantum simulation and many-body physics, and discuss the central challenges in benchmarking, scaling, and control. These perspectives position quantum annealing as a distinctive framework at the interface of optimisation, stochastic sampling, and programmable quantum dynamics, with a role that is complementary to both classical algorithms and gate-based quantum computing.

</details>


### [58] [Breaking QAOA's Fixed Target Hamiltonian Barrier: A Fully Connected Quantum Boltzmann Machine via Bilevel Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07473)
*Jun Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于双层优化架构的全连接量子玻尔兹曼机（fully connected QBM），通过将量子近似优化算法（QAOA）电路扩展为内层正相能量最小化与外层负相对比散度学习，在单层电路（p=1）下即可实现高概率目标量子态测量，并在噪声环境中展现出显著鲁棒性，同时在小样本（10次测量 shot）条件下仍能稳定生成量子比特网格图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典部分连接玻尔兹曼机与主流量子玻尔兹曼机（quantum Boltzmann machine, QBM）均存在局限性，前者受限于连接结构，后者受限于噪声与训练效率，因此需要一种兼具全连接能力与噪声鲁棒性的新型量子玻尔兹曼机架构。

Method: 将经典量子近似优化算法（quantum approximate optimization algorithm, QAOA）电路扩展为双层优化架构：内层训练模拟正相（positive phase）能量最小化，基于传统QAOA电路的计算过程；外层训练通过优化目标哈密顿量的结构参数，模拟负相（negative phase）对比散度学习（contrastive divergence learning）。

Result: 第一，仅使用单层（p=1）QAOA电路，在无噪声条件下测量目标量子态的平均概率达0.9559。第二，在主流商用量子计算设备的典型噪声水平下，平均概率为0.6047；当噪声强度加倍时，仍维持在0.3859，且目标量子态的测量概率在所有检测态中始终最高，为第二高状态的数倍。第三，在p=1、仅10次测量 shot的逐块学习策略下，模型无论有无噪声干扰均能稳定生成目标量子比特（qubit）网格图像。

Conclusion: 所提全连接QBM在极简电路深度下即可实现高性能，且对噪声具有强鲁棒性，即使在超出当前主流商用量子设备噪声上限的条件下仍能保持最高测量概率，并在图像生成任务中表现出稳定的小样本生成能力。

Abstract: To overcome the limitations of classical partially connected Boltzmann machines and mainstream quantum Boltzmann machines (QBMs), this work extends the conventional circuit of the quantum approximate optimization algorithm (QAOA) to a bilevel optimization architecture and proposes a fully connected QBM. The inner-loop training simulates positive phase energy minimization based on the computational process of the conventional QAOA circuit, whereas the outer-loop training simulates negative phase contrastive divergence learning by optimizing the structural parameters of the target Hamiltonian. It is found that, first, the model exhibits superior performance using only a single layer (p=1) in the QAOA circuit, with an average probability of 0.9559 in measuring the target quantum state under noiseless conditions. Second, the model exhibits notable noise robustness. Under the typical noise level of current mainstream commercial quantum computing devices, the average probability of measuring the target quantum state reaches 0.6047; when the noise rises to a more stringent level with doubled intensity, this probability remains at 0.3859. In both scenarios, the target quantum state maintains the highest measurement probability among all detected states, with a value several times higher than that of the second-ranked state. This indicates that the model retains strong robustness even when noise meets or exceeds the upper limit of current mainstream commercial quantum computing devices. Third, under a block-by-block learning strategy with p=1 and only 10 measurement shots, the model consistently generates the target "qubit" grid image regardless of noise interference, demonstrating strong robustness in image generation.

</details>


### [59] [svPITE: A Python package for the state-vector-based probabilistic imaginary-time evolution algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07559)
*Pascal Sievers,Satoshi Ejima*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于概率虚时演化（probabilistic imaginary-time evolution）算法，实现状态向量（state-vector）版本的基态制备模拟，同时提供标准射弹（shot-based）模拟支持。通过专用封装（wrapper）与精确对角化进行基准比较，并利用与其他软件包的强互操作性实现后续动力学计算。

Result: 该软件包能够高效地调优初始参数，有助于系统性地探索和优化算法性能。从制备好的基态出发，可进一步执行实时演化（real-time evolution）并计算谱函数，例如自旋-自旋动力学结构因子（spin-spin dynamical structure factor）。

Conclusion: 该Python软件包为基于概率虚时演化（probabilistic imaginary-time evolution）的基态制备提供了一种灵活、可验证的计算工具，兼具状态向量与射弹模拟能力，并通过互操作性扩展至动力学性质的模拟，具有较好的实用性和可扩展性。

Abstract: We present a Python package for ground-state preparation based on the probabilistic imaginary-time evolution algorithm, with particular focus on its state-vector-based implementation. A standard shot-based simulation is also supported, and results can be benchmarked against exact diagonalisation via a dedicated wrapper. The package enables efficient tuning of initial parameters, facilitating systematic exploration and optimisation of the method's performance. Starting from the prepared ground state, the strong interoperability with other packages further enables real-time evolution and the computation of spectral functions, such as the spin-spin dynamical structure factor.

</details>


### [60] [Typical Mixing and Rare-State Bottlenecks in Open Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07619)
*Caisheng Cheng,Ruicheng Bao*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在开放量子系统中，无结构系综的非线性迹距离（trace distance）弛豫曲线会集中于其确定性的平均值附近，从而将典型性（typicality）从标准物理可观测量推广到非可观测的动力学量——混合时间（mixing time），并揭示典型混合时间与最坏情况基准之间的分离由稀有态瓶颈定律（rare-state bottleneck law）控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放量子系统中混合时间（mixing time）通常用单一的最坏情况时间（worst-case time）来刻画，但该基准可能由指数稀少（exponentially rare）的初始态主导。这种单一时标描述掩盖了典型行为与极端行为之间的巨大差异，因此需要更精细的统计分析来理解典型混合时间及其与最坏情况的关系。

Method: 通过对无结构系综（unstructured ensembles）的分析，证明非线性迹距离弛豫曲线在确定性平均值附近集中。利用Haar随机纯态（Haar-random pure states）得到固定时间迹距离的瞬时集中（vertical concentration），进而通过平均曲线以有限斜率穿过距离阈值的方式，将垂直集中转化为混合时间的水平集中（horizontal concentration）。进一步推导出稀有态瓶颈定律，其分离程度由缓慢左本征算子（slow left eigenoperator）的极值与典型初始态交叠（overlap）的对数比控制。该框架还扩展至精确及近似的幺正2-设计（unitary 2-designs）以及Hilbert-Schmidt/诱导系综（induced ensembles）。

Result: 典型混合时间与最坏情况基准之间的分离呈现出层次结构：在皮肤效应（skin-effect）设置中为对数关系，在边界支撑的多体慢模（boundary-supported many-body slow modes）中为线性关系，而在保护扇区族（protected-sector family）中则为指数关系——该族中一般态快速混合，而稀有态停滞不前。

Conclusion: 该工作将典型性从通常的可观测静态量推广至非可观察的动力学量——混合时间，并揭示了不同物理设置下典型与最坏情况混合时间的普适层次结构，为理解开放量子系统中混合动力学的统计行为提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Mixing in open quantum systems is often summarized by a single worst-case time, even though that benchmark can be set by exponentially rare initial states. We show that for broad unstructured ensembles the nonlinear trace-distance relaxation curve itself concentrates around a deterministic mean. For Haar-random pure states this yields fixed-time concentration of the instantaneous trace distance to the steady state, which we term vertical concentration since typical relaxation curves bundle along the distance axis. Whenever the mean curve crosses the distance threshold with a finite slope, it converts this vertical concentration into a horizontal concentration of the mixing time, extending typicality from standard physical observables to a fundamentally non-observable dynamical quantity. This sharp concentration naturally raises the question of how the typical mixing timescale compares to the worst-case benchmark. We show that in a one-mode tail regime, this separation is controlled by the logarithmic ratio of extremal to typical initial-state overlaps for the slow left eigenoperator. This rare-state bottleneck law yields a hierarchy that is logarithmic in skin-effect settings, linear for boundary-supported many-body slow modes, and exponential in a protected-sector family where generic states mix rapidly while rare states stagnate. The framework also extends beyond Haar to exact and approximate unitary 2-designs and Hilbert-Schmidt/induced ensembles.

</details>


### [61] [Entanglement-informed distributed wavefunction approach to scalable quantum many-body systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07621)
*Adriano Amaricci*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明量子多体态的纠缠结构（entanglement structure）可定义一种自然且最优的分布式表示（distributed representation），用于其数值模拟。通过将哈密顿量应用（Hamiltonian application）转化为局部收缩（local contractions）与通信最优操作，该方法在大系统中实现了近线性扩展，并指出纠缠谱分裂（entanglement spectrum fragmentation）是控制计算成本的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统的数值模拟面临计算复杂度随系统规模指数增长的挑战。现有方法（如Krylov子空间方法）在哈密顿量应用步骤中存在通信瓶颈与扩展性限制，亟需一种基于系统内在结构、不依赖具体方法（method-independent）的统一扩缩方案。

Method: 利用任意纠缠割（entanglement cut）对波函数（wavefunction）进行二分分解（bipartite decomposition），将其分布映射到纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）的分布上。在该表示中，Krylov子空间方法的核心步骤——哈密顿量应用——被简化为局部收缩与通信最优操作（communication-optimal operations）。

Result: 基于不同方法与模型的基准测试表明，对于足够大的系统，该方法呈现出近线性扩展（near-linear scaling）。同时识别出纠缠谱分裂（entanglement spectrum fragmentation）是控制计算成本的关键因素。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了纠缠（entanglement）作为量子多体模拟的一种组织原则（organizing principle），提供了一条统一且不依赖具体方法的扩缩路线。

Abstract: We show that the entanglement structure of quantum many-body states defines a natural and optimal distributed representation for their simulation. An arbitrary entanglement cut induces a bipartite decomposition of the wavefunction, mapping its distribution onto that of the entanglement spectrum. In this representation the Hamiltonian application, the core of Krylov-subspace methods, reduces to local contractions and communication-optimal operations. Using benchmarks from different methods and models, we demonstrate near-linear scaling for sufficiently large systems and identify entanglement spectrum fragmentation as a key factor controlling computational cost. This establishes entanglement as an organizing principle and unified, method-independent, route for scaling up quantum many-body simulations.

</details>


### [62] [Universal Symmetry-Breaking Dynamics at Continuous Phase Transitions: Evidence for a New Dynamical Critical Exponent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07753)
*Tobias Wiener,Laurin Brunner,Markus Heyl*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在连续相变系统中发现了一种此前未知的非平衡普适动力学行为：在对称性破缺淬火后，Ising模型的序参量涨落在不同系统尺寸和淬火强度下呈现出时间塌缩现象，并引入了一个新的动力学临界指数加以解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示和理解物质远离平衡态（far from equilibrium）时的普适动力学（universal dynamics）仍是一个关键挑战。本文旨在发现此前未被认识的、在连续相变（continuous phase transitions）中对称性破缺淬火（symmetry-breaking quench）后涌现的普适行为形式。

Method: 作者通过研究Ising模型（Ising models）在不同维度和淬火强度下的序参量涨落（order-parameter fluctuations），观察其时间演化规律，并引入了一个新的动力学临界指数（dynamical critical exponent）来解释所观测到的单变量标度形式（single-variable scaling form）。

Result: 研究发现，在二维量子、三维和四维经典Ising模型中，序参量涨落表现出显著的时间塌缩（temporal collapse），指示一种涌现的单变量标度形式。但在二维经典和一维量子Ising模型中未观测到该现象，表明该普适区域存在一个较低的临界有效维度（lower critical effective dimension）。

Conclusion: 本文所发现的远离平衡态普适标度行为可能不仅限于Ising模型，而是更广泛地适用于具有非守恒序参量（non-conserved order parameters）的系统，为在理论和当前实验平台上探索普适动力学开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Uncovering and understanding universal dynamics in matter far from equilibrium remains a key challenge. In this work, we identify a so far unrecognized form of universal behavior that emerges after a sudden symmetry-breaking quench at continuous phase transitions. Our key observation is that the order-parameter fluctuations in Ising models exhibit a compelling temporal collapse across a wide range of system sizes and quench strengths, indicative of an emergent single-variable scaling form. This phenomenon can be explained by introducing a so far unknown dynamical critical exponent for the underlying continuous phase transition. We find evidence for a lower critical effective dimension of this universal regime: it is observed in the 2D quantum and 3D and 4D classical Ising models, but not in the 1D quantum or 2D classical cases. Our results suggest that our observed universal far-from-equilibrium scaling may extend beyond the Ising models studied here and could more broadly characterize systems with non-conserved order parameters, opening new avenues for exploring universal dynamics both theoretically and in current experimental platforms.

### [63] [Reducibility of native weighted graphs on Rydberg Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07952)
*J. Kombe,J. D. Pritchard*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了最大独立集（MIS）和最大加权独立集（MWIS）问题在随机单位圆盘图（UDG）实例上的经典可约性。通过先进的核化（kernelisation）技术，系统分析了经典预处理对这类原生优化问题的简化效果：稀疏图可完全约简，而稠密图通常保留有限不可约核；顶点权重会提升可约性，但扩大相互作用距离会抑制约简效率。最终发现，剩余有限核在量子执行时需非原生嵌入且代价高昂，表明直接运行原生实例可能更实用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在界定经典约简失效的问题实例区间，这些区间对测试和基准化近期的量子优化硬件最为关键，从而为量子与经典处理方法的分工提供依据。

Method: 采用最先进的核化（kernelisation）技术，对随机单位圆盘图（unit-disk graph, UDG）的最大独立集（maximum independent set, MIS）和最大加权独立集（maximum weighted independent set, MWIS）实例进行系统的经典预处理，分析不同规模和连接度下图的可约简程度。

Result: 小规模或稀疏实例可完全约简；稠密图即使经过广泛约简仍保留有限不可约核。引入顶点权重会提升可约性，而扩大UDG连接中的相互作用距离会抑制约简效率。剩余有限核在量子执行时需非原生嵌入，带来可观的资源开销。

Conclusion: 对于无法被经典约简消除的有限核，直接运行原生实例比嵌入约简后的核更为实际。

Abstract: We investigate the classical reducibility of random unit-disk graph (UDG) instances of the maximum independent set (MIS) and maximum weighted independent set (MWIS) problems, which can be natively realised in Rydberg atom quantum processors. Using state-of-the-art kernelisation techniques, we systematically probe how far classical preprocessing can simplify such native optimisation problems of varying size and connectivity. While many small or sparse instances can be fully reduced, dense graphs often retain finite irreducible kernels even after extensive reductions. Introducing vertex weights tends to increase reducibility, whereas extending the interaction range in the underlying UDG connectivity suppresses the reduction efficiency. By exploring where classical reductions cease to be effective, we aim to delineate the regime of problem instances that remain computationally demanding - those most relevant for testing and benchmarking near-term quantum optimisation hardware. We find that for the remaining finite kernels, quantum execution would require non-native embeddings with substantial resource overheads, suggesting that directly running native instances may be more practical than embedding a reduced kernel.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将Kronig-Penney模型中的方势阱替换为截断谐振子势，通过解析求解得到该模型的能量色散关系与波函数；将控制方程改写成类似紧束缚近似（tight-binding approximation）的形式，从而推导出隧穿振幅（tunneling amplitude）与谐振子势参数之间的解析表达式。

Result: 得到了截断谐振子势Kronig-Penney模型的能量色散关系与波函数；该模型与传统模型既有重要相似性也存在差异；成功推导了用谐振子势参数表示的隧穿振幅表达式。

Conclusion: 截断谐振子势可替代方势阱用于Kronig-Penney模型并获得解析解；该模型能够自然地与紧束缚近似框架衔接，为隧穿振幅提供基于势参数的解析表达式。

Abstract: The celebrated Kronig-Penney model traditionally has been formulated with square well potentials representing atomic centres. Here, we use a slightly more realistic potential, the truncated harmonic oscillator, in lieu of square well potentials, and solve the model analytically. We derive the energy dispersion and wave functions for this model. This configuration has some important similarities and differences compared to the usual model. In particular, we write the governing equation in a form suggestive of the tight-binding approximation, as can be done for the usual model. In this way, it is straightforward to derive an expression for the tunneling amplitude used in tight-binding in terms of the harmonic oscillator potential parameters.

Abstract: Certain Feynman integrals can be expressed as periods of differential forms on Calabi--Yau manifolds. We provide a mathematical proof of a result of Duhr and Maggio on the modularity of the two-dimensional conformal traintrack integral. Our approach is based on a factorization of the associated Picard-Fuchs system into a tensor product of Gauss hypergeometric systems via a gauge transformation due to Clingher, Doran and Malmendier.

### [66] [Physics-Inspired Probabilistic Computing for Extremely Large-Scale MIMO Detection in Future 6G Wireless Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07884)
*Andrea Grimaldi,Christian Duffee,Eleonora Raimondo,Edoardo Piccolo,Deborah Volpe,Filip B. Maciejewski,Mario Carpentieri,Massimo Chiappini,Pedram Khalili Amiri,Davide Venturelli,Giovanni Finocchio*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出基于伊辛机（Ising machines, IMs）的物理启发式非传统计算方法，用于解决超大规模多输入多输出（XL-MIMO）系统中的信号检测问题。实验表明，在2048×2048天线规模下，概率伊辛机（PIM）和振荡器伊辛机可在100次迭代内实现最优最大似然（ML）检测，而针对M-QAM调制的广义PIM框架（基于d维概率变量p-dits）在256×256规模下以更低复杂度优于或持平最小均方误差（MMSE）工业标准，为6G网络的XL-MIMO检测提供了可扩展的新范式。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用物理启发的非传统计算方法，即基于伊辛机（Ising machines, IMs）的框架。对于二进制调制，使用概率伊辛机（probabilistic IMs, PIMs）和振荡器基伊辛机（oscillator-based IMs）；对于M-QAM调制（最高256-QAM），提出一种广义PIM启发框架，基于d维概率变量（probabilistic dits, p-dits）直接编码QAM符号。

Result: 在2048×2048天线规模下，PIM和振荡器基IM仅需100次迭代即可实现最优ML检测，匹配最优球形译码器（sphere decoder）在可计算规模下的性能，并优于最小均方误差（MMSE）工业标准。对于M-QAM（最高256-QAM），p-dit框架在256×256天线规模下表现出低误比特率（bit-error-rate），以更低的算法复杂度优于或持平MMSE性能。此外，p-dit的交互矩阵与QAM阶数无关，支持自适应MIMO调制。

Conclusion: 基于伊辛机的物理启发式计算方法为未来6G网络中的XL-MIMO检测提供了一种有前景的可扩展范式（scalable paradigm），在超大天线规模下实现高性能与低复杂度的平衡，并支持灵活的调制自适应。

Abstract: Extremely large-scale multiple-input multiple-output (XL-MIMO) architectures are a key enabler of forthcoming 6G wireless communication networks by allowing high data rates through massive spatial multiplexing. Here, we approach these problems with physics-inspired unconventional computing based on Ising machines (IMs). For binary modulation, probabilistic IMs (PIMs) and oscillator-based IMs achieve optimal ML detection with systems up to 2048x2048 antennas with only 100 iterations, matching optimal sphere decoder performance for computationally treatable sizes and outperforming the minimum mean-square error (MMSE) industrial standard. For M-QAM up to 256, a generalized PIM-inspired framework, based on d-dimensional probabilistic variables (p-dits) that directly encode QAM symbols, shows low bit-error-rate across sizes up to 256x256 antennas, outperforming or matching MMSE with reduced algorithmic complexity. Unlike the binary mapping, the p-dit interaction matrix is independent of the QAM order, enabling adaptive MIMO modulation. These results show a promising scalable paradigm for XL MIMO detection in future 6G networks.

### [67] [Droplet Deformation and Emulsion Rheology in Two-Dimensional Odd Stokes Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07754)
*Thomas Appleford,Hugo França,Maziyar Jalaal*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文在奇粘度（odd viscosity）存在的情况下，研究了二维粘性液滴在简单剪切流中的变形问题。通过解析求解奇斯托克斯流（odd Stokes flow）框架下的液滴形状与流场，得到了稀乳液（dilute emulsion）的表观偶数/奇数粘度的闭式表达式。结果表明，只要粘度差异适中，液滴稳态泰勒变形参数（Taylor deformation parameter）的主导阶保持不变，但高阶效应及数值模拟揭示了奇粘度带来的显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典液滴变形理论仅考虑偶数粘度（even viscosity），而在手性流体（chiral fluids）或活性物质等系统中，奇粘度（odd viscosity）这一非耗散粘性项对液滴动力学的影响尚不明确。本文旨在解析奇粘度如何改变二维液滴在剪切流中的变形行为，并阐明其对稀乳液有效流变学（effective rheology）的修正作用。

Method: 在奇斯托克斯流（odd Stokes flow）框架下，推导液滴形状及周围流场的解析解；允许液滴与周围流体在偶数粘度和奇数粘度上均存在差异。采用直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulations）验证高阶效应。得到稀乳液（dilute emulsion）宏观表观偶数粘度和奇数粘度的闭式表达式。

Result: 稳态泰勒变形参数（Taylor deformation parameter）在粘度差异适中的条件下满足 $D_T^\infty = \text{Ca} + \mathcal{O}(\text{Ca}^2)$，即主导阶结果与经典偶数粘性情形一致。但高阶项显示出奇粘度差异对液滴变形的显著影响；数值模拟证实了这一效应。此外，流动仅取决于液滴与介质之间的奇粘度差值，而非各自的绝对值。

Conclusion: 奇粘度（odd viscosity）在主导阶不改变液滴变形，但其高阶效应显著，因此通过精确的液滴变形测量可能探测奇粘性响应。本文结果为理解奇粘度如何修正稀乳液的宏观流变学提供了理论框架，并为基于液滴的手性流体实验测量提供了指导。

Abstract: We study the deformation of a two-dimensional viscous droplet in simple shear in the presence of odd viscosity.
  We derive an analytical solution for the droplet shape and surrounding flow field within the framework of odd Stokes flow, allowing for differences in both even and odd viscosity between the droplet and the surrounding fluid.
  This solution yields closed-form expressions for the macroscopic apparent even and odd viscosities of a dilute emulsion.
  We show that, provided all viscosity differences remain moderate, the steady-state Taylor deformation parameter satisfies
  $D_T^\infty = \text{Ca} + \mathcal{O}(\text{Ca}^2)$
  so that the leading-order droplet deformation is unchanged from the classical (even-viscous) result.
  Nevertheless, pronounced effects emerges beyond leading order, where our direct numerical simulations reveal odd-viscous differences to the droplet deformation.
  In addition, we show that the flow is influenced only by the difference in odd viscosity between the droplet and the medium and not on their individual values.
  Our analysis clarifies how odd viscosity might modify the effective rheology of dilute emulsions and provides a framework for interpreting droplet-based measurements of odd-viscous response.
  Key words: odd viscosity $|$ droplets $|$ emulsions $|$ surface tension $|$ chiral fluids

</details>


### [68] [Elastocapillary morphing of self-encapsulated droplets floating at the oil-air interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07759)
*D. Andrini,D. Riccobelli,L. Gazzera,S. Molteni,P. Metrangolo,P. Ciarletta*

TL;DR: 本文通过实验、建模与模拟相结合的方法，研究了漂浮在油-空气界面上的自封装液滴在蒸发过程中的形貌变化，包括扁平化、起皱和皱缩等形状突变，并建立了基于自由能最小化的轴对称力学框架，生成了预测性的形态相图。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 所建立的框架能够定量预测液滴蒸发过程中的形态演化与应力重分布，揭示了表面张力比、密度比和壁面效应等多参数对形貌转变的关键调控作用。

Abstract: Self-encapsulated droplets floating at an oil--air interface undergo striking shape changes during evaporation, including flattening and localized loss of membrane tension leading to crumpling and wrinkling. Here we combine experiments, modeling and simulations to obtain predictive morphological maps. We perform contact-angle and evaporation experiments on water droplets coated by a hydrophobin protein film and floating in a fluorinated oil, providing reference profiles and volume-loss sequences for quantitative validation. We develop an axisymmetric mechanics framework in which equilibria follow from minimization of a total free energy combining surface energies, membrane strain energy and gravitational potential, subject to volume and contact-line constraints. A quasi-convex tension-relaxation rule accounts for compression-free states and enables coexistence of taut, wrinkled (one principal tension vanishes) and crumpled (both vanish) membrane domains. A finite element algorithm computes quasi-static morphing under volume reduction; key parameters are identified by fitting the reference contact-angle profile and then used without further tuning. The model reproduces the experimentally observed shape evolution and resolves the associated stress redistribution. Systematic parameter scans yield morphological phase diagrams governed by the Bond number, the oil--droplet surface-tension ratio and the density ratio. For buoyant droplets, crumpling relocates between exposed and submerged caps as parameters vary; for heavy droplets, a crossover to circumferential wrinkling along the immersed sidewall emerges. Wall-meniscus variations shift phase boundaries and can suppress bottom crumpling, consistent with wall-affected experiments.

### [69] [LLM-Guided Open Hypothesis Learning from Autonomous Scanning Probe Microscopy Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06839)
*Boris Slautin,Utkarsh Pratiush,Yu Liu,Kamyar Barakati,Sergei Kalinin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种开放假设学习框架（open hypothesis-learning framework），将符号回归（symbolic regression）与大语言模型（large language model, LLM）的物理评估相结合，用于自主扫描探针显微镜（scanning probe microscopy）。该框架能够从稀疏测量数据中自动生成并筛选符合物理规律的候选解析关系，实现了从闭环优化（closed-loop optimization）到开放假设发现（open hypothesis discovery）的转变，使物理定律直接从实验数据中浮现而非预先指定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自主实验工作流大多局限于在固定目标或假设空间中选取测量，无法从实验数据中生成新的物理模型。该研究旨在突破这一局限，建立一个能够自主发现候选物理定律的实验框架。

Method: 该框架包括两个核心组件：符号回归（symbolic regression）从稀疏测量数据中直接生成候选解析关系；基于大语言模型（large language model, LLM）的评估器根据物理合理性（physical plausibility）、标度行为（scaling behavior）和与已知机制的一致性对这些候选表达式进行排序。

Result: 在PZT薄膜铁电畴开关的自主压电力显微镜（piezoresponse force microscopy）实验中，从五个初始测量点（seed measurements）出发，工作流逐步将物理不完整的候选表达式演化为可解释的电压-时间生长规律，该规律与动力学畴壁运动（kinetic domain-wall motion）一致。

Conclusion: 该工作将自主显微镜从闭环优化扩展到开放假设发现，使候选物理定律直接从实验本身浮现而非预先设定。更广泛地，该框架为将符号回归、物理推理与自适应实验整合为分层自主科学工作流（hierarchical autonomous scientific workflows）建立了路径。

Abstract: Autonomous experimentation has transformed microscopy and materials discovery by enabling closed-loop optimization including imaging and spectroscopy tuning, strucutre property relationship discovery, and exploration of combinatorial libraries. However, most current workflows remain limited to selecting measurements within fixed objective or hypothesis spaces, rather than generating new physical models from experimental data. Here, we introduce an open hypothesis-learning framework that combines symbolic regression with large-language-model-based physical evaluation and implement it for autonomous scanning probe microscopy. Symbolic regression generates candidate analytical relationships directly from sparse measurements, while the language-model evaluator ranks these candidates according to physical plausibility, scaling behavior, and consistency with known mechanisms. We demonstrate the approach on autonomous piezoresponse force microscopy measurements of ferroelectric domain switching in a PZT thin film. Starting from five seed measurements, the workflow evolves from physically incomplete candidate expressions toward interpretable voltage-time growth laws consistent with kinetic domain-wall motion. This work extends autonomous microscopy from closed-loop optimization toward open hypothesis discovery, where candidate physical laws emerge from the experiment itself rather than being specified in advance. More broadly, the framework establishes a route for integrating symbolic regression, physical reasoning, and adaptive experimentation into hierarchical autonomous scientific workflows.

</details>

### [71] [Physics Aware Representation Learning on Electronic Charge Density for Materials Property Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07227)
*Kammampati Sai Kumar,Albert Linda,Shubham Kumar Maurya,Somnath Bhowmick*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子电荷密度是决定晶体固体力学与热力学性质的基本量，但由于其高维度（high dimensionality）特性，直接用于快速性质预测仍面临挑战。因此，亟需一种能够从高维电荷密度中高效提取物理有意义特征并实现性质预测的方法。

Method: 首先利用三维卷积自编码器（3D convolutional autoencoder）对高分辨率电荷密度网格（128×128×128）进行无监督降维，压缩至紧凑的隐空间表示（latent representation，16×16×16×16），并保持极小的重构误差。随后，将隐层表示分别输入两种回归模型——Light Gradient Boosting Machine (LightGBM) 和注意力三维卷积神经网络（Attention-based 3D CNN, Att CNN）进行性质预测。此外，将基于组成的描述符（MAGPIE）与电子电荷密度数据结合，进一步提升了模型精度。

Result: 基于约6059种涵盖多种晶体对称性的无机化合物数据集，模型在体积模量K（R²=0.94）、杨氏模量E（R²=0.88）、剪切模量G（R²=0.87）、形成能Eform（R²=0.96）和德拜温度Θ（R²=0.89）上均取得优异的预测性能。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了电子电荷密度作为一种可迁移、具有物理基础的描述符（transferable, physics-grounded descriptor）在材料性质预测中的有效性，其计算资源需求仅为完整DFT计算的约1/25，显著提升了预测效率。

Abstract: The fundamental quantity governing the mechanical and thermodynamic properties of a crystalline solid is its electronic charge density. Yet, its direct use for the rapid prediction of materials properties remains challenging due to its high dimensionality. Here, we present a physics-informed deep learning framework that directly predicts mechanical and thermodynamic properties from the three-dimensional electronic charge density derived from density functional theory (DFT). The proposed approach first utilizes a three-dimensional convolutional autoencoder for unsupervised dimensionality reduction, compressing a high-resolution charge-density grid (128 x 128 x 128) into a compact latent representation (16 x 16 x 16 x 16) while preserving physically meaningful features, as confirmed by negligible reconstruction errors across diverse crystal systems. The compressed latent-space representation of charge density is then used by two different regression models for property prediction: Light Gradient Boosting Machine (LightGBM) and Attention-based 3D Convolutional Neural Networks (Att CNN), and their performance is compared. Combining composition-based descriptors (Material Agnostic Platform for Informatics and Exploration or MAGPIE) with electronic charge density data further improves the model accuracy. Using a dataset of about 6059 inorganic compounds spanning multiple crystal symmetries, the models achieve strong predictive performance for bulk modulus K (R2 = 0.94), Young's modulus E (R2 = 0.88), shear modulus G (R2 = 0.87), formation energy Eform (R2 = 0.96), and Debye temperature Θ (R2 = 0.89). This work establishes electronic charge density as a transferable, physics-grounded descriptor for materials property prediction, requiring ~ 1/25 the computational resources of full-fledged DFT calculations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: PFNet 采用扩散启发的 U-Net（diffusion-inspired U-Net）结构，结合周期性填充（periodic padding）、基于熵的状态条件化（entropy-based state conditioning）以及热力学参数调制（thermodynamic-parameter modulation），以编码边界一致性、瞬时有序状态和自由能景观的变化。

Conclusion: 物理信息算子学习（physics-informed operator learning）能够为相场动力学及更广泛的能量耗散动力系统（energy-dissipative dynamical systems）提供可迁移的替代模型。

Abstract: Phase-field simulations provide mechanistic descriptions of microstructure evolution, but repeated high-fidelity integration over long horizons and broad parameter spaces remains computationally expensive. We present PFNet, a physics-informed neural operator framework that advances microstructural states by learning conditional evolution operators rather than direct correlations. PFNet combines a diffusion-inspired U-Net with periodic padding, entropy-based state conditioning and thermodynamic-parameter modulation to encode boundary consistency, instantaneous ordering state and changes in the free-energy landscape. For Cahn-Hilliard coarsening, PFNet achieves accurate one-step prediction and stable autoregressive rollouts across composition, gradient-energy coefficient, coarsening stage and morphology class, with errors concentrated near diffuse interfaces and topology-changing regions. The same framework extends to a four-channel martensitic-transformation benchmark without martensite-specific redesign. These results indicate that physics-informed operator learning can provide transferable surrogates for phase-field dynamics and broader energy-dissipative dynamical systems.

Adding incremental doses of water to the sample at cryogenic temperatures produces distinct structures governed by the competition between water-surface and water-water interactions. With two water molecules per surface unit cell, water-surface interactions dominate: In line with previous theoretical predictions, adsorbates follow the surface lattice. Above a critical density of four water molecules per unit cell, water-water interactions prevail, and water clusters are formed. ### [74] [Revisiting Ferroelectricity Beyond Polar Space Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07382)
*Yudi Yang,Changming Ke,Shi Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文回顾了分数量子铁电性与离子导体铁电性这两种新兴现象，并利用Berry相位的现代极化理论将其统一解释：绝缘周期晶体中的极化并非单值矢量，而是模极化量子的多值晶格量。非极性晶体可具有非零形式极化（formal polarization），长程离子迁移导致的大极化变化可通过氧化态的拓扑定义自然理解。这些材料最有前景的功能在于创建和调控由形式极化不连续性带来的带电界面与畴壁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统对称性范式将铁电性（ferroelectricity）严格与极性空间群（polar space groups）绑定，但近年来发现的分数量子铁电性（fractional quantum ferroelectricity）与离子导体铁电性（ionic-conductor ferroelectricity）表明可切换极化可在远超该范式允许的丰富形式中出现，亟需一套统一的理论框架加以解释。

Method: 基于Berry相位（Berry phase）的现代极化理论（modern theory of polarization），将极化视为定义在模极化量子（polarization quantum）下的多值晶格量；引入广义Neumann原则（generalized Neumann principle）描述多值形式极化的对称性；利用氧化态（oxidation state）的拓扑定义将离子输运与量子化电荷转移及极化变化联系起来。

Result: 非极性晶体可能具有非零形式极化；连接对称等价结构的绝热路径可在不违反对称性原理的前提下产生极化的量子化变化；分数量子铁电体与离子导体铁电体中由长程离子迁移引起的大极化变化均可通过氧化态的拓扑定义自然解释；讨论了开关路径、边界条件与畴壁动力学在α-In₂Se₃等体系中对非常规极化态物理可及性的影响。

Conclusion: 这些非常规铁电材料最有前景的功能可能不在于传统的体铁电开关（bulk ferroelectric switching），而在于利用形式极化不连续性创建和调控带电界面（charged interfaces）与畴壁（domain walls）。

Abstract: Ferroelectricity, a hallmark of spontaneous inversion-symmetry breaking, has been a central concept in condensed matter physics and functional materials research, yet recent discoveries are revealing that switchable polarization can emerge in forms far richer than allowed by the conventional symmetry-based paradigm. Fractional quantum ferroelectricity and ionic-conductor ferroelectricity challenge the long-standing association of ferroelectricity exclusively with polar space groups. In this Review, we reconcile these emerging phenomena within the Berry-phase modern theory of polarization. We emphasize that polarization in insulating periodic crystals is not a single-valued vector, but a multivalued lattice quantity defined modulo a polarization quantum. Consequently, nonpolar crystals may possess nonzero formal polarization, and adiabatic paths connecting symmetry-equivalent structures can produce quantized changes in polarization without violating symmetry principles. The symmetry of this multivalued formal polarization is governed by a generalized Neumann principle. We further show that the large polarization changes induced by long-range ion migration in both fractional quantum ferroelectrics and ionic-conductor ferroelectrics can be naturally understood through the topological definition of oxidation state, which links ionic transport to quantized charge transfer and polarization change. We discuss the physical accessibility of these unconventional polarization states, highlighting the roles of switching pathways, boundary conditions, and domain-wall dynamics, particularly in systems such as $α$-In$_2$Se$_3$. Finally, we suggest that the most promising functionality of these materials may lie not in conventional bulk ferroelectric switching, but in the creation and control of charged interfaces and domain walls arising from discontinuities in formal polarization.

Abstract: A major challenge in electrochemistry is to decouple the reactive intermediates of a catalytic cycle to optimise their energies independently. Here, we show that an external stimulus, such as a magnetic field, can relax the scaling relationships between intermediates during the OER. Spectroscopic measurements and Density Functional Theory simulations in Ni-Fe oxyhydroxides reveal that applying a magnetic field alters surface chemisorption and injects structural flexibility at the interface. We interpret these observations as a consequence of stimulated changes in the spin-lattice coupling, which allow access to quasi-degenerate oxygenated intermediates that modulate the reaction energy demands. Our findings redefine the scaling limitations as state-projected rather than intrinsic and establish external stimulation as a strategy to navigate multi-state energy landscapes in electrocatalysis and sensing applications.

*Sreehari M S,Ashutosh Krishna Amaram,Raghavan Ranganathan*

TL;DR: 本研究通过密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT）计算和微调MACE机器学习原子间势（Machine Learning Interatomic Potential, MLIP）基础模型，系统比较了单层非晶碳（Monolayer Amorphous Carbon, MAC）与晶态碳衍生物（如原始石墨烯和石墨炔）的析氢反应（Hydrogen Evolution Reaction, HER）催化性能。研究发现MAC具有多样化的局域结构（五、六、七元环），其吉布斯自由能变化（ΔG_H）分布更广，约15%的位点ΔG_H低于+0.25 eV，表明通过优化局域特征（七元环、曲率和波纹高度）可达到与贵金属催化剂竞争的活性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 析氢反应（HER）在二维催化剂上的增强依赖于催化平面中的无序和缺陷配位，而非晶材料因其固有的无序性而具有催化适应性。本研究旨在通过对比单层非晶碳（MAC）与晶态碳衍生物（如石墨烯和石墨炔）的HER性能，探索非晶碳材料的催化潜力及其与贵金属催化剂竞争的可能性。

Method: 采用熔融淬灭（melt-quench）模拟生成单层非晶碳（MAC）；利用密度泛函理论（DFT）计算氢吸附自由能变化（ΔG_H）；对MAC在30种不同局域环境中进行吸附研究，分析核心结构性质随半径的变化；微调MACE机器学习原子间势（MLIP）基础模型以预测整个MAC表面的催化活性。

Result: 晶态碳材料活性位点有限，β-石墨炔的ΔG_H最佳为+0.34 eV；MAC的DFT计算显示ΔG_H分布在-0.02 eV至+1.35 eV之间；微调后的MLIP预测ΔG_H范围扩展至-0.91 eV至+1.70 eV，约15%位点ΔG_H低于+0.25 eV；特征分析表明七元环、曲率和波纹高度有助于增强HER活性。

Conclusion: 通过精细优化局域特征（如七元环、曲率和波纹高度），单层非晶碳（MAC）可被调控至与贵金属催化剂相竞争的HER催化活性水平。

Abstract: Disorder and defective coordination in the catalytic plane are crucial for enhancing the Hydrogen Evolution Reaction (HER) on two-dimensional catalysts. Amorphous materials are disordered, making them catalytically adaptive for many reactions. In this work, the HER capabilities of Monolayer Amorphous Carbon (MAC) were studied in comparison with crystalline carbon derivatives, such as pristine graphene (GE) and graphyne derivatives. MAC generated from melt-quench simulations revealed a diverse framework of predominantly sp2 and sp3 carbons with numerous 5-, 6-, and 7-membered rings. Density Functional Theory (DFT) calculations investigated free-energy variations in hydrogen adsorption for each material. According to Sabatier's principle, optimum activity is achieved when the Gibbs free energy (Delta GH) change approaches zero. Crystalline carbon materials possess limited active sites, with beta-graphyne showing the best Delta GH value of +0.34 eV. The adsorption study for MAC was conducted in 30 distinct local environments, where core structural properties were analyzed against varying radii. Calculations showed a Delta GH distribution for MAC ranging from -0.02 eV to +1.35 eV. To evaluate activity across the entire MAC surface, a MACE MLIP foundation model was finetuned, achieving optimal energy and force fitting of 1.67 meV/atom and 29.15 meV/A, respectively. The MLIP predicted Delta GH values from -0.91 eV to +1.70 eV, with approximately 15% of sites exhibiting values below +0.25 eV. Feature analysis revealed that 7-membered rings, curvature, and ripple height enhance HER activity. Our findings suggest that, with careful optimization of local features, MAC can be tuned to compete with noble metal catalysts.

### [79] [Selectivity- and Activity-Aware Catalyst Descriptors for CO$_2$ Hydrogenation on Alloy Nanocatalysts using Machine-Learned Force Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07714)

Method: 首先，利用基于Open Catalyst Project数据训练的通用机器学习力场（machine-learned force fields），计算226种金属、二元及三元合金在2,626个不同晶体表面上的约140万个吸附位点的吸附能。然后，采用统计与无监督学习技术（statistical and unsupervised learning techniques）分析分晶面AED，识别高活性和高甲醇选择性的晶面。

However, previous approaches have not sufficiently resolved facet-specific contributions, despite the catalytic significance and prevalence of certain Miller planes in nanoscale catalysts, limiting their applicability in predicting activity and selectivity. Here, we introduce an updated facet-resolved framework for predicting catalytic activity, which also enables insight into selectivity toward C1 products. Using statistical and unsupervised learning techniques, we analyzed facet-specific AEDs to identify highly active and methanol-selective facets. Our approach provides insight into the relationship between structure and catalytic performance metrics like activity and selectivity, and presents a set of alloy compositions and their respective surface orientations for experimental validation toward highly selective CO$_2$ hydrogenation.

### [80] [Exploring the Potential of Ternary Blending for Two and Three-Junction RAINBOW Solar Cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07718)
*Francesc Xavier Capella-Guardià,Jolanda Simone Muüller,Muhammad Ahsan Saeed,Xabier Rodríguez-Martínez,Miquel Casademont-Viñas,Albert Harillo-Baños,Jaime Martín,Jenny Nelson,Alejandro R. Goñi,Mariano Campoy-Quiles*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文探索了一种名为RAINBOW的光谱分裂几何结构在有机光伏（organic photovoltaics, OPV）中的应用。该结构将子电池并排放置并外部连接，避免了叠层结构中的制备和电流匹配难题。通过实验制备和器件模拟，2结和3结RAINBOW器件效率分别达到15.9%和17.3%，验证了该架构在可规模化、高效率OPV中的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有机光伏（OPV）效率在过去十年稳步提升并达到20%里程碑，但多结架构（multijunction architectures）被认为是进一步提升性能的潜在途径。然而，传统的垂直堆叠（vertically stacked）多结结构面临制备复杂和电流匹配（current matching）困难，因此需要探索更简便可行的多结方案。

Method: 采用RAINBOW光谱分裂几何结构，将子电池并排放置并由外部连接。首先测试了7种能隙范围从1.98 eV到1.16 eV的二元体系（binaries），再评估5种三元混合体系（ternaries）以克服宽窄能隙体系的损耗。通过器件模拟（device simulations）识别最佳2结和3结配置，并使用弯月面引导刮涂（meniscus-guided blade coating）等可规模化方法制备了概念验证器件。

Result: 单结器件效率为12.9%，2结RAINBOW器件效率提升至15.9%（模拟值为16.4%），3结器件达到17.3%（模拟值为17.7%）。三元混合能够调控开路电压（Voc），在形态和能级匹配良好的情况下提升特定光谱区域的功率转换效率（PCE），例如PTB7-Th:COTIC-4F:BTP-eC9作为红色子电池时的表现。详细平衡分析（detailed balance analysis）表明该几何结构的潜力很大，但需要高效率的宽能隙（2–2.5 eV）材料。

Conclusion: RAINBOW架构可有效规避垂直堆叠多结OPV中的制备和电流匹配挑战，通过三元混合优化子电池性能，结合可规模化刮涂工艺，成功实现了从单结到多结器件的效率提升。研究证实了该架构用于可规模化、高效率有机光伏的可行性，并指出了宽能隙材料开发对未来性能突破的关键作用。

Abstract: The efficiency of organic photovoltaics (OPV) has been steadily increasing over the past decade until reaching the 20\% milestone. Multijunction architectures provide a promising approach to further enhance performance. Here we explore the potential of a spectral splitting geometry, referred to as RAINBOW, in which subcells are placed side-by-side and externally connected, thus minimizing the fabrication and current matching challenges found in vertically stacked configurations. First, we tested 7 different binaries with bandgaps spanning from 1.98 to 1.16 eV. The systems with the widest and narrowest gaps suffered greater losses and so we evaluate if ternary mixing could help to overcome these limitations by evaluating 5 different ternaries. Generally speaking, ternary mixing tunes the Voc, and when morphology and energy levels are well aligned, the overall PCE can be boosted in the spectral region where the subcell should absorb, as is the case for PTB7-Th:COTIC-4F:BTP-eC9 when operating as red subcell. Device simulations help to identify the 2-junction and 3-junction configurations with highest PCEs, all of which include ternaries. We fabricate proof-of-concept RAINBOW devices using scalable methods in which the subcells are deposited by meniscus-guided blade coating. The efficiency improves from 12.9\% in single-junction devices to 15.9\% in 2-junction devices (16.4\% in simulations) and 17.3\% in 3-junction devices (17.7\% in simulations), confirming the viability of the RAINBOW architecture for scalable, high-efficiency OPVs. Finally, detailed balance analysis indicates that the potential of this geometry can be very high provided that high efficiency wide bandgap (2-2.5eV) materials become available.

Abstract: Magnetic kagome metals provide a fertile platform for exploring unusual magnetotransport phenomena arising from the intricate interplay between electronic topology, electron correlations, and magnetic order. Here, we report a combined study of single-crystal neutron diffraction (SCND) and magnetotransport properties of MgMn6Sn6, supported by first-principles calculations. At low temperatures, the anomalous Hall conductivity develops a pronounced anisotropic extrinsic component, highlighting the directional sensitivity of scattering processes. The significantly large value of the Sommerfeld coefficient, in the absence of f-electrons, underscores enhanced electron correlation. Therefore, the non-collinear kagome ferromagnet MgMn6Sn6 is a promising candidate for studying the effects of electron correlation on magnetotransport properties.

Here, by utilizing time-domain THz emission spectroscopy we directly probe charge carrier dynamics in monolayer WS2 on gold (Au) and fused silica (SiO2) as a function of interface morphology. For laser excitation above the band gap of WS2, we independently extract effective transport times for both electrons and holes and find that discontinuous WS2 contacts on rough Au generate larger net photocurrents than uniform, strongly coupled interfaces - a counterintuitive observation attributed to imbalanced electron and hole transfer from WS2 to Au. Crucially, we demonstrate that ultrafast charge extraction and separation suppress recombination-driven energy release and thereby prevent photo-induced degradation under ambient conditions, eliminating the need for encapsulation. *Han Yang,Xixian Liu,Chenxi Hu,Yichi Zhou,Yu Shi,Chang Liu,Junfu Tan,Jielan Li,Guanzhi Li,Qian Wang,Yu Zhu,Zekun Chen,Shuizhou Chen,Fabian Thiemann,Claudio Zeni,Matthew Horton,Robert Pinsler,Andrew Fowler,Daniel Zügner,Tian Xie,Lixin Sun,Yicheng Chen,Lingyu Kong,Yeqi Bai,Deniz Gunceler,Frank Noé,Hongxia Hao,Ziheng Lu*
