TL;DR: 本文提出 MatterSim-MT，一个基于多任务学习的材料模拟基础模型（foundation model），通过在超过 3500 万个第一性原理（first-principles）标记结构上进行预训练，并针对多种材料性质（如 Bader 电荷、磁矩等）进行微调，实现了对材料结构、动力学和热力学的高精度预测，并通过多任务架构支持复杂模拟（如压电分裂、电滞回线、氧化还原转变）。实验表明该模型具有良好的可扩展性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料设计中性质表征是主要瓶颈；现有第一性原理方法和专用机器学习模型在可扩展性和泛化性方面存在根本性局限，无法覆盖真实材料设计中巨大的结构和性质空间。

Method: 构建多任务基础模型 MatterSim-MT，在超过 3500 万个覆盖 89 种元素、温度高达 5000 K、压力高达 1000 GPa 的第一性原理标记结构上预训练，随后针对 Bader 电荷（Bader charges）、磁矩（magnetic moments）、Born 有效电荷（Born effective charges）和介电矩阵（dielectric matrices）等多种性质进行微调。

Result: MatterSim-MT 实现了 SiC 中压力依赖的 LO-TO 声子分裂（LO-TO phonon splitting）与实验高度吻合，成功模拟了铁电 BaTiO₃ 的电滞回线（electric hysteresis）以及富锂正极材料脱锂过程中的阳离子-阴离子氧化还原转变（cationic-to-anionic redox transition）。模型随数据量和参数规模的增加表现出良好的规模化能力。

Conclusion: MatterSim-MT 提供了一条可扩展的精确计算机材料表征（in silico materials characterization）技术路线，能够高效微调到更高理论水平，并通过主动学习（active learning）扩展到新体系。

Abstract: Accurate property characterization is a major bottleneck in materials design. While first-principles methods and task-specific machine-learning models have driven important progress, they remain fundamentally limited in scalability and generalizability across the vast space of structures and properties relevant to real-world materials design. We present MatterSim-MT, a multi-task foundation model for in silico materials simulation and property characterization. The model is pretrained on over 35 million first-principles-labeled structures covering 89 elements, temperatures up to 5000 K and pressures up to 1000 GPa, and is fine-tuned on various properties including Bader charges, magnetic moments, Born effective charges, and dielectric matrices. Out of the box, MatterSim-MT not only serves as a foundation model for predicting material structure, dynamics and thermodynamics, its multi-task architecture also enables a wide range of complex simulations that cannot be captured by potential energy surfaces alone. For example, we demonstrate pressure-dependent LO-TO phonon splitting in SiC with close agreement with experiment, electric hysteresis in ferroelectric BaTiO3, and the cationic-to-anionic redox transition during delithiation of a Li-rich cathode material. Finally, we show that MatterSim-MT scales well with more data and parameters, can be efficiently fine-tuned to higher levels of theory, and can be efficiently extended to new systems via active learning. Overall, we believe this approach provides a scalable route to accurate in silico materials characterization.

</details>


### [85] [Anisotropic Defect Diffusion in Layered CsPbBr$_\mathrm{x}$I$_\mathrm{3-x}$ Perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08055)
*Konrad Wilke,Mike Pols,Titus S. van Erp,Geert Brocks,Shuxia Tao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过反应力场分子动力学模拟，发现混合卤化物钙钛矿中卤素离子（Br/I）的层状有序排列可诱导强烈的各向异性缺陷扩散：沿层方向迁移容易，跨层方向则被显著抑制。这种各向异性的物理机制因缺陷类型而异——Cs缺陷源于方向性晶格应变与八面体倾斜，卤化物缺陷则受应变与局部键合构型的共同调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合卤化物钙钛矿（mixed-halide perovskites）能在提升相稳定性和调控光电性能方面展现出潜力，但其中缺陷的迁移机制及其与卤素有序排列的关系尚不清晰。本研究旨在揭示如何通过Br和I阴离子的层状有序排列来调控缺陷迁移率并改善材料稳定性。

Method: 采用基于反应力场（reactive force field）的大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，对CsPbBrₓI₃₋ₓ钙钛矿中的缺陷行为进行研究。

Result: 层状卤素有序排列导致了强烈的各向异性缺陷扩散（anisotropic defect diffusion）：沿层方向的迁移较为容易，而跨层方向的扩散被强烈抑制。对于Cs缺陷，各向异性源于方向性晶格应变（directional lattice strain）及其关联的八面体倾斜（octahedral tilting）；卤化物迁移则由应变与局部卤素键合构型（preferential local halide bonding configurations）之间的相互作用主导。

Conclusion: 通过层状有序排列引入的各向异性缺陷扩散机制，为控制混合卤化物钙钛矿中的缺陷行为和提高材料稳定性提供了新的调控途径。

Abstract: Mixed-halide perovskites offer a route to enhance phase stability and modify optoelectronic properties. Here, we use large-scale molecular dynamics simulations with a reactive force field to investigate defects in CsPbBr$_\mathrm{x}$I$_\mathrm{3-x}$ perovskites, focusing on how defect mobility can be controlled and the stability of the material may be improved by layered ordering of Br and I anions in layers. Our results show that layered halide ordering induces strongly anisotropic defect diffusion: migration proceeds readily along the layers, whereas diffusion across them is strongly suppressed. For Cs defects, this anisotropy originates from directional lattice strain and the associated octahedral tilting, while halide migration is governed by an interplay between strain and preferential local halide bonding configurations.

</details>

### [86] [When Does Critique Improve AI-Assisted Theoretical Physics? SCALAR: Structured Critic--Actor Loop for Agentic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06772)
*Vasilis Niarchos,Constantinos Papageorgakis,Alexander G. Stapleton,Sokratis Trifinopoulos*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过SCALAR框架（一套基于Actor-Critic-Judge管线的结构化交互系统）研究了大型语言模型（LLM）与智能体（agent）之间不同交互方式对解决量子场论（quantum field theory）和弦论（string theory）问题表现的影响，发现多轮对话整体优于单次尝试，但改进机制和提示策略（prompting strategy）的效果高度依赖于Actor与Critic的配对方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM在研究级物理推理任务中展现出越来越大的潜力，且智能体AI（agentic AI）日趋普及，一个实际问题随之产生：研究者与智能体之间的交互如何影响最终结果？本文旨在系统性地考察这一问题。

Method: 采用SCALAR（Structured Critic--Actor Loop for AI Reasoning）管线，包含三个角色：Actor负责提出解决方案，Critic提供迭代反馈，独立的Judge根据参考答案评估整个对话记录。研究通过变化Actor的角色设定（persona）、Critic的反馈策略以及Actor的模型家族与模型规模（scale）来进行控制实验。

Result: 多轮对话在所有设定下均优于单次尝试；同一模型家族内增大模型规模（如从DeepSeek-R1 8B到70B）可改善部分简单问题的表现，但无法消除最难的瓶颈。Critic反馈策略在非对称Actor-Critic组合（如轻量级Haiku Actor配合更强Sonnet Critic）中影响最显著，建设性反馈能提升平均得分；在同模型家族的对称设定中策略效果较弱，宽松反馈有时更优，而严格和对抗性反馈无益。

Conclusion: SCALAR为评估何种交互结构有助于或阻碍AI驱动的科学发现提供了一个受控的测试平台。交互的改进机制和提示选择的价值强烈依赖于Actor-Critic配对关系。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) show increasing promise on research-level physics reasoning tasks and agentic AI becomes more common, a practical question emerges: How does the interaction between researchers and agents affect the results? We study this using SCALAR (Structured Critic--Actor Loop for AI Reasoning), an Actor--Critic--Judge pipeline applied to quantum field theory and string theory problems. The Actor proposes solutions, the Critic provides iterative feedback, and an independent Judge evaluates the transcript against reference solutions. We vary the Actor persona, the Critic feedback strategy, and the Actor model family and scale. Multi-turn dialogue improves over single-shot attempts throughout, but both the mechanism of improvement and the value of different prompting choices depend strongly on the Actor--Critic pairing. Increasing the scale within one model family (e.g. from the 8B-parameter DeepSeek-R1 variant to DeepSeek-R1 70B) improves some easier-problem behavior, but does not remove the hardest bottleneck we observe. Critic feedback strategy matters most clearly in the asymmetric Actor--Critic setting (e.g., a lightweight Haiku Actor guided by a stronger Sonnet Critic), where constructive feedback improves mean-score outcomes. In same-family Actor--Critic settings, strategy effects are weaker: lenient feedback is sometimes favored, while strict and adversarial feedback are not beneficial. Taken together, SCALAR provides a controlled testbed for evaluating which interaction structures help or hinder AI-driven scientific discovery.

</details>


### [87] [XDecomposer: Learning Prior-Free Set Decomposition for Multiphase X-ray Diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05866)
*Hanyu Gao,Bin Cao,Yunyue Su,Tong-Yi Zhang,Qiang Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: XDecomposer 是一个无需先验信息的框架，用于多相粉末X射线衍射图谱的联合分解与结构识别；它将多相分析建模为集合预测问题，通过相位查询驱动分解与衍射一致性重建，在模拟和实验数据集上均实现了显著优于现有方法的分解精度与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实合成过程常产生复杂混合物，其组成相（component phase）难以可靠解离；尽管基于表征的晶体检索与生成方法取得进展，但现有方法大多假设单相输入，在多相场景下失效。

Method: 将多相衍射分析形式化为集合预测（set prediction）问题，在统一架构中推断各相的无序集合、混合比例及对应结构表示；采用相位查询驱动分解机制（phase-query-driven decomposition mechanism）结合衍射一致性物理重建（diffraction-consistent physical reconstruction）实现源分离。

Result: 在模拟和实验数据集上，XDecomposer 在多种化学体系中显著提升了重建精度与相识别能力，并对未见混合物展现出强泛化性能。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一条面向数据驱动、源解析的多相XRD分析实用路径，降低了对传统先验引导迭代相位匹配（prior-guided iteratively phase matching）方法的长期依赖。

Abstract: Multiphase powder X-ray diffraction (PXRD) analysis remains a fundamental bottleneck in structure identification, as real-world synthesis often produces complex mixtures whose constituent phases (components) cannot be reliably disentangled. While recent advances in representation-based crystal retrieval and generation suggest the possibility of inferring structures directly from PXRD, existing approaches largely assume single-phase inputs and break down in multiphase settings. Here, we present XDecomposer, a prior-free framework for joint decomposition and identification of multiphase XRD patterns without requiring candidate phase lists, structural templates, or prior knowledge of phase number. We formulate multiphase diffraction analysis as a set prediction problem, where the model infers an unordered set of phase-resolved components, their mixture proportions, and corresponding structural representations within a unified architecture. A phase-query-driven decomposition mechanism, together with diffraction-consistent physical reconstruction, enables accurate source separation while preserving crystallographic fidelity. Extensive experiments on both simulated and experimental datasets show that XDecomposer substantially improves reconstruction accuracy and phase identification across diverse chemical systems, while maintaining strong generalization to unseen mixtures. These results provide a practical route toward data-driven, source-resolved multiphase XRD analysis and reduce long-standing dependence on prior-guided iteratively phase matching. The code is openly available at https://github.com/Licht0812/XDecomposer

</details>

### [88] [A Hardware-aware Hopfield Network with a Nonlinear Memristor Array for Robust Associative Memory with Superlinear Capacity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07223)
*Younghyun Lee,Hakseung Rhee,Unhyeon Kang,Seungmin Oh,Kyungmin Lee,Hyun Jae Jang,Seongsik Park,YeonJoo Jeong,Inho Kim,Jong Keuk Park,Kyung Min Kim,Suyoun Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一种硬件感知型Hopfield网络（hardware-aware Hopfield network, HHN），利用电荷陷阱忆阻器（charge-trap memristor）的非线性电流-电压特性，在无需增大网络规模的前提下提升记忆容量。实验表明，HHN的记忆容量远超经典Hopfield网络的极限（K~0.14N），并在高维图像数据上达到K~0.3×N^1.2的标度关系，同时保持能量最小化动力学和对噪声的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Hopfield网络（CHN）作为联想记忆的经典框架，记忆容量有限；现代Hopfield网络（MHN）虽通过softmax激活函数和显式模式存储提升了容量，但对噪声敏感且硬件实现因网络规模随存储模式数增大而复杂。因而需要一种兼顾高容量、硬件可扩展且对噪声鲁棒的联想记忆架构。

Method: 引入硬件感知型Hopfield网络（HHN），利用电荷陷阱忆阻器的非线性电流-电压特性来工程化调控能量景观（energy landscape），从而在不增加额外神经元或显式模式存储的前提下提高记忆容量。采用25×25非线性忆阻器阵列进行实验验证，并结合大规模高维图像数据仿真分析。

Result: 实验表明，HHN能以远超经典极限（K~0.14N）的容量可靠重建受损模式。大规模仿真显示，在固定突触预算下，记忆容量经验标度关系为K~0.3×N^1.2。HHN保留了Hopfield型能量最小化动力学，并对突触电导噪声保持鲁棒。

Conclusion: HHN作为一种可扩展的硬件原生架构，为低功耗联想记忆和生成式推理（generative inference）提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Associative memory retrieves complete patterns from partial or corrupted inputs and constitutes a primitive form of generative inference. Classical Hopfield networks (CHN) provide a canonical framework for associative memory but suffer from limited memory capacity. Recently, modern Hopfield networks (MHN) were introduced to achieve higher capacity by using explicit pattern-wise storage and neurons with the softmax activation function, which makes the MHN vulnerable to noise and the hardware implementation complicated due to its network size varying with the number of stored patterns. Here, we introduce a hardware-aware Hopfield network (HHN), in which the intrinsic nonlinear current-voltage characteristics of a charge-trap memristor are leveraged to engineer the energy landscape of the HN, increasing the memory capacity. Using a 25 x 25 nonlinear memristor array, we demonstrate reliable reconstruction of corrupted patterns with memory capacity far exceeding the classical limit (K ~ 0.14N, where N is the number of neurons). The HHN preserves Hopfield-type energy-minimization dynamics and remains robust to synaptic conductance noise. Large-scale simulations on high-dimensional image data reveal an empirical memory capacity scaling of K ~ 0.3 x N^1.2 under a fixed synaptic budget. These results establish HHN as a scalable hardware-native architecture for low-power associative memory and generative inference.

### [89] [Spectral Dynamics in Deep Networks: Feature Learning, Outlier Escape, and Learning Rate Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07870)
*Clarissa Lauditi,Cengiz Pehlevan,Blake Bordelon*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种双层次动态平均场理论（two-level dynamical mean-field theory），用于分析宽神经网络中隐层权重谱的演化，揭示了尖峰（outlier）和体（bulk）谱在随机梯度下降训练下的动态行为，并指出了不同参数化方案（如μP与NTK参数化）对超参数迁移（hyperparameter transfer）和边缘稳定性（edge of stability）的影响差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解宽神经网络在（随机）梯度下降训练过程中隐层权重谱的演化规律，特别是尖峰（outlier）与体（bulk）谱成分之间的相互依赖关系，并探究不同参数化方案（如μP与NTK参数化）对谱动力学的影响。

Method: 建立了一种双层次动态平均场理论（two-level dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT），能够联合跟踪尖峰系综（spiked ensemble）中体谱和离群谱的动力学；将该框架应用于两种设定：（1）平均场/μP标度下的无限宽非线性网络；（2）比例高维极限下的深度线性网络。

Result: 理论预测了离群值如何随训练时间、宽度、输出标度和初始化方差演化。在深度线性网络中，μP参数化产生宽度一致的离群动力学（width-consistent outlier dynamics）和超参数迁移（hyperparameter transfer），包括主NTK模式向边缘稳定性（edge of stability, EoS）的宽度稳定增长。NTK参数化则表现出强烈的宽度依赖性。输出通道少时该体+离群图像适用，但输出通道多时（如ImageNet分类或GPT语言建模）更适合用谱体重构来描述。

Conclusion: 不同参数化方案对谱动力学行为有显著影响，μP参数化在宽度一致性和超参数迁移方面优于NTK参数化；体+离群的谱分解框架在输出通道较少的简单任务中有效，而大规模输出任务中谱体本身发生重构；对于足够宽的网络，谱边缘仍收敛。

Abstract: We study the evolution of hidden-weight spectra in wide neural networks trained by (stochastic) gradient descent. We develop a two-level dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) that jointly tracks bulk and outlier spectral dynamics for spiked ensembles whose spike directions remain statistically dependent on the random bulk. We apply this framework to two settings: (1) infinite-width nonlinear networks in mean-field/$μ$P scaling and (2) deep linear networks in the proportional high-dimensional limit, where width, input dimension, and sample size diverge with fixed ratios. Our theory predicts how outliers evolve with training time, width, output scale, and initialization variance. In deep linear networks, $μ$P yields width-consistent outlier dynamics and hyperparameter transfer, including width-stable growth of the leading NTK mode toward the edge of stability (EoS). In contrast, NTK parameterization exhibits strongly width-dependent outlier dynamics, despite converging to a stable large-width limit. We show that this bulk+outlier picture is descriptive of simple tasks with small output channels, but that tasks involving large numbers of outputs (ImageNet classification or GPT language modeling) are better described by a restructuring of the spectral bulk. We develop a toy model with extensive output channels that recapitulates this phenomenon and show that edge of the spectrum still converges for sufficiently wide networks.

</details>

### [90] [Fragility of Unidirectional Transport in Weakly Disordered Photonic Chern Insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07092)
*Xiaoxuan Shi,Tiantao Qu,Xianbin Wu,Mudi Wang,Lei Zhang,Jun Chen*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文揭示了光子陈绝缘体（photonic Chern insulator）中弱无序（weak disorder）通过形成拓扑平庸杂质带（topologically trivial impurity band）破坏手性边缘态（chiral edge state）单向传播的新机制，尽管全局拓扑不变量（global topological invariant）保持不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弱无序如何影响拓扑手性边缘态（topological chiral edge state）的鲁棒传播，在已有理论中尚未被充分理解，而这一理解对实际光子集成器件（photonic integrated circuits）的稳健性至关重要。

Method: 在磁性光子晶体（magnetic photonic crystal）中以少量非磁化杂质（nonmagnetized impurity）随机替换磁化柱（magnetized rod），通过数值实验研究弱无序对拓扑边缘态传播行为的影响。

Result: 当激发频率接近单个杂质缺陷态频率时，空间延展的缺陷态之间形成弱耦合，在拓扑带隙（topological gap）内生成一条拓扑平庸的杂质带（impurity band），使杂质态与手性边缘态共存并耦合；耦合缺陷态形成的互易性“项链态”（necklace state）输运通道打破了预期的单向传播特性。

Conclusion: 拓扑手性边缘态与无序之间的相互作用比以往认知更为复杂；该发现为实际应用中的拓扑输运（topological transport）稳定性与控制提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Photonic Chern insulators enable unidirectional light transport protected by nontrivial band topology -- essential for robust photonic integrated circuits and error-free communication. However, disorder from impurities or defects inevitably exists in practical applications, yet how weak disorder affects topological chiral edge states remains insufficiently understood. Here, we reveal a previously unrecognized mechanism by which weak disorder can disrupt robust propagation of chiral edge states in photonic Chern insulators, despite the preservation of global topological invariants. By randomly replacing a small number of magnetized rods with nonmagnetized impurities in a magnetic photonic crystal, we find that when the excitation frequency approaches the single impurity defect state frequency, weak coupling between spatially extended defect states forms a topologically trivial impurity band inside the topological gap. This enables coexistence and coupling of defect states and chiral edge states. The reciprocal "necklace state" transport channels formed by coupled defect states break the expected unidirectional propagation in topological Chern insulators with weak disorder. Our work reveals that topological chiral edge state and disorder interactions are more intricate than previously understood and provides new insights into stability and control of topological transport in realistic applications.

</details>


### [91] [Active Control of Topological Exceptional Points in Non-Hermitian Metasurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07702)
*Parul Sharma,Sobhan Subhra Mishra,Yash Gupta,Brijesh Kumar,Ranjan Singh,Abhishek Kumar,Anshuman Kumar*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过光激发锗（Ge）作为有源介质，在太赫兹（THz）波段实现了非厄米光子体系中奇异点（EP）的动态时间操控，在亚皮秒时间尺度内完成本征模切换和拓扑相位积累，证明了泵浦-探测延迟时间可作为EP拓扑结构的动力学控制参数，开启了超快非厄米光子学的新方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米光子体系（non-Hermitian photonic systems）的有源控制和超快开关是下一代可重构光学技术的关键需求，但目前缺乏在太赫兹波段实现高速动态操控奇异点（EP）的有效方案。

Method: 利用光激发锗（germanium, Ge）作为有源介质，以泵浦-探测延迟时间（pump-probe delay）作为连续调谐参数，在太赫兹波段实现奇异点的动态时间操控；通过超表面结构产生手性模式响应，并结合理论建模与Petermann因子验证。

Result: 实现了亚皮秒级本征模切换（约0.5 ps）和约2 ps内完整的时间分辨奇异点环绕，直接观测到拓扑相位积累；在约1 ps内完成超快本征模切换与拓扑相位演化，交叉偏振调制深度超过99%；实验与理论建模高度吻合，Petermann因子高达约10^3。

Conclusion: 建立了泵浦-探测延迟时间作为奇异点拓扑结构动力学控制参数的新范式，为太赫兹波段的高速开关、高灵敏度探测和可调偏振控制提供了超快非厄米光子学的全新途径。

Abstract: Active control and ultrafast switching of non-Hermitian photonic systems are essential for next-generation reconfigurable optical technologies. Here, we demonstrate dynamic temporal manipulation of EPs in the terahertz (THz) regime using optically excited germanium (Ge) as an active medium. By exploiting pump-probe delay as a continuous tuning parameter, we achieve sub-picosecond eigenmode switching (~0.5 ps) and realize a complete time-resolved EP encirclement within ~2 ps, enabling direct observation of topological phase accumulation. At EP, the metasurface exhibits highly asymmetric transmission for circularly polarized light, characteristic of chiral mode response. Furthermore, we observe ultrafast eigenmode switching and topological phase evolution within ~1 ps, achieving >99% cross-polarization modulation depth. The measured results show strong agreement with theoretical modeling, with a high Petermann factor of approximately 10^3, confirming the effectiveness of the design. Our work establishes pump-probe delay time as a dynamical control parameter for EP topology, introducing a new regime of ultrafast non-Hermitian photonics for high-speed switching, enhanced sensitivity, and tunable polarization control in the THz domain.

</details>


### [92] [Hot biexcitons driven by extreme optical confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08041)
*Xinyi Wang,Kaushik Kudtarkar,Wenjing Wu,Yunjo Jeong,Yuxuan Cosmi Lin,Xiaofeng Qian,Junichiro Kono,Shengxi Huang,Shoufeng Lan*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过将非辐射连续谱束缚态（BIC）集成到光子晶体（PhC）缺陷腔中，形成准三维（q-3D）开放光约束，在能量上不利的二硫化钨（WS2）双层中观测到了四体热双激子（hot biexcitons），并实现了室温下的显著谷极化（valley polarization）和相干性（coherence）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解具有多组分、非孤立和复杂性质的凝聚态物质（如二维材料）需要研究多体相互作用（many-body interactions），但实验观测高阶多体相互作用因高度依赖低阶复合物的丰度而极具挑战。

Method: 将非辐射连续谱束缚态（bound state in the continuum, BIC）集成到光子晶体（photonic crystal, PhC）缺陷腔中，形成准三维（quasi-three-dimensional, q-3D）但开放的光约束，在倒易空间（reciprocal space）和物理空间（physical space）中产生极端受限的光子，高效激发位于间接带隙（indirect bandgap）上方的两体热激子（hot excitons），进而形成压倒性的四体热双激子（hot biexcitons）。

Result: 在能量上不利的二硫化钨（tungsten disulfide, WS2）双层中观测到了四体热双激子，这些热双激子在室温下表现出显著的谷极化（valley polarization）和相干性（coherence），这归因于BIC的拓扑性质（topological nature）及伴随的具有轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）的q-3D约束。

Conclusion: 除了实现室温双激子（room-temperature biexcitons）外，q-3D约束对于高阶相互作用（如三激子（triexcitons））以及许多其他多体现象（包括玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensation））具有潜在价值。

Abstract: A powerful means to understanding condensed matter that possesses a multi-constituent, non-isolated, and complex nature, with a preeminent example being two-dimensional (2D) materials, is studying many-body interactions. However, experimentally observing high-order many-body interactions is a daunting task due to its heavy reliance on the abundance of low-order complexes. Here, we report the observation of four-body hot biexcitons in an energetically unfavorable bilayer of tungsten disulfide (WS2) through creating extreme optical confinement. Specifically, we integrate a non-radiative bound state in the continuum (BIC) into a photonic crystal (PhC) defect cavity, forming a quasi-three-dimensional (q-3D) but open confinement for photons at the driving frequency. The extremely confined photons in both reciprocal and physical spaces then excite inherently unproductive two-body hot excitons situated slightly above the indirect bandgap so efficiently that they form overwhelmed higher-order four-body hot biexcitons. Distinctively, these hot biexcitons exhibit substantial valley polarization and coherence at room temperature, which we attribute to the topological nature of BICs and the associated q-3D confinement with an orbital angular momentum. Besides achieving room-temperature biexcitons, the q-3D confinement could be valuable for higher-order interactions, such as triexcitons, and many other many-body phenomena, including Bose-Einstein condensation.

</details>

### [93] [Towards black-hole horizons and geodesic focusing in causal sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06813)
*Astrid Eichhorn,Pedro Gamito,Nawder Stokes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在因果集量子引力（causal set quantum gravity）框架下，探讨如何在离散时空中识别黑洞视界（event horizon）。首先构造基于离散类时曲线的局域诊断来近似全局事件视界，随后利用“梯子（ladder）”结构追踪零测地线（null geodesics）以识别表观视界（apparent horizon），并通过“模糊梯子（fuzzy ladder）”延长跟踪范围，在1+1维黑洞玩具模型中构建了离散视界的一部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论（General Relativity）中，事件视界是因果结构动态性的最显著体现。而在因果集量子引力中，时空的基本结构由点之间的因果关系构成，因此如何在该离散框架下识别黑洞视界成为一个关键问题。

Method: 首先，基于离散类时曲线（discrete timelike curves）构造一个局域诊断量，以近似全局的“事件视界”。其次，利用“梯子”（ladder）结构作为零测地线的示踪器，探测表观视界，并检验离散版本的膨胀标量（expansion）在黑洞视界两侧的符号变化。最后，引入“模糊梯子”（fuzzy ladder）概念，以在更大的仿射参数（affine parameter）区间内追踪零测地线。

Result: 离散版本的膨胀标量在黑洞视界处改变了符号，符合理论预期。通过模糊梯子，能够在1+1维黑洞玩具模型中成功构建出一部分离散视界。

Conclusion: 在因果集框架下，可以构造出有效的局域诊断来识别离散黑洞视界，借助梯子和模糊梯子结构，表观视界和事件视界的探测均取得了初步成功。

Abstract: The event horizon of a black hole is arguably the most dramatic manifestation of the fact that in General Relativity, causal structure is dynamical and spacetimes can be separated into distinct regions by causal boundaries. Causal set quantum gravity is an approach to quantum gravity in which causal relations between spacetime points constitute the basic structure on which the theory is based. This raises the question how a discrete horizon can be identified in a causal set. In our paper, we first construct a local diagnostic to approximate a global concept, namely the event horizon, based on discrete timelike curves.
  We then turn to the concept of an apparent horizon, which is based on local properties of geodesics, rather than global properties of the entire spacetime. We undertake first steps towards detecting apparent horizons in causal sets, using so-called ladders as tracers of null geodesics. We find that a discrete counterpart of the expansion changes sign across the black-hole horizon, as it should. Finally, we introduce the notion of a fuzzy ladder, which enables us to track null geodesics for larger intervals of the affine parameter. Thereby, we construct a portion of a discrete horizon in a toy-model for a black-hole spacetime in 1+1 dimensions.

</details>


### [94] [Probing Gravitational Wave Signatures from Periodic Orbits of Regular Black Holes in Asymptotically Safe Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07187)
*Arun Kumar,Abolhassan Mohammadi,Sushant G. Ghosh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了渐近安全引力（asymptotically safe gravity）正则黑洞时空中类时测地线的束缚与周期运动及其引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）特征，发现量子参数ξ会显著改变轨道频率谱、增强回转行为，并在极端质量比旋进（EMRI）中产生可探测的振幅调制和相移，其应变谱峰值落在LISA、Taiji、TianQin等空间探测器的灵敏度范围内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索渐近安全引力框架下量子修正对强场黑洞时空几何及动力学可观测效应的影响，特别是通过极端质量比旋进（EMRI）系统中的zoom–whirl轨道动力学来约束量子引力偏离经典广义相对论（general relativity）的可能性。

Method: 推导含量子修正参数ξ的大质量试探粒子有效势，分析稳定圆轨道与束缚轨道条件；利用Levin的zoom–whirl分类法，通过拓扑整数(z,w,v)和有理频率比q=ω_φ/ω_r−1对周期轨道进行分类；在四极矩近似（quadrupole approximation）下计算EMRI的引力波波形。

Result: 量子参数ξ会改变轨道频率谱、增强回转行为并导致与Schwarzschild极限的偏离；随着ξ增大，EMRI信号的振幅调制和相移变得可探测；应变谱峰值位于毫赫兹频段且随ξ单调增大，在LISA、Taiji、TianQin等探测器的灵敏度范围内。

Conclusion: 从EMRI中zoom–whirl动力学的精确测量可以获取强场区域量子引力诱发偏离经典广义相对论的观测约束。

Abstract: We investigate bound and periodic timelike geodesics and their associated gravitational-wave (GW) signatures in the spacetime of a regular black hole arising in asymptotically safe gravity (ASG). The geometry incorporates quantum corrections via a running gravitational coupling, encoded in a dimensional scaling parameter $ξ$, that modifies the near-horizon structure while preserving asymptotic flatness. We derive the effective potential for massive test particles and determine the conditions for stable circular and bound motion as functions of $ξ$, including the shift in the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). The three topological integers $(z,w,v)$, which represent the number of zooms, whirls, and vertices per radial cycle, are used to categorize the test particles' periodic orbits using Levin's zoom -- whirl taxonomy. Moreover, we employ the rational frequency ratio $q = \frac{ω_φ}{ω_r} - 1$ to find closed orbits, where $ω_φ$ and $ω_r$ stand for the azimuthal and radial frequencies, respectively. We examine how the orbital frequency spectrum is altered, whirl behaviour is enhanced, and deviations from the Schwarzschild limit are produced by the quantum parameter $ξ$. The GW forms for extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) are calculated within the quadrupole approximation. We find that as $ξ$ increases, the signals that are released exhibit detectable amplitude modulations and phase shifts. The corresponding typical strain spectra fall within the anticipated sensitivity limits of space-based detectors such as LISA, Taiji, and TianQin, as they peak in the millihertz frequency band. Peak strain increases monotonically with $ξ$, indicating that observational restrictions on quantum-gravity-induced deviations from classical general relativity in the strong-field domain can be obtained from precise measurements of zoom -- whirl dynamics in EMRIs.

</details>


### [95] [Formulation of testing gravitational redshift based on Laser Time link between China Space Station and a ground station](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07216)
*Rui Xu,Wenbin Shen,Hok Sum Fok,Pengfei Zhang,Lihong Li,Lei Wang,Kuangchao Wu,An Ning,Youchao Xie,Ziyu Shen,Lingxuan Wang,Yongqi Zhao,Kai Liu,Yuanjin Pan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用中国空间站（CSS）激光时间传递（CLT）系统，基于c^{-3}阶相对论模型，实现了引力红移验证精度达到(1.8 ± 47)×10^{-7}，相较于此前实验提升约一个数量级，是首次将激光时间传递技术应用于高精度引力红移检验，并开创了CSS CLT链路在广义相对论基础检验中的先例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力红移实验的验证精度有限，且主要依赖微波（microwave）时间传递方法，易受电离层效应（ionospheric effects）和一阶多普勒频移（first-order Doppler shifts）干扰，亟需更高精度的检验手段来推进广义相对论（General Relativity）基础检验以及大地测量应用。

Method: 基于c^{-3}阶相对论模型（relativistic model）建立空间-地面钟比对观测方程，利用中国空间站实际轨道数据进行仿真模拟，采用激光时间传递（CLT）链路替代传统微波方法进行引力红移验证。

Result: 引力红移验证精度为(1.8 ± 47)×10^{-7}，较以往实验提升约一个数量级；可实现引力势差（gravitational potential difference）测量精度达0.1 m²/s²；残差分析（residual analysis）表明，对流层延迟变化（tropospheric delay variations）和大气湍流（atmospheric turbulence）是主要剩余不确定度来源。

Conclusion: 该工作为高精度相对论物理检验建立了新基准，证明星基光学时间传递（space-based optical time transfer）在基础物理和大地测量领域具有变革性潜力，可支持洲际高程传递（intercontinental height transfer）等测地学应用。

Abstract: This paper presents a high-precision gravitational redshift test using the China Space Station (CSS) Laser Time Transfer (CLT) system. We develop a comprehensive observation equation based on a c^{-3} order relativistic model for space-ground clock comparison. While the CSS optical clock system is currently in the orbital debugging phase, our simulation using actual CSS orbit data achieves a gravitational redshift verification precision of (1.8 \pm 47)*10^{-7} -- approximately one order of magnitude improvement over previous experiments. Our work represents the first application of laser-based time transfer for gravitational redshift verification at such precision, and the first use of the CSS CLT link for testing this fundamental aspect of General Relativity. Unlike microwave-based methods, our laser approach avoids ionospheric effects and first-order Doppler shifts. Residual analysis identifies tropospheric delay variations and atmospheric turbulence as the primary remaining uncertainty contributors. The achieved precision enables gravitational potential difference measurements with 0.1 m^2/s^2 precision -- offering new capabilities for both fundamental physics investigations and geodetic applications including intercontinental height transfer. This work establishes a new benchmark for high-precision tests of relativistic physics and demonstrates the transformative potential of space-based optical time transfer.

</details>


### [96] [Traversable wormholes in $\boldsymbol{f(Q)}$ gravity: Energy conditions, stability and quasinormal modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07224)
*Jaydeep Goswami,Rupam Jyoti Borah,Umananda Dev Goswami*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在$f(Q)$引力框架下，通过幂律模型$f(Q)=\gamma(-Q)^m$构造了静态球对称可穿越虫洞解，证明了其在几何一致性、能量条件局域破坏、各向异性应力平衡以及动力学稳定性方面的可行性，并利用六阶WKB方法和时域模拟验证了标量扰动的稳定衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索扩展引力理论（modified gravity）中是否存在满足几何要求且动力学稳定的可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）解，特别是研究$f(Q)$引力对虫洞物质含量和稳定性条件的调控作用。

Method: 采用幂律模型$f(Q)=\gamma(-Q)^m$，假设各向异性物质分布及各向异性状态方程，解析求解形状函数（shape function）；通过广义Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff方程分析平衡配置；对标量扰动导出薛定谔型波动方程，利用六阶WKB方法配合Padé逼近计算准正则模（quasinormal modes），并进行时域模拟验证。

Result: 模型参数约束为$0<m<1/2$，对应精质态（quintessence-like regime）$(-1<\omega<-1/3)$；零能量条件与弱能量条件在虫洞喉部附近不可避免但局域化破坏；各向异性参数在全时空为正，提供主导外向支撑力；准正则模虚部为负，表明扰动稳定衰减；时域模拟与WKB结果吻合良好，仅阻尼率存在微小偏差。

Conclusion: $f(Q)$引力能够支持几何上一致且动力学稳定的可穿越虫洞解，其效应有效调控了所需的物质含量，为虫洞存在性提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We investigate static and spherically symmetric traversable wormhole solutions in the framework of $f(Q)$ gravity by considering a power-law model of the form $f(Q)=γ(-Q)^m$. By adopting an anisotropic matter distribution and imposing an equation of state relating the radial pressure and energy density, we obtain an analytic shape function that satisfies the geometric requirements for a traversable wormhole. The model parameter is constrained to $0<m<1/2$, corresponding to a quintessence-like regime with $-1<ω<-1/3$. The energy conditions are analyzed in detail, showing that violations of the null and weak energy conditions are unavoidable but remain localized near the wormhole throat. The anisotropy parameter is positive throughout the spacetime, indicating that repulsive anisotropic stresses play a key role in sustaining the wormhole. The equilibrium configuration is examined using the generalized Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equation for both zero and logarithmic redshift functions, where a consistent force balance is achieved with anisotropic effects providing the dominant outward support. Dynamical stability is studied through scalar perturbations, leading to a Schrödinger-like wave equation with a single-peak effective potential. The quasinormal modes are computed using the sixth-order WKB method with Padé approximation. The resulting frequencies possess negative imaginary parts, indicating stable damping of perturbations. Time-domain simulations further confirm the stability of the solutions and show good agreement with the WKB results, with small deviations in the damping rates. Thus, these results establish that $f(Q)$ gravity admits traversable wormhole solutions that are geometrically consistent and dynamically stable, with $f(Q)$ gravity effects effectively regulating the required matter content.

</details>


### [97] [Black holes at a finite distance: Quasi-local restricted phase space formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07236)
*Bai-Hao Huang,Liu Zhao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中球对称黑洞的受限相空间（restricted phase space）形式论扩展到准局域（quasi-local）情形的静态观测者情形，证明了仅当引入观测者所在余2维超曲面（codimension-2 hypersurface）的面积与压力作为额外热力学变量时，RN和RN-AdS黑洞的第一定律与欧拉关系（Euler relation）才成立。准局域描述下的RN黑洞与渐近描述下的RN黑洞行为显著不同，但与渐近描述下的RN-AdS黑洞高度相似，例如允许等荷温度-熵相变、缺乏等势温度-熵相变；在零荷极限下还出现类霍金-佩奇（Hawking-Page-like）相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将受限相空间形式论从渐近无穷远观测者推广到有限径向距离处的准局域静态观测者场景，检验并修正黑洞热力学第一定律和欧拉关系在非渐近边界条件下的适用性。

Method: 采用受限相空间形式论（restricted phase space formalism），对爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中的球对称黑洞解在准局域（quasi-local）框架下进行分析，引入静态观测者所在余2维超曲面（codimension-2 hypersurface）的面积与压力作为额外热力学变量对。

Result: 准局域描述下的RN黑洞在热力学相变行为上与渐近描述下的RN-AdS黑洞极为相似：都存在等荷温度-熵相变（isocharge temperature-entropy phase transitions），缺乏等势温度-熵相变（isovoltage temperature-entropy phase transitions）；且在零荷极限（neutral limit）下出现渐近描述中不存在的类霍金-佩奇相变（Hawking-Page-like transitions）。

Conclusion: 只有纳入观测者所在余2维超曲面的面积和压力作为额外的热力学变量对，准局域黑洞热力学的第一定律和欧拉关系才成立；准局域描述揭示了RN黑洞从渐近到准局域描述的特性转变，其行为趋向于类似RN-AdS黑洞在渐近描述中的表现。

Abstract: We extend the restricted phase space formalism for spherically symmetric black hole solutions of Einstein-Maxwell theory to the quasi-local regime, with the static observers located at a finite radial distance. The first law and Euler relation for the RN and RN-AdS black holes are proved to hold, but only with the inclusion of an extra pair of thermodynamic variables, i.e. the pressure and the area of the codimension-2 hypersurface on which the observers reside. For the RN black holes, the quasi-local behavior is analyzed in detail. It turns out that the RN black holes in the quasi-local description behaves significantly different from itself in the asymptotic description, but is extremely similar to the RN-AdS black holes in the asymptotic description, e.g. allowing for isocharge temperature-entropy phase transitions and lack of isovoltage temperature-entropy phase transitions. In the neutral limit, the Hawking-Page-like transitions appear in the quasi-local description which is absent in the asymptotic description.

</details>


### [98] [Scalar memory from compact binary coalescences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07778)
*Jann Zosso,Silvia Gasparotto,Llibert Aresté Saló,Daniela D. Doneva,Stoytcho S. Yazadjiev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在里奇耦合标量-高斯-博内引力（Ricci-coupled scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity）中研究双黑洞并合的引力记忆（gravitational memory）效应，发现并合过程中系统标量荷（scalar charge）的变化会产生显著的标量记忆贡献，其量级可与纯标量-高斯-博内对张量记忆（tensor memory）的修正相当，从而大幅增强对广义相对论预言的总偏离，并指出这是一种普适机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力记忆是引力的一种独特低频探针，但广义相对论之外的并合研究仍然有限，因此有必要在修改引力理论中探索记忆效应的特征。

Method: 基于双黑洞并合的数值相对论（numerical-relativity）波形，分析了里奇耦合标量-高斯-博内引力中系统的标量荷在并合前后的变化及其对标量记忆（scalar-memory）贡献的影响。

Result: 对于GW150914类似系统，标量记忆效应在引力波探测器中可观测的时间尺度上与纯标量-高斯-博内对张量记忆的修正量级相当，且能在广泛源和探测器配置下显著增强与广义相对论预言的总偏离。

Conclusion: 当致密双星并合改变额外引力场的渐近荷（asymptotic charge），且该场源生可观测的额外极化（extra polarization）时，由此产生的记忆可成为新引力物理的领先低频信号；这是一种普遍机制。

Abstract: Gravitational memory provides a distinctive low-frequency probe of gravity, but explicit merger studies beyond general relativity remain limited. In this work, we investigate memory from binary black hole mergers in Ricci-coupled scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity, a natural extension of scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory that admits an additional scalar breathing polarization. Based on numerical-relativity waveforms of binary black hole coalescences, we show that the change in the scalar charge of the system across merger generates a significant scalar-memory contribution. For a GW150914-like system, this effect modifies the memory signal in a gravitational-wave detector on the same observable timescale and by an amount comparable to the pure scalar-Gauss-Bonnet correction to tensor memory. Thus, it can substantially enhance the total deviation from the general-relativity prediction over a broad range of source and detector configurations. We argue that this identifies a general mechanism: whenever a compact-binary merger changes the asymptotic charge of an additional gravitational field, and that field sources an observable extra polarization, the resulting memory can provide a leading low-frequency signature of new gravitational physics.

</details>


### [99] [Fuzzy-novae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07848)
*Francesco Fazzini,Waleed Sherif*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一个受圈量子引力启发的唯象模型，通过基于局域能量密度而非平均能量密度的量子引力修正，实现了完全正则的时空演化，同时解决了中心奇点和壳交叉奇点问题。数值模拟显示，局域量子排斥与引力吸引的相互作用形成了稳定的外向孤立物质波，并由动力学局域反捕获区域支撑。该机制允许恒星质量以类时方式喷出——即“模糊新星”（fuzzy-nova）——标志着宏观黑洞的终结。该工作为信息悖论提供了具体的动力学机制，并开辟了量子引力的现实观测窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子引力坍缩模型通常依赖平均能量密度引入修正，无法同时解决中心奇点（central singularity）和壳交叉奇点（shell-crossing singularities）；此外，黑洞信息悖论（information paradox）缺乏具体的物质逃逸动力学机制。

Method: 基于圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）的启发，构建一个包含局域能量密度量子引力修正的唯象模型（phenomenological model），并通过数值模拟（numerical simulations）分析坍缩动力学。

Result: 模型同时消除了中心奇点和壳交叉奇点；局域量子排斥与引力吸引的相互作用生成稳定的外向孤立物质波，该波由动力学局域反捕获区域（dynamical local anti-trapped region）支撑；恒星物质以类时方式整体喷出，形成“模糊新星”。

Conclusion: 该模型为物质逃逸出捕获区域提供了具体动力学机制，为解决信息悖论奠定了基础，并为量子引力效应开辟了现实可观测的窗口。

Abstract: We propose a novel phenomenological model of quantum gravitational collapse inspired by loop quantum gravity that ensures a completely regular spacetime evolution. By incorporating quantum gravitational modifications based on local rather than average energy density, our model simultaneously resolves both the central singularity and the shell-crossing singularities. Numerical simulations reveal that the interplay between local quantum repulsion and gravitational attraction leads to the formation of a stable, outgoing solitary matter wave, supported by a dynamical local anti-trapped region. This mechanism allows for a time-like ejection of the entire stellar mass -- a \emph{fuzzy-nova} -- which signals the end of macroscopic black holes. By providing a concrete dynamical mechanism for matter to escape the trapped region, our work sets a new stage for resolving the information paradox and opens a realistic observational window into quantum gravity.

</details>


### [100] [Gravitational Wave Memory in Beyond GR Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07879)
*Silvia Gasparotto*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次在标量-高斯-博内引力（scalar Gauss-Bonnet gravity）中，基于完整的旋进-合并-振铃（inspiral-merger-ringdown）波形计算引力波记忆（gravitational-wave memory），发现与广义相对论（GR）的偏差可达百分之几，且记忆效应显著增强了GR与修正引力理论波形之间的不匹配（mismatch），表明记忆可作为下一代探测器检验引力的互补观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波记忆是一种低频非振荡信号，是探测强场引力（strong-field gravity）的重要手段。然而，此前尚未有研究在广义相对论（GR）之外的引力理论中，基于完整的旋进-合并-振铃波形计算记忆效应。

Method: 聚焦于标量-高斯-博内引力（scalar Gauss-Bonnet gravity），首次计算了完整旋进-合并-振铃（inspiral-merger-ringdown）波形中的记忆效应。

Result: 与GR的偏差达到百分之几（percent-level）水平，主要由修正的合并动力学（merger dynamics）驱动；标量场诱导的张量记忆贡献被强烈抑制。包含记忆后，GR与修正引力理论波形之间的不匹配（mismatch）显著增大。

Conclusion: 引力波记忆可作为下一代探测器检验引力的互补观测量（complementary observable），有效增强区分GR与修正引力理论的能力。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave memory is a low-frequency, non-oscillatory signal that provides a promising probe of strong-field gravity. We present the first computation of memory from full inspiral--merger--ringdown waveforms in a theory beyond GR, focusing on scalar Gauss--Bonnet gravity. We find percent-level deviations from GR, mainly driven by modified merger dynamics, while scalar-induced contributions to tensor memory are strongly suppressed. We found that including memory greatly enhances the mismatch between GR and beyond-GR waveforms, highlighting its potential as a complementary observable for tests of gravity with next-generation detectors.

### [101] [Uncertainty Principles and Maximum Entropic Force](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07992)
*Jonas Mureika,Elias C. Vagenas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了多种引力不确定性原理（包括GUP、EUP、GEUP和LQGUP）对最大熵力（entropic force）的量子引力修正，发现修正后的熵力依赖于不确定性原理的无量纲参数以及EUP区域中普朗克面积（Planck area）的数量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究量子引力效应对熵力（entropic force）——一种与全息原理（holographic principle）和黑洞热力学（black hole thermodynamics）相关的概念——可能产生的修正。

Method: 通过考虑四种引力不确定性原理：广义不确定性原理（Generalized Uncertainty Principle, GUP）、扩展不确定性原理（Extended Uncertainty Principle, EUP）、广义扩展不确定性原理（Generalized Extended Uncertainty Principle, GEUP）以及线性-二次型GUP（Linear-Quadratic GUP, LQGUP），计算并比较它们对最大熵力的量子引力修正。

Result: 修正后的熵力依赖于各不确定性原理中的无量纲参数，从而依赖于具体的量子引力理论；此外，在扩展不确定性原理框架下，修正后的熵力还依赖于构成"EUP面积"的普朗克面积数量。

Conclusion: 量子引力修正的熵力可作为区分不同不确定性原理（从而区分不同量子引力理论）的一个潜在判据。

Abstract: We consider quantum gravity corrections to the maximum entropic force that arise from several gravitational uncertainty principles. These include the Generalized Uncertainty Principle (GUP), the Extended Uncertainty Principle (EUP), the Generalized Extended Uncertainty Principle (GEUP), and the Linear-Quadratic GUP (LQGUP). We find that the modified entropic force depends on the dimensionless parameters of the uncertainty principles and, thus, on the underlying quantum gravity theory. Furthermore, the entropic force, which is quantum gravity corrected in the framework of the extended uncertainty principles, also depends on the number of Planck areas that made the ``EUP area".

### [102] [DESI and Dynamical Dark Energy from Extended Pre-geometric Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07344)
*Andrea Addazi,Yermek Aldabergenov,Daulet Berkimbayev,Yifu Cai,Salvatore Capozziello,Giuseppe Meluccio*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了MacDowell-Mansouri前几何引力（pre-geometric gravity）的最简二次扩展，该扩展保持了拓扑前体积形式对称性（topological pre-volume form symmetry）。对称性破缺后，理论变为(Lovelock)²引力，其对偶为类Galileon的Horndeski标量-张量理论。引力Higgs机制使得Gauss-Bonnet耦合常数与裸宇宙学常数成反比。二次修正将引力的θ角动力学化，形成一个引力轴子（gravi-axion），其有效质量设定暗能量尺度，从而自然实现动力学暗能量。该模型与DESI的BAO+FS数据拟合优异（χ²_red = 1.394），在引力滑移参数γ(z)上与ΛCDM仅有百分之几的偏差，且张量扰动稳定。这项工作在前几何引力和宇宙加速之间建立了一座具体、可验证的桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索前几何引力（pre-geometric gravity）与观测宇宙学之间的具体联系，尤其是解释暗能量（dark energy）的起源，并提供一个可被大尺度结构数据检验的理论框架。

Method: 在MacDowell-Mansouri前几何引力的框架下，引入保持拓扑前体积形式对称性的最简二次扩展。通过对称性自发破缺（引力Higgs机制），将理论约化为(Lovelock)²引力及其对偶的Horndeski标量-张量理论。利用理论中的引力轴子（gravi-axion）动力学实现暗能量，并通过DESI BAO+FS数据进行拟合验证。

Result: 该模型与DESI的Baryon Acoustic Oscillations (BAO) and Full Shape (FS)数据的拟合结果优异，约化卡方值（χ²_red）为1.394。在引力滑移参数γ(z)上，模型与ΛCDM仅有百分之几的偏差，且张量扰动保持稳定。

Conclusion: 该工作在前几何引力和宇宙加速膨胀之间建立了具体且可检验的联系，表明该模型可以自然地实现动力学暗能量，并能够与当前的大尺度结构观测数据良好吻合。

Abstract: We consider the simplest quadratic extension of MacDowell-Mansouri pre-geometric gravity preserving the topological pre-volume form symmetry. After symmetry breaking, it becomes $(\mathrm{Lovelock})^2$ gravity, dual to a Galileon-like Horndeski scalar-tensor theory. The gravitational Higgs mechanism forces the Gauss-Bonnet coupling to be inversely proportional to the bare cosmological constant. The quadratic correction renders the gravitational $θ$-angle dynamical in the form of a gravi-axion, whose effective mass sets the dark energy scale, thus naturally realizing a dynamical dark energy. The model fits DESI's BAO+FS data exceptionally well ($χ^2_{\rm red} = 1.394$), deviating from $Λ\mathrm{CDM}$ by only a few percent in the gravitational slip parameter $γ(z)$ with stable tensor perturbations. This analysis establishes a concrete, testable bridge between pre-geometric gravity and cosmic acceleration.

### [103] [Cellular-scale mechanism of cell crawling responding to substrate stiffness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07109)
*Sohei Nakamura,Mitsusuke Tarama*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过构建一个整合细胞内生化反应、细胞形变及基底粘附的机械化-化学（mechanochemical）模型，从理论上研究了趋硬性（durotaxis）中细胞迁移行为对基底刚度（substrate stiffness）的非单调依赖机制，并揭示了记忆效应（memory effect）对持续时间的调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管趋硬性现象已被研究二十余年，但细胞如何感知基底刚度并调控自身运动的基本机制仍不清楚。本文旨在阐明这一细胞尺度的底层机制。

Method: 提出一个机械化-化学理论模型，将细胞内生化反应、细胞形变及基底粘附耦合在一起。通过数值分析（numerical analysis）研究细胞运动特征随基底刚度的变化，并引入记忆效应使细胞力学对化学反应产生反馈。

Result: 细胞的特征速度（characteristic speed）和扩散常数（diffusion constant）随基底刚度呈非单调变化，表明存在一个最优迁移刚度。在低于该最优值的基底上，记忆效应使细胞持久时间（persistence time）随刚度增加而增大。细胞形变与基底粘附的对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）是产生非单调依赖的根源。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为理解复杂的趋硬性细胞迁移提供了一个统一的描述，所预测的非单调行为与实验观测相吻合。

Abstract: Biological cells are able to adapt their behaviour in response to environmental cues. Durotaxis is a phenomenon in which cells adjust their migration depending on the mechanical properties of a surrounding substrate. Although durotaxis has been studied more than two decades, basic cellular-scale mechanism of how cells regulate the motility responding to substrate stiffness remains to be elucidated. We address this issue by developing a theory utilising a mechanochemical model that integrates intracellular biochemical reactions with cellular deformation and substrate adhesion. Numerical analysis reveals that the characteristic speed and diffusion constant of cells change non-monotonically with respect to substrate stiffness, indicating the emergence of an optimal stiffness for migration. In addition, by introducing a memory effect that allows feedback from cell mechanics to the intracellular chemical reactions, the persistence time increases with substrate stiffness on a substrate softer than the optimal. We further investigate theoretically the origin of the non-monotonic dependence, that is comparable to the experimental observations, in terms of cell deformation and symmetry breaking in substrate adhesion. We believe that our study provides a unifying framework to understand complex durotactic cell migration.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We describe an electron bunch injector scheme based on proton-driven plasma wakefield acceleration for the Electron-Ion Collider. The proton bunches needed to drive the plasma wake are taken from the existing Blue-Ring of RHIC. The polarized electron source is taken from the current EIC design. We describe the different elements making up the injection scheme and give an estimate for the performance. Our initial study indicates that the design parameters of the EIC are within reach when accelerating the electron bunches in the proton-driven plasma wake, with average polarization of ~70% and a luminosity of 1e34 cm$^{-2}$s$^{-1}$.

</details>


### [105] [Multilayer model for coatings with arbitrary layers for superconducting radio-frequency applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07958)
*Aaron Gobeyn,Wolfgang Ackermann,Herbert De Gersem*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 该论文对Kubo等人提出的超导-绝缘体-超导（SIS）多层结构模型进行了两方面扩展：一是推广至任意类型（超导、正常导体、绝缘体）和任意序列的层状结构；二是考虑了所有贡献，包括欧姆损耗和介电效应。研究发现最优构型为n=1的情况，但超导涂覆层厚度可缩减至穿透深度以下而性能损失较小。通过引入虚拟层表示过渡区，模拟了SS双层膜中的转变，发现过渡层越厚，最大可加场下降，有效穿透深度增大。利用Leontovich边界条件计算表面阻抗，并通过Poynting定理确定各层损耗贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Kubo模型仅适用于特定SIS结构，缺乏对更一般层序和材料类型的建模能力，且未完整计入欧姆损耗和介电效应。本文旨在扩展该模型，使其能够描述任意类型（超导、正常导体、绝缘体）和任意序列的多层结构，并全面考虑各类贡献。

Method: 将Kubo多层模型推广至任意层序与任意类型；计入欧姆损耗与介电效应；通过引入具有插值参数（interpolated parameters）的虚拟层（virtual layers）来模拟SS双层膜中的过渡区；利用Leontovich边界条件（Leontovich boundary condition）计算表面阻抗；应用Poynting定理（Poynting theorem）确定各层损耗贡献。

Result: 对(SI)^nS结构，最优构型为n=1；超导涂覆层厚度可降至穿透深度以下，性能损失较小；过渡层越厚，最大可加场（maximum applicable field）越低，有效穿透深度（effective penetration depth）越大；推导出适合集成到有限元仿真（finite element simulations）中的表面阻抗公式。

Conclusion: 扩展后的多层模型能够灵活描述任意层序和材料类型的SIS、SNS及SS双层膜等结构，并提供了适用于数值仿真的表面阻抗和损耗计算方法。

Abstract: We extend the multilayer model of \etal{Kubo} for superconductor-insulator-superconductor (SIS) structures in two ways:
  first, by generalizing it to arbitrary sequences of layers of arbitrary type, i.e. superconducting, normal conducting, and
  insulating; and second, by accounting for all contributions, including ohmic losses and dielectric effects. We examine the maximum
  applicable field for $(\text{SI})^n\text{S}$ structures. We find that the optimum configuration corresponds to the
  $n=1$ case. However, the thickness of the superconducting coating layers can be reduced to below their penetration depth
  with minor performance penalty. We discuss the ability to model transitions in SS bilayers by introducing a set of virtual layers
  that represent the transition region through interpolated parameters. We find degradation of the maximum applicable field
  with thicker transition layers, and a larger effective penetration depth of the electromagnetic fields. Furthermore,
  the surface impedance of the multilayer structure is calculated using the Leontovich boundary condition, yielding a formulation
  suitable for integration into finite element simulations. Additionally, the Poynting theorem is used to determine the loss
  contributions of individual layers.

</details>

### [106] [Nuclear Constraints on $^{12}$C$(α,γ)^{16}$O and Their Impact on Black-Hole Mass Predictions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07027)
*Akram Mukhamedzhanov*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究利用最新核物理数据重新分析低能\(^{12}{\rm C}(α,γ)^{16}{\rm O}\)反应的S因子，得到更低的\(S(300~{\rm keV})\)估值，并据此估算第一代黑洞质量间隙的下限约为\(61–75\,M_\odot\)，这表明该质量间隙的下限可能高于部分引力波人口推断的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波观测重新激发了对黑洞质量间隙（black-hole mass gap）及第一代黑洞最大质量的兴趣，而\(^{12}{\rm C}(α,γ)^{16}{\rm O}\)反应决定了碳氧比，进而影响大质量恒星演化至脉动对不稳定超新星（pulsational pair instability）和对不稳定超新星（pair-instability supernovae）的过程。然而，通过引力波人口推断（population inference）约束\(S(300~{\rm keV})\)存在模型依赖性（model dependence）的严重限制，因此需要独立核物理约束来验证。

Method: 本文利用亚阈值\(1^{-}\)和\(2^{+}\)态以及\(^{16}{\rm O}\)基态的渐近归一化系数（asymptotic normalization coefficients, ANCs）等最新信息，结合直接俘获（direct capture）数据，重新分析低能区\(^{12}{\rm C}(α,γ)^{16}{\rm O}\)反应的S因子。

Result: 新的核物理约束倾向于比旧的中心评估更低的\(S(300~{\rm keV})\)值，不支持某些黑洞人口解释所要求的极大值。基于ANC约束的\(S(300~{\rm keV})\)范围及其与对不稳定质量间隙下界的转换关系，得到第一代黑洞质量下限估计为\(M_{\rm BH}/M_\odot\simeq 61\text{--}75\)。

Conclusion: 当前的核物理约束支持第一代黑洞质量间隙的下限处于相对较高的位置（约\(61–75\,M_\odot\)），且从黑洞人口推断得出的\(S(300~{\rm keV})\)值必须与独立的核物理约束保持一致。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave observations have renewed interest in the black-hole mass gap and in the maximum mass of first-generation black holes below its lower edge. The \(^{12}{\rm C}(α,γ)^{16}{\rm O}\) reaction plays a central role in this problem because it determines the carbon-to-oxygen ratio after core-helium burning and thereby affects the later evolution of massive stars toward pulsational pair instability and pair-instability supernovae.
  Recent attempts to constrain \(S(300~{\rm keV})\) from gravitational-wave population inferences face important limitations, because the lower edge of the black-hole mass gap is not directly measured. It is inferred model dependently from assumptions about stellar evolution, metallicity, mass loss, rotation, binary evolution, hierarchical mergers, selection effects, priors, and the adopted population model. Therefore, values of \(S(300~{\rm keV})\) inferred from black-hole populations must remain consistent with independent nuclear-physics constraints.
  In this work we reanalyze the low-energy \(^{12}{\rm C}(α,γ)^{16}{\rm O}\) \(S\) factor using updated information on the subthreshold \(1^{-}\) and \(2^{+}\) ANCs and on the ground-state ANC of \(^{16}{\rm O}\), together with direct capture data. These constraints favor a lower \(S(300~{\rm keV})\) than the older central evaluation and disfavor very large values required by some black-hole-population interpretations. Using the resulting ANC-constrained \(S(300~{\rm keV})\) range and the transformed relation between this quantity and the lower edge of the pair-instability mass gap, we estimate \[ \frac{M_{\rm BH}}{M_\odot}\simeq 61\text{--}75 . \] Thus, the present nuclear-physics constraints favor a relatively high lower edge of the first-generation black-hole mass gap.

</details>


### [107] [Magnetar field dynamics driven by chiral anomalies without magnetic helicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08068)
*Clara Dehman*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文研究了手征磁效应（chiral magnetic effect, CME）在磁星磁场演化中的作用，发现即使初始磁场无整体螺旋度，CME也能在数十年时间尺度上高效产生磁星强度偶极场，其机制由局域螺旋结构驱动，结果对初始螺旋度分布敏感，拓展了CME在更现实磁场构型中的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前研究表明，CME可在初始磁场携带净螺旋度（net helicity）的条件下产生磁星强度偶极场，但中子星诞生时是否具有磁螺旋度尚不确定。本文旨在考察CME在不同初始螺旋度构型（包括非螺旋初始条件）下的表现，以评估其在更现实条件下的有效性。

Method: 作者在一系列初始螺旋度构型（含非螺旋条件）下数值模拟CME的演化过程，分析偶极场生成效率、不稳定性触发条件及其与初始螺旋度分布的关系。

Result: CME在数十年时间尺度上高效产生磁星强度偶极场（$B_{\rm dip} \gtrsim 10^{14}~\mathrm{G}$），且该过程独立于初始整体螺旋度。不稳定性由局域螺旋结构（localized helical structures）驱动，触发条件为最大手征化学势（chiral chemical potential）$μ_5^{\rm max} \gtrsim \mathrm{few}\times10^{-11}~\mathrm{MeV}$。生成的偶极场可稳定并经历标准欧姆衰变（Ohmic decay），或在获得足够螺旋度后经由手征反常（chiral anomaly）失稳衰变至低螺旋模式。

Conclusion: CME在更现实的磁场构型中仍具适用性；中子星诞生时的螺旋度分布是决定其磁场演化和磁星形成的关键因素，但目前对这一分布的认识仍极为有限。

Abstract: The chiral magnetic effect (CME), arising from the chiral anomaly and enabling a mutual conversion between magnetic topology and fermionic chirality, is a key mechanism in magnetar field evolution. Previous work by Dehman & Pons (2025) demonstrated that the CME can efficiently generate dipolar fields ($B_{\rm dip} \gtrsim 10^{14}~\mathrm{G}$), consistent with magnetar timing measurements, provided that the initial magnetic field carries net helicity. However, whether neutron stars are born with magnetic helicity remains uncertain. In this work, we investigate the CME across a range of initial helicity configurations, including non-helical initial conditions. We find that the CME efficiently generates magnetar-strength dipoles on timescales of decades, independently of the initial helicity content. The instability is driven by localized helical structures that induce a residual chiral asymmetry and is primarily governed by the maximum chiral chemical potential, requiring $μ_5^{\rm max} \gtrsim \mathrm{few}\times10^{-11}~\mathrm{MeV}$ for onset in the magnetar regime. Our results further show that these dipoles may either remain stable and subsequently evolve through standard Ohmic decay, or become unstable if they acquire sufficient helicity, in which case they decay through the chiral anomaly, transferring energy to less helical modes. This outcome depends sensitively on the initial helicity distribution. These findings extend the applicability of the CME to more realistic magnetic-field configurations and underscore the importance of the helicity distribution at birth, a quantity that remains poorly constrained in neutron star formation, yet is crucial for determining neutron star magnetic evolution and magnetar formation.

</details>

### [108] [On ratios of theta functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07580)
*Senping Luo,Juncheng Wei*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 本文受自由玻色子平均配分函数和Narain模空间上配分函数平均的启发，完整分类了theta函数与Epstein zeta函数之比的极值点（最大化与最小化），揭示了六角格点（hexagonal lattice）的关键作用。这些结果直接应用于共形场论（conformal field theory）和Liouville场论，并为结晶学和相互作用粒子理论中的相关函数极差提供了最小值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机来自两方面的前沿进展：c个自由玻色子（free bosons）的平均配分函数（average partition function）以及Narain模空间（Narain moduli space）上亏格1配分函数的平均。作者希望系统理解其中出现的theta函数（theta function）与Epstein zeta函数（Epstein zeta function）之比的极值行为。

Method: 本文采用完全分类（complete classification）的方法，系统研究theta函数与Epstein zeta函数之比的极小化子（minimizers）和极大化子（maximizers）。通过数学分析确定六角格点在这些极值问题中的核心角色。

Result: 完整分类了theta函数和Epstein zeta函数之比的极值点，证明了六角格点是其关键结构。此外，还得到了这些函数之差的极小值。

Conclusion: 本研究的成果可直接应用于共形场论和Liouville场论（Liouville field theory）中的配分函数计算。同时，theta函数和Epstein zeta函数之差的极小值对结晶学（crystallization）和相互作用粒子理论（interacting particle theory）具有数学意义。

Abstract: Motivated by the average partition function of c free bosons $($Afhkami-Jeddi et al. \cite{Afhk2021}$)$ and the average of the genus 1 partition function over the Narain moduli space $($Maloney-Witten \cite{Witten2020}$)$, we investigate ratios of theta functions. In this paper, we completely classify the minimizers (or maximizers) for ratios of theta and Epstein zeta functions. We find that the hexagonal lattice plays a pivotal role there. These results have direct applications in conformal and Liouville field theory via partition functions. Additionally, they yield the minima of differences of theta and Epstein zeta functions, which have implications for the mathematics of crystallization and interacting particle theory (\cite{Bet2016,Bet2019AMP}).

### [109] [Quantum Ergodicity on large hyperbolic surfaces for local and pseudolocal operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07696)
*Nalini Anantharaman,Soumyajit Saha*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文证明了一个量子遍历性定理（quantum ergodicity theorem），针对在Benjamini-Schramm意义下收敛到庞加莱圆盘（Poincaré disc）的闭双曲曲面序列。在注入半径一致有下界且存在谱间隙（spectral gap）的条件下，该定理建立了固定谱窗上量子方差（quantum variance）的消失性，适用于包含微分算子和有限传播光滑算子（finite-propagation smooth operators）的一类可观测量（observables）。这一结果将Le Masson与Sahlsten从标量可观测量推广到了局域和“伪局域”（pseudolocal）算子设定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将量子遍历性理论从标量可观测量的情形推广到更一般的算子类（如微分算子和有限传播光滑算子），以理解在双曲曲面趋于连续极限时量子方差的渐近行为。

Method: 使用Benjamini-Schramm收敛性框架来刻画闭双曲曲面序列向庞加莱圆盘的逼近过程；在注入半径一致有下界和谱间隙假设下，对固定谱窗上的量子方差建立消失性结果，并将可观测量的范围从标量函数扩展至局域与伪局域算子。

Result: 证明了在所述条件下，对于包含微分算子和有限传播光滑算子在内的可观测量类，量子方差在固定谱窗上趋于零，即量子遍历性成立。

Conclusion: 该定理将Le Masson与Sahlsten的标量结果推广到了算子层面，深化了对闭双曲曲面在连续极限下量子遍历性行为的理解。

Abstract: We prove a quantum ergodicity theorem for sequences of closed hyperbolic surfaces converging to the Poincaré disc in the Benjamini-Schramm sense. Assuming a uniform lower bound on the injectivity radius and a spectral gap, we establish vanishing of quantum variance on fixed spectral windows for a class of observables that contains differential operators and finite-propagation smooth operators. This generalises a result of Le Masson and Sahlsten from scalar observables to both local and 'pseudolocal' operator settings.

</details>

### [110] [Virasoro extensions for diffeomorphisms with breaks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07682)
*Anton Izosimov,Boris Khesin,Howard Xiao*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在圆环上除有限个奇点外光滑的“破损微分同胚”（broken diffeomorphisms），它们不构成李群（Lie group）而构成李群胚（Lie groupoid）；通过构造该群胚的一个非平凡n维中心扩张（central extension），将其限制在光滑情形时回归经典Virasoro群（Virasoro group），并进一步描述了相应的“破损Virasoro”代数胚（algebroid）。作为副产品，还分析了区间上端点处消失的向量场及固定端点的微分同胚群的中心扩张，以及允许端点变化时对应的李代数胚和群胚。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Virasoro代数是圆上向量场李代数的中心扩张，在共形场论和弦论中有重要应用。本文试图将这一结构推广到圆上存在有限个奇点（破损点）的情形，从而将光滑微分同胚的Virasoro结构延拓到更一般的、仅分段光滑的几何对象上。

Method: 首先将破损微分同胚自然地组织为李群胚，然后构造该群胚的一个非平凡n维中心扩张，该扩张在限制到光滑子对象时退化回经典Virasoro群。进一步定义相应的“破损Virasoro”代数胚，即除n个点外光滑的圆上向量场李代数胚的非平凡n维中心扩张。作为副产品，将类似构造应用于区间上端点处消失的向量场及固定端点的微分同胚群。

Result: 得到了一个非平凡的n维中心扩张的“破损Virasoro”群胚及相应的代数胚，它们将经典Virasoro代数推广到了带有有限个破损点的圆上。在区间情形，得到了端点处消失向量场李代数的非平凡中心扩张及相应群的中心扩张，以及允许端点变化时的代数胚与群胚结构。

Conclusion: 本文建立的破损Virasoro群胚与代数胚为处理圆上带有奇点的微分结构提供了统一的代数和几何框架，推广了经典的Virasoro代数与Virasoro群。区间情形的结果则进一步丰富了带有边界的类似结构，为相关领域（如可积系统、边界共形场论）提供了新的代数工具。

Abstract: We study homeomorphisms of the circle that are smooth diffeomorphisms away from a finite set of $n$ points. These "broken diffeomorphisms" do not form a Lie group, but instead naturally assemble into a Lie groupoid. We construct an explicit nontrivial $n$-dimensional central extension of this groupoid, which restricts to the classical Virasoro group when confined to smooth diffeomorphisms. We further describe the associated "broken Virasoro" algebroid, defined as a nontrivial $n$-dimensional central extension of the Lie algebroid of vector fields on the circle that are smooth except at $n$ points. This construction generalizes the Virasoro algebra.
  As a byproduct, we analyze a related setting on an interval: we construct a nontrivial central extension of the Lie algebra of vector fields vanishing at the endpoints, together with the corresponding central extension of the group of diffeomorphisms fixing the endpoints. We also describe the associated Lie algebroid and groupoid obtained by allowing the endpoints to vary.

*Dion Mann*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文利用微分同胚论（diffeology）严格构造了I.M. Singer的通用联络（universal connection），将其推广至微分同胚情境，并建立了从和乐表示（holonomy representations）重构微分同胚主丛-联络对（diffeological principal bundles with connections）的范畴等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为I.M. Singer的通用联络提供严格构造，并将其推广至微分同胚（diffeological）框架下，使得能够从和乐表示（holonomy representations）重构微分同胚主丛及其联络。

Method: 采用微分同胚论（diffeology）作为理论工具，对Singer通用联络进行严格构造，并将其推广至微分同胚情境；通过和乐表示的共轭关系（conjugate holonomy representations）建立微分同胚丛-联络对之间的等价关系；最终通过范畴论（category theory）方法总结为和乐范畴（holonomy category）与微分同胚丛-联络对范畴之间的范畴等价（equivalence of categories）。

Result: 成功构造了Singer通用联络并推广至微分同胚情境；证明了任何两个具有共轭和乐表示的微分同胚丛-联络对在特定意义下等价；建立了和乐范畴与微分同胚丛-联络对范畴之间的范畴等价。

Conclusion: 本文的结果在范畴论框架下统一了和乐表示与微分同胚丛-联络对之间的对应关系，为微分同胚主丛理论（diffeological principal bundle theory）提供了严格的联络构造基础。

Abstract: We provide a rigorous construction of I.M. Singer's universal connection, a natural connection on a bundle of paths associated to any manifold, using the theory of diffeology. Furthermore, we generalize the universal connection to the diffeological setting, which enables the reconstruction of diffeological principal bundles with connections from their holonomy representations. We show that any two diffeological bundle-connection pairs with conjugate holonomy representations must be equivalent in a certain sense. These constructions are functorial in that, ultimately, our results can be summarized as an equivalence of categories between the so-called holonomy category and the category of diffeological bundle-connection pairs.

### [112] [Unbinned extraction of $γ$ from $B\to DK$ with normalizing flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06768)
*Yuval Grossman,Tony Menzo,Stefan Schacht,Chinhsan Sieng,Jure Zupan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于归一化流（normalizing flows, NFs）的无分箱方法，用于从衰变链 $B^\pm \to (D \to K_S \pi^+ \pi^-) K^\pm$ 中提取 CKM 角 $\gamma$。通过 Monte Carlo 数据验证，该方法能在不确定度内成功恢复注入的 $\gamma$ 值，并采用集成策略传播统计误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统 CKM 角 $\gamma$ 的提取通常依赖对 $D$ 介子衰变达利兹平面（Dalitz plot）进行分箱（binned）处理，这种离散化可能导致信息损失。作者旨在利用归一化流（normalizing flows, NFs）学习连续的振幅与强相位表示，从而实现无分箱（unbinned）分析，提升对有限数据样本的利用效率。

Method: 首先在 $D$ 衰变数据上训练归一化流（normalizing flows, NFs），使其学习 $D \to K_S\pi^+\pi^-$ 达利兹平面上振幅与强相位的连续表示。然后将该表示作为输入，利用 $B$ 衰变数据提取参数 $r_B$、$\delta_B$ 和 $\gamma$。统计不确定度通过集成（ensemble）多个独立训练的流来传播。文章探索了两种版本的方法，区别在于相位变化的三角约束（trigonometric constraint）编码方式不同。

Result: 在 Monte Carlo 生成数据上的测试表明，该方法能够在不确定度范围内成功恢复注入的 $\gamma$ 值。当前实现仅传播由有限训练数据引入的统计不确定度，未处理系统实验误差。

Conclusion: 该方法展示了归一化流在无分箱 CKM 角提取中的可行性，并为未来扩展至贝叶斯归一化流（Bayesian normalizing flows）提供了方向，后者无需集成训练即可直接提供所学密度（learned densities）的不确定度估计。

Abstract: We introduce an unbinned method for extracting the CKM angle $γ$ from the decay chain $B^\pm \to (D \to K_S π^+ π^-) K^\pm$ using normalizing flows (NFs). The NFs, trained on $D$ decay data, learn a faithful continuous representation of the amplitude and strong phase variation over the $D\to K_Sπ^+π^-$ Dalitz plot whose fidelity improves with increased data sample sizes. With this input, the $B$ decay data can be used to extract the parameters $r_B$, $δ_B$, and $γ$. We test the method on Monte Carlo generated data, where it successfully recovers the injected value of $γ$ within uncertainties. The present implementation propagates statistical uncertainties from finite training data via an ensemble of independently trained flows, and does not attempt to capture the effects of systematic experimental errors. We explore two versions of the method that differ in how the trigonometric constraint on phase variation is encoded, and comment on the possible extension to Bayesian NFs, which would provide direct uncertainty estimates on the learned densities without requiring ensemble training.

</details>


### [113] [Neutrino-Antineutrino Conversion from Ultralight Vector Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06777)
*Asher Berlin,Rodolfo Capdevilla,Ting Cheng,Matheus Hostert,Pedro A. N. Machado*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超轻矢量暗物质与轻子数耦合的相互作用，如何影响马约拉纳中微子的传播行为，并挖掘这类效应在尚未被现有实验覆盖的参数区域的探测潜力。

Method: 在超轻矢量暗物质背景（如 $\text{U}(1)_{B-L}$ 或 $\text{U}(1)_{L_i - L_j}$ 规范玻色子）下，分析马约拉纳中微子转化为反中微子的过程，并利用长天体基线放大该微弱效应。

Result: 对于 $\text{U}(1)_{B-L}$ 暗物质，DUNE、Hyper-Kamiokande 和 JUNO 等探测器观测超新星中微子暴，可探测的规范耦合强度低至 $e^\prime \sim 10^{-32} - 10^{-25}$，暗物质质量范围为 $m_{A^\prime} \sim 10^{-22} \ \text{eV} - 10^{-14} \ \text{eV}$，远超其他未来探测手段的能力。

Conclusion: 该机制为利用未来中微子实验探测极弱耦合的超轻暗物质提供了新途径，有望覆盖其他探测方法无法触及的参数空间。

Abstract: We show that Majorana neutrinos convert into antineutrinos in a background of ultralight vector dark matter coupled to lepton number, such as the gauge boson of $\text{U}(1)_{B-L}$ or $\text{U}(1)_{L_i - L_j}$ with $i, j = e , μ, τ$. This effect is suppressed by the small neutrino mass, but the enhancement by long astrophysical baselines can enable future searches for solar and supernova neutrinos to explore uncharted parameter space. For instance, for $\text{U}(1)_{B-L}$ dark matter, the observation of a supernova neutrino burst at DUNE, Hyper-Kamiokande, and JUNO could probe gauge couplings as small as $e^\prime \sim 10^{-32} - 10^{-25}$ for dark matter masses of $m_{A^\prime} \sim 10^{-22} \ \text{eV} - 10^{-14} \ \text{eV}$, beyond the capability of other future probes.

### [114] [The structure of multi-axion solutions to the strong CP problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06787)
*Mario Fernández Navarro,Marta F. Zamoro,Marko Pesut,Xavier Ponce Díaz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了多轴子（multi-axion）理论中强CP问题的广义解，揭示了多种不同于单轴子QCD轴子带（QCD axion band）的质-光耦合模式，推导了N-轴子系统的一般求和规则，并识别了决定轴子参数空间位置的关键物理要素（PQ对称性破缺结构与QCD/电磁反常的相对对齐）。研究结果为扩展轴子搜索计划提供了理论动机，并对标准模型的紫外完备化具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轴子理论（multi-axion theories）是对标准单轴子图像的重要推广，因为额外的轴子态会普遍修改质量-光子耦合关系。然而，目前对多轴子强CP问题解的一般结构及其带来的多样化现象学可能性尚缺乏系统性理解。作者旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用一般性理论分析方法，研究多轴子强CP解的结构；推导了N-轴子系统的一般求和规则（general sum rule），该规则同时包含广义Peccei-Quinn破缺（PQ breaking）和非普适反常系数（non-universal anomaly coefficients）；将框架应用于双轴子系统和一般多轴子构型，并识别出现不同现象学区域的紫外完备理论（UV-complete theories）。

Result: 发现了多种定性不同的质-光耦合模式，包括出现在QCD轴子带右侧的轴子、位于实验可及左侧区域的轴子，以及QCD轴子带本身被位移的场景。识别出Peccei-Quinn对称性破缺的结构与QCD和电磁反常之间的相对对齐是决定轴子在参数空间中位置的关键因素。

Conclusion: 本文的一般性分析揭示了受限于更严格假设下无法捕捉的广泛现象学可能性。研究结果激励扩展现有的轴子搜索计划，并对理解基本物理学以及标准模型（Standard Model）的紫外完备化具有重要启示。

Abstract: A broad experimental program is targeting the QCD axion band predicted by single-axion solutions to the strong CP problem. Multi-axion theories provide a well-motivated departure from this canonical picture, since additional states generically modify the mass-photon-coupling relation. We investigate the general structure of multi-axion solutions to the strong CP problem and study the different qualitative mass-coupling patterns that arise, including axions to the right of the QCD band, axions in the experimentally accessible region to its left, and scenarios in which the QCD axion band itself is displaced. This general treatment reveals a broad set of phenomenological possibilities that are not captured by more restrictive assumptions. In particular, we identify the structure of Peccei-Quinn symmetry breaking and the relative alignment between the QCD and electromagnetic anomalies as key ingredients determining the location of the axions in parameter space. Combining these ingredients, we derive a general sum rule for $N$-axion systems that incorporates both general PQ breaking and non-universal anomaly coefficients. We apply the framework to the two-axion system and to general multi-axion setups, identifying UV-complete theories in which the different phenomenological regimes arise naturally. Our results motivate an extended axion search program and have implications for our understanding of fundamental physics and the ultraviolet completion of the Standard Model.

</details>


### [115] [Flavor as an Incomplete Structure: Conceptual Questions and the Role of DUNE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07890)
*Claudio S. Montanari*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统梳理了标准模型中“味”（flavor）结构的概念不完整性，并论证通过DUNE实验的精密振荡测量、近探测器系统与数据驱动预测策略，可以有效检验现有三味描述的自洽性及其可能的偏离信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型中的味结构尽管经验上极为成功，却缺乏对费米子家族（fermion families）、质量层级（mass hierarchies）及混合模式（mixing patterns）起源的基本解释；中微子（neutrinos）的微小质量、大混合角及其质量生成机制可能不同于带电费米子，使味问题成为亟待探索的概念性难题。

Method: 通过DUNE实验的分阶段规划（phased program）——涵盖长基线振荡测量、I期近探测器复合体（near-detector complex）以及DUNE-PRISM策略（用于控制相互作用模型系统误差并实现数据驱动的近-远预测）——来系统搜索超出最小味框架（minimal flavor framework）的微小关联偏离。

Result: DUNE实验凭借其长基线与近探测器之间的互补性（complementarity），以及PRISM策略对模型系统误差的抑制能力，尤其适合探测与三味描述存在的小幅关联性偏离。

Conclusion: 味是标准模型中经验成功但概念不完整的结构；DUNE为检验当前三味框架的自洽性及其可能局限提供了强有力的实验平台。

Abstract: Flavor remains one of the most successful yet least understood structures of the Standard Model. The discovery of the Higgs boson completed the electroweak account of mass generation, but did not explain the origin of fermion families, mass hierarchies, or mixing patterns. In this sense, flavor can be regarded as an empirically successful but conceptually incomplete structure. Neutrinos occupy a particularly sensitive place within this problem: their masses are tiny, their mixing is large, and their mass-generation mechanism may differ from that of charged fermions. In this article, we discuss flavor as an open conceptual problem and argue that DUNE, as a phased program spanning precision oscillation measurements and sensitivity to BSM and dark-sector phenomena, provides a powerful framework for testing the self-consistency and possible limits of the present three-flavor description. In particular, the complementarity between the long-baseline program and the Phase I near-detector complex, together with the DUNE-PRISM strategy for controlling interaction-model systematics and enabling data-driven near-to-far predictions, makes DUNE especially well-suited to search for small, correlated departures from the minimal flavor framework.

Abstract: This work presents the first comprehensive phenomenological analysis of the newly released Coherent Elastic Neutrino-Nucleus Scattering (CE$ν$NS) data on germanium, measured by the COHERENT collaboration at the Spallation Neutron Source. Leveraging the unprecedented precision of this dataset, we provide state-of-the-art determinations of key Standard Model and nuclear physics parameters. *Fukutaro Miya,Ryosuke Sato*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cho-Maison单极子（Cho-Maison monopole）基于电弱类型对称性破缺（electroweak-type symmetry breaking）构建，其本质结构暗示类似单极子构型在包含此类破缺机制的规范理论中应普遍存在，需要予以明确验证。

Method: 通过理论构造，在广泛模型类别中显式构建类Cho-Maison单极子构型；并利用低能有效场论（low-energy effective field theory）方法，将Cho-Maison单极子嵌入't Hooft-Polyakov单极子，通过积分掉（integrate out）高于电弱能标的自由度实现描述层次的衔接。

Result: Cho-Maison-like单极子构型确实存在于涵盖Pati-Salam模型在内的多类理论中；Pati-Salam模型中的单极子在电弱能标以下退化为电弱Cho-Maison单极子。

Conclusion: Cho-Maison单极子不仅是电弱理论中的孤立构造，更可作为't Hooft-Polyakov单极子在低能极限下的有效描述，从而在更基础的规范理论框架中获得了统一解释。

Abstract: A monopole configuration in the electroweak theory was constructed by Cho and Maison, allowing for a singular behavior at the origin. Since the essential structure of the Cho-Maison monopole is based on an electroweak-type symmetry breaking, similar monopole configurations are expected to arise more generally in gauge theories containing such a structure. In this paper, we explicitly show that Cho-Maison-like monopole configurations can indeed be constructed in a broad class of models. We also show that the Cho-Maison monopole can be embedded into an 't Hooft-Polyakov monopole as its low-energy effective description. In particular, we find that a monopole in the Pati-Salam model behaves as the electroweak Cho-Maison monopole once degrees of freedom which are heavier than the electroweak scale are integrated out.

### [118] [Collinear matching for leading power gluon transverse momentum distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07516)
*Alessio Carmelo Alvaro,Nanako Kato,Barbara Pasquini,Cristian Pisano,Simone Rodini*

TL;DR: 本文在树图（tree-level）和单圈（one-loop）水平上推导了领头幂次胶子横动量依赖部分子分布函数（gluon transverse momentum dependent parton distribution functions, TMD PDFs）的匹配关系，首次获得了胶子worm-gear T分布的Wandzura-Wilczek近似，并给出了包含质量修正的闭合表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对胶子横动量依赖部分子分布函数（gluon TMD PDFs）的匹配关系及高阶修正尚不完整，特别是twist-2和twist-3贡献、质量修正（mass corrections）以及Wandzura-Wilczek近似在胶子扇区（gluon sector）的应用仍属空白。

Method: 在树图水平，采用旋量形式（spinor formalism）推导了twist-2和twist-3贡献，并得到了T-even和T-odd分布的完整质量修正级数。在单圈精度，将部分子内部分子（parton-in-parton）框架扩展至小b展开（small-b expansion）的领头项之外，并发展了一种将质量修正纳入单圈结果的方法。

Result: 首次获得了胶子worm-gear T分布的Wandzura-Wilczek近似；给出了适用于数值实现（numerical implementations）的质量修正级数的闭合表达式（closed-form expression）。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一套系统处理胶子TMD PDF匹配关系及质量修正的理论框架，为高精度QCD现象学提供了重要的解析工具。

Abstract: We compute the tree-level and one-loop matching relations for leading power gluon transverse momentum dependent parton distribution functions. At tree-level, working within the spinor formalism, we focus on twist-2 and twist-3 contributions, deriving the complete series of mass corrections for both T-even and T-odd distributions. At one-loop accuracy, we extend the parton-in-parton framework to include contributions beyond the leading term in the small-b expansion. Applying this methodology to the gluon sector, we obtain for the first time the Wandzura-Wilczek approximation for the gluon worm-gear T distribution. Furthermore, we develop a method to include the mass corrections in one-loop results and provide a closed-form expression for the mass series suitable for numerical implementations.

### [119] [Bulk-mediated reflection of chirality-protected surface spin waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07875)
*Vitaliy I. Vasyuchka,Florin Ciubotaru,Andrii V. Chumak,Burkard Hillebrands,Alexander A. Serga*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本论文通过实验和模拟发现，在微米厚度的钇铁石榴石（YIG）薄膜中，手性Damon-Eshbach表面自旋波在边界反射时会激发局域化的厚度量子化体模式（bulk modes），而非互易的后向体积波则近似弹性反射。该结果表明体模式激发是实现手性局域表面波反向传播的物理途径，定义了基于手性的背散射免疫性的极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Damon-Eshbach型表面自旋波具有非互易传输特性，其手性动力学场结构（chiral dynamical field structure）被认为能在无体模式（bulk modes）的频率范围内抑制薄膜中的直接背散射。然而，在较厚的三维磁性介质中，体激发谱线与表面波重叠时，手性如何影响反射行为尚不清楚，这一空白构成了本文的研究动机。

Method: 采用布里渊光散射光谱学（Brillouin light scattering spectroscopy）、红外热成像（infrared thermography）以及微磁学模拟（micromagnetic simulations）三种手段，对微米厚度钇铁石榴石（yttrium iron garnet）薄膜中的手性Damon-Eshbach波反射行为进行实验观测和数值分析。

Result: 实验和模拟结果一致表明，手性Damon-Eshbach波在磁性介质边界反射时，会激发空间局域化的厚度量子化体模式；而作为对照，互易的后向体积波（backward-volume waves）反射时几乎不发生能量耗散。此外，定量表征了反射边界处驻立体激发的磁振子能量积累与耗散。

Conclusion: 体模式激发（bulk-mode excitations）是实现厚膜中手性局域表面波反向传播的物理途径，从而明确了基于手性的背散射免疫性（chirality-based backscattering immunity）的适用范围，并为非互易磁性介质中的波输运提供了通用框架。

Abstract: Surface spin waves of the Damon-Eshbach type exhibit intrinsically nonreciprocal transport properties with a chiral dynamical field structure that localizes counterpropagating waves at opposite film surfaces. Such chirality has been predicted to suppress direct backscattering in thin films within frequency ranges free of bulk modes. However, how chirality influences reflection in thicker three-dimensional magnetic media, where a dense spectrum of bulk excitations overlaps with surface waves, remains unclear. Here we demonstrate that, in micrometer-thick yttrium iron garnet films, reflection of the chiral Damon-Eshbach wave from the boundary of the magnetic medium is accompanied by excitation of spatially localized thickness-quantized bulk modes, whereas reciprocal backward-volume waves reflect nearly elastically. Brillouin light scattering spectroscopy, infrared thermography, and micromagnetic simulations reveal standing bulk excitations at the reflecting boundary and quantify the associated magnon energy accumulation and dissipation. These results identify bulk-mode excitations as the physical pathway enabling reversal of chirally localized surface waves in thick films, thereby defining the limits of chirality-based backscattering immunity and providing a general framework for wave transport in nonreciprocal magnetic media.

</details>

*Pranjal Praneel,Thomas G Kiely,Andre G Petukhov,Erich J Mueller*

Method: 本文从理论上构造了棋盘格玻色-哈伯德模型（checkerboard Bose Hubbard model），引入子晶格偏置作为调控参数，并通过transmon阵列实验平台进行物理实现与分析。

Result: 子晶格偏置将共度超流相（commensurate superfluid phase）推入实验可及的区域；同时获得了超流相与绝缘相的特征描述，并系统考虑了有限尺寸效应（finite size effects）的影响。

Conclusion: 子晶格偏置为二维玻色-哈伯德模型提供了新的探测手段，并使相关量子相在实验上更易实现，为超流-绝缘相变的研究提供了有价值的实验与理论框架。

Abstract: Adding a sublattice bias to the two dimensional Bose Hubbard model greatly enriches the available physics, and introduces knobs which can be used to control and interrogate the quantum state. We describe the physics of this checkerboard Bose Hubbard model and how it can be explored using transmon arrays. We show that the sublattice bias brings the commensurate superfluid phase into an experimentally accessible regime, and gives new probes. We characterize the superfluid and insulating phases, with careful attention to finite size effects.

### [121] [Rabi-coupling-induced three-component quantum droplet in ultracold Bose gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07372)
*Xiao Ding,Dajun Wang,Xiaoling Cui*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文揭示了一种在超冷玻色气体中实现三组分量子液滴（quantum droplet）的新机制：仅需一种组间相互作用为吸引性，通过拉比耦合（Rabi coupling）将第三组分接入已自束缚的二元液滴，并利用有限失谐（detuning）抵消因耦合增强引入的不稳定性。热力学分析与扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程数值模拟在Na-Rb混合体系中验证了该方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索仅依靠单一吸引性组间相互作用实现多组分量子液滴的可能性，并解决因引入更多排斥力导致液滴失稳的问题。

Method: 提出三组分液滴的形成机制：先由一种吸引性组间相互作用形成自束缚二元液滴，再通过拉比耦合将第三组分接入；采用热力学分析方法与基于扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程（extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation）的数值模拟，在Na-Rb混合体系中验证方案。

Result: 更强的拉比耦合会增大第三组分的占比，但同时引入更多排斥力而破坏液滴稳定性；通过在拉比耦合组分之间施加有限失谐（finite detuning），可有效弥补这种不稳定性。

Conclusion: 提出了一种通用策略：借助合适的单粒子场（single-particle fields）将现有二元液滴与额外组分桥接，从而稳定多组分液滴。

Abstract: We uncover a new mechanism for realizing three-component quantum droplets in ultracold Bose gases, where only one inter-species interaction is attractive. In this scheme, the inter-species attraction leads to a self-bound binary droplet, and the third component joins through Rabi coupling with one component of the binary droplet. We find that a stronger Rabi coupling leads to a larger fraction of the third component, but also destabilizes the entire droplet due to the involvement of more repulsive forces. Such instability can be remedied by a finite detuning between the Rabi-coupled components. We demonstrate these results in realistic Na-Rb mixtures, using both thermodynamic analyses and numerical simulations based on extended Gross-Pitaevskii equations. Our work outlines a general route for stabilizing multi-component droplets by bridging an existing binary droplet with additional components via suitable single-particle fields.
