### [122] [Landau free energy and the absence of spontaneous magnetization of the one-dimensional Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06691)
*Z. F. Zheng,R. K. Lin,J. M. Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从朗道自由能（Landau free energy）视角重新审视一维伊辛模型（one-dimensional Ising model）的自发磁化（spontaneous magnetization）问题。通过定义并计算态密度（density of states），结合最大项近似（maximum-term approximation）严格证明了在任意有限温度下该模型均不存在自发磁化，且朗道自由能在$m=0$处的二阶导数为正且非解析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典结论认为一维伊辛模型在有限温度下不存在自发磁化，但作者希望从朗道自由能（Landau free energy）这一不同理论视角出发，对该结论进行重新推导与严格证明，以深化对统计力学（statistical mechanics）基本模型的理解。

Method: 作者首先遵循伊辛（Ising）引入的技术定义并计算了一维伊辛模型（one-dimensional Ising model）的态密度（density of states）。基于该态密度的单调性（monotonicity property）给出启发式论证，随后在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下使用最大项近似（maximum-term approximation）精确求解模型，并分析了朗道自由能（Landau free energy）关于磁化强度$m$的函数行为。

Result: 态密度具有单调性，启发式地表明模型在任意有限温度下不存在自发磁化（spontaneous magnetization）。朗道自由能（Landau free energy）是$|m|$的增函数，且$m=0$处的二阶导数为正并随温度非解析变化，严格证明了模型在任意有限温度下均无自发磁化。

Conclusion: 从朗道自由能（Landau free energy）视角出发，通过态密度（density of states）分析与最大项近似（maximum-term approximation）精确求解，严格证明了经典结论：一维伊辛模型（one-dimensional Ising model）在任何有限温度下都不存在自发磁化（spontaneous magnetization）。

Abstract: We revisit the problem of spontaneous magnetization of the one-dimensional Ising model from the Landau free energy perspective. To this end, we define and calculate the density of states of the one-dimensional Ising model following a technique introduced by Ising. The observed monotonicity property of the density of states suggests heuristically that the model does not exhibit spontaneous magnetization at any finite temperature. Subsequently, we solve the model exactly in the thermodynamic limit by employing the maximum-term approximation, which is feasible due to the simple analytical expression of the density of states. We also show that the Landau free energy is an increasing function of $|m|$ and its second derivative at $m=0$ is positive and non-analytic in temperature, proving rigorously the absence of spontaneous magnetization of the model at any finite temperature.

</details>


### [123] [Breakdown of Adiabatic Scaling and Noise-Induced Functional Synchronization in Deeply Quiescent Excitable Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06692)
*Yefan Wu*

TL;DR: 本文针对三维Sherman-Rinzel-Keizer（SRK）模型中的乘性Feller噪声驱动随机动力学，发现传统极值评估方法存在“浴缸效应”（bathtub effect）导致统计偏差，提出对数质心提取法（logarithmic centroid extraction method）恢复绝热Kramers标度，并揭示了噪声诱导的次阈值生理性颤抖向宏观功能同步的跃迁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可激发生物系统中的相干共振（coherence resonance）评估常因能量景观平坦化和复杂非线性动力学而失真，需发展更稳健的统计方法以提取最优噪声强度。

Method: 采用三维SRK模型并引入乘性Feller噪声；针对传统极值评估的“浴缸效应”提出对数质心提取法，以滤除随机抖动并恢复绝热Kramers标度。

Result: 对数质心提取法在强噪声极限下实现了高线性度（R² > 0.95）的绝热Kramers标度恢复；识别了绝热近似（adiabatic approximation）失效的物理边界；在间隙连接（gap-junction）耦合系统中观察到噪声诱导的次阈值生理性颤抖向宏观功能同步的相变。

Conclusion: 本研究为平坦能量谷中的最优噪声强度提取提供了数学框架，揭示了静息生物系统如何利用随机涨落实现功能恢复。

Abstract: Coherence resonance (CR) characterizes noise-induced regularity in excitable systems, yet its evaluation in quiescent biological media is often obscured by flattened energy landscapes and complex nonlinear dynamics. In this study, we investigate the stochastic dynamics of a 3D Sherman-Rinzel-Keizer (SRK) model driven by multiplicative Feller noise. We show that traditional extremal evaluations of CR encounter a "bathtub effect" a broad resonance valley that can lead to statistical inaccuracies. To address this, we propose a logarithmic centroid extraction method, which filters out stochastic jitter and recovers the underlying adiabatic Kramers scaling with high linearity (R^2 > 0.95). Furthermore, we identify the physical boundary where this adiabatic approximation breaks down under the strong-noise limit. Extending our analysis to gap-junction coupled systems, we observe a noise-induced transition from sub-threshold physiological shivering (characterized by statistical correlation but negligible functional output) to macroscopic functional synchronization. Our results provide a mathematical framework for extracting optimal noise intensities in broad energy valleys and offer insights into how quiescent biological systems utilize stochastic fluctuations for functional recovery

### [124] [Emergence of Tsallis Statistics from a Self-Referential Nonlinear Operator: A Variational Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06705)
*Lucio Marassi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个自指非线性算子的变分热力学框架，证明在局域核（平均场）近似下，自由能极小化自然导出Tsallis q-指数分布，其中熵指标q = α + β由算子的不动点结构直接决定，而非人为假设。该框架建立了非广延统计力学的算子理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非广延统计力学（nonextensive statistical mechanics）中，Tsallis分布的熵指标q通常作为自由参数被引入，缺乏从底层动力学机制出发的推导。本文旨在通过自指非线性算子（self-referential nonlinear operator）的变分框架，建立q与系统结构指数之间的直接联系，从而为非广延统计提供算子理论基础。

Method: 研究者构建了一个由结构指数α > 0、β ≥ 0、对称核K和自耦合常数κ ≥ 0表征的非线性算子Ω。核心工具是自洽熵S[Ψ] = -D_KL(Ψ || ΩΨ)，该量在Ω的不动点处为零，并充当自然的Lyapunov泛函。在局域核（平均场）近似下，通过极小化自由能F = U - T S导出平衡态分布。

Result: 平衡态分布为Tsallis q-指数分布，熵指标q = α + β直接从算子的不动点结构涌现。框架给出了自洽的热力学描述，包括广义状态方程PV = (2 - q)T、响应函数以及自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）对应的临界温度。q = α + β的关系将可独立测量的反馈机制结构指数与分布尾指数直接关联，提供了一个无自由参数的判据。

Conclusion: 该工作为非线性自指反馈在平均场极限下自然生成Tsallis统计提供了算子理论层面的严格基础，将本工作与超统计（superstatistics）、约束熵极大化和q-变形形式主义等已有方法明确区分开来。

Abstract: We develop a variational thermodynamic framework for statistical systems governed by a self-referential nonlinear operator Omega characterized by structural exponents alpha > 0, beta >= 0, a symmetric kernel K, and a self-coupling constant kappa >= 0. The central object is the self-consistency entropy S[Psi] = -D_KL(Psi || Omega Psi), which vanishes at the fixed points of Omega and serves as a natural Lyapunov functional.
  Within the local kernel (mean-field) approximation, minimization of the free energy F = U - T S admits the Tsallis q-exponential distribution as an equilibrium state, with the entropic index q = alpha + beta emerging directly from the fixed-point structure of the operator rather than being postulated. The framework yields a consistent thermodynamic description, including a generalized equation of state PV = (2 - q) T, response functions, and a critical temperature associated with spontaneous symmetry breaking.
  The relation q = alpha + beta connects independently measurable structural exponents of the feedback mechanism to the observed tail index, providing a parameter-free criterion that distinguishes this approach from superstatistics, constrained entropy maximization, and q-deformed formalisms. This work establishes an operator-theoretic foundation for nonextensive statistical mechanics in which nonlinear self-referential feedback naturally generates Tsallis statistics in the mean-field limit.

### [125] [Direct Experimental Test of Conformal Invariance via Grazing Scattering: A Proposal for X-ray and Neutron Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06773)
*Alessandro Podo,Slava Rychkov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过全反射条件下的X射线或中子散射实验，测量边界条件下两点关联函数来直接检验临界现象中保角不变性（conformal invariance）的方案，并通过动量空间中的保角Ward恒等式（conformal Ward identity）将散射截面与动量传递和散射角之间的微分约束联系起来。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于存在边界（boundary）条件下的两点关联函数（two-point correlation function），利用全反射条件（即掠入射散射）下的X射线或中子散射实验进行研究。将动量空间中的保角Ward恒等式表达为散射截面关于动量传递（momentum transfer）和散射角（scattering angle）的微分约束。

Result: 该实验方案在现有技术条件下完全可行，例如可以利用二元合金（binary alloys）作为实验体系。这将是保角不变性在临界现象中的首个直接实验检验。

Conclusion: 保角不变性作为临界现象中一项被广泛假设但从未直接验证的对称性，有望通过本文提出的掠入射散射实验方案得到首次直接实验检验。

Abstract: We propose a test of conformal invariance in critical phenomena based on the study of a two-point correlation function in the presence of a boundary. This two-point function can be studied using X-ray or neutron scattering in the conditions of total reflection (so-called grazing scattering). The conformal Ward identity in momentum space is here expressed as a differential constraint on the scattering cross-section, as a function of the momentum transfer and the scattering angle. Experimental verification, using e.g. binary alloys, appears well within the existing techniques. This would be the first direct experimental test of conformal invariance in critical phenomena, a symmetry widely assumed but never directly verified.

### [126] [Bootstrapping ground state properties of classical frustrated magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06784)
*Nisarga Paul,Gil Refael*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于半定规划（semidefinite programming）的方法，通过有限维凸优化（convex optimization）层级结构，为无限格点上的平移不变经典自旋模型提供基态能量密度与关联函数（correlation functions）的严格双侧界。该方法将Lasserre层级（Lasserre hierarchy）适配至阻挫磁学（frustrated magnetism），并在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下证明层级收敛，同时推广了Luttinger-Tisza方法，适用于非二次哈密顿量（non-quadratic Hamiltonians）与非布拉维晶格（non-Bravais lattices）。在二维阻挫自旋模型上的数值实验表明，该方法能在宽参数范围内以高精度界定能量密度与可观测量（observables），每参数点典型运行时间仅为秒级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无限格点上的经典自旋模型基态问题本质上是非凸优化（non-convex optimization），传统解析方法如Luttinger-Tisza方法受限于二次哈密顿量与布拉维晶格，难以处理阻挫系统中的复杂约束；此外，先前方法无法系统性地给出能量密度的严格双侧界，制约了对阻挫磁学相行为的可靠数值研究。

Method: 该方法将无限格点上的非凸优化问题替换为一族基于正性条件（positivity conditions）的有限维凸优化层级：要求任意自旋构型上的概率分布满足特定矩条件，由此构建半定规划（semidefinite programming）问题。该框架本质上是多项式优化理论中Lasserre层级在阻挫磁学中的适配，并在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下证明了层级收敛性。

Result: 在多个二维阻挫自旋模型上的应用表明，该方法能够在宽参数范围内准确界定基态能量密度与可观测量，每参数点的典型运行时间为秒级。该方法不仅统一了Luttinger-Tisza方法，还扩展至非二次哈密顿量与多原子基的非布拉维晶格，克服了先前解析方法的适用范围限制。

Conclusion: 该工作为经典阻挫自旋系统的严格数值分析提供了一种通用且高效的凸优化框架，在精度与计算效率之间取得了良好平衡，并为未来向量子系统或更高维格点的推广奠定了基础。

Abstract: We introduce a method based on semidefinite programming that produces rigorous two-sided bounds on ground state energy densities and correlation functions of translation-invariant classical spin models on infinite lattices. In this method, the challenge of non-convex optimization on an infinite lattice is replaced with a hierarchy of finite-size convex optimizations arising from positivity conditions that any probability distribution over spin configurations must satisfy. This adapts the Lasserre hierarchy in the theory of polynomial optimization to the context of frustrated magnetism, and we prove convergence of this hierarchy in the thermodynamic limit. Our method subsumes the Luttinger--Tisza method and further applies to non-quadratic Hamiltonians and non-Bravais lattices, thus addressing limitations of prior analytical methods. We apply the method to various two-dimensional frustrated spin models, where it brackets the energy densities and observables accurately across large parameter ranges with typical run times of seconds per parameter point.

*Gunter M. Schutz,Ali Zahra*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解多物种排斥过程（exclusion process）在大尺度下的流体动力学规律，给出 Riemann 问题的显式解，并推广至开放边界情形以刻画稳态相图及边界诱导相变。

Method: 利用随机粒子系统的流体动力学极限（hydrodynamic limit）得到耦合的守恒律方程组；通过构造 Riemann 不变量求解 Riemann 问题；将周期系统的方法推广到开放边界系统，利用不变测度为乘积测度的特殊边界速率流形导出相图。

Result: 周期系统：得到 $n$ 个耦合无粘 Burgers 方程，证明存在 Riemann 不变量，获得激波（shock waves）和稀疏波（rarefaction fans）的显式解；开放系统：证明特定边界速率下不变测度与周期系统同为乘积测度，获得 $2n+1$ 个相的稳态相图，边界诱导相变与单物种 ASEP 类似。

Conclusion: PEP($n$) 的宏观行为可通过 Riemann 不变量完全刻画，其开放边界系统的相结构是单物种 ASEP 相图的多物种推广。

Abstract: The $n$-species particle-exchange process (PEP($n$)) is an exclusion process in which particles of $n$ different species exchange positions on neighbouring sites with rates chosen such that the invariant measure on the discrete torus is a product measure. We address the large-scale hydrodynamic behaviour of this process which yields a system of $n$ coupled inviscid Burgers equations. This system of conservation laws is shown to admit Riemann invariants for arbitrary $n$ from which explicit solutions of the Riemann problem in terms of shock waves and rarefaction fans are obtained. We also introduce the open PEP($n$), in which particles are exchanged with boundary reservoirs. For a distinguished manifold of boundary rates, we prove that the invariant measure is the same product measure as in the periodic system. The hydrodynamic description in terms of Riemann invariants is used to derive the stationary phase diagram explicitly in terms of microscopic boundary rates. In the generic case, the steady state exhibits $2n+1$ phases, with boundary-induced phase transitions analogous to those of the single-species asymmetric simple exclusion process.

### [129] [Tamed Feynman-Kac diffusion processes: Killing-branching intertwine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07824)
*Piotr Garbaczewski,Mariusz Żaba*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了有漂移布朗运动（drifted Brownian motion）的平衡弛豫，通过推断得到的薛定谔半群算子（Schrödinger semigroup operator）的费曼-卡茨核（Feynman-Kac kernel）来量化弛豫过程。该核函数本身也向平衡态弛豫，其涉及的隐式费曼-卡茨势（Feynman-Kac potential）可以是负值，对应分支（branching）机制，而正势可解释为杀死率（killing rate）。作者通过计算机辅助路径论证，在一维非线性模型中验证了这种杀死/分支驯服场景的一致性，并特别关注双阱势（double well potential）形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弥合推断费曼-卡茨核在概率论中的解释空白：该核函数看似缺乏自然的概率意义（除路径积分定义外），作者试图通过杀死扩散过程与分支（杀死/分支驯服）的路径视角为其提供物理解释和一致性论证。

Method: 采用计算机辅助的路径论证（computer-assisted path-wise arguments），针对一维空间中的多个非线性模型系统，考察费曼-卡茨势的正负区域与杀死率、分支率之间的对应关系，并在双阱势等解析解稀缺的系统中进行验证。

Result: 费曼-卡茨势的正值区域可解释为杀死率，负值区域可通过符号反转解释为分支（克隆/分叉）率；该势的负值子域必然伴随着对杀死效应的驯服（taming），且这种驯服通常过度补偿（overcompensated）了杀死效应。杀死/分支驯服场景在一维非线性模型中取得了一致性。

Conclusion: 被杀死的带分支扩散过程可视为被驯服（弛豫）的费曼-卡茨扩散的路径背景；该路径解释框架在双阱势等半经典区之外解析可及性有限的系统中仍需进一步研究。

Abstract: Relaxation to equilibrium of a drifted Brownian motion is quantified by a probability density function, whose main (multiplicative) entry is an inferred Feynman-Kac kernel of the Schrödinger semigroup operator. Although seemingly devoid of a natural probabilistic significance (except for its explicit path integral definition), the pertinent kernel relaxes to equilibrium as well. The implicit Feynman-Kac potential ${\cal{V}}(x)$, continuous, confining and bounded from below, may take negative values. If positive, ${\cal{V}}(x)$ can be interpreted as the killing rate of the decaying diffusion process. In case of relaxing F-K kernels the killing effects are tamed (often overcompensated). The taming inavoidably appears in conjunction with the existence of the negativity subdomains of ${\cal{V}}(x)$ in $R$. If locally ${\cal{V}}(x) < 0$, its sign inversion $- {\cal{V}}(x)$ can be interpreted as the branching (cloning, alternatively bifurcation) rate in the course of the other wise free random motion. The arising killed diffusion processes with branching, we interpret as the possible path-wise background of tamed (relaxing) Feynman-Kac diffusions. We present acomputer-assisted path-wise arguments, towards a consistency of the killing/branching taming scenario, for a number of nonlinear model systems in one space dimension. Special attention is paid to Feynman-Kac potential shapes, presumed to be in the double well form, where an analytic access to eigenvalues and eigenfunctions is scarce beyond the semiclassical regime.

</details>


### [130] [Multiscale Structure of Eigenstate Thermalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08079)
*Pavel Orlov,Rustem Sharipov,Enej Ilievski*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过引入可调电荷涨落规模的统计系综，证明宏观系统中局域可观测量矩阵元的分布不仅依赖于宏观态参数（如局域守恒荷密度），还依赖于采样本征态所用系综的性质；在可积场论中识别出一类可解析计算矩阵元抑制率的状态，揭示了矩阵元的多尺度结构，其代数指数呈现非解析的涨落尺度依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本征态热化假说（eigenstate thermalization hypothesis, ETH）为理解孤立量子多体系统（isolated quantum many-body systems）的热化（thermalization）提供了框架，但传统分析局限于微正则窗口（microcanonical windows），未能充分考察矩阵元分布对系综选择（ensemble selection）的依赖性。本文旨在探究矩阵元分布是否不仅依赖于宏观态参数，还受采样本征态所用系综性质的影响。

Method: 本文放弃传统的微正则窗口分析，引入具有可调尺度参数（scale parameter）的统计系综（statistical ensembles），该参数规定了电荷涨落（charge fluctuations）的幅度。具体研究了一个可积场论（integrable field theory），该理论允许对矩阵元进行高效数值采样，并可可靠地外推到热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）。

Result: 在该系统中识别出一类特殊状态，使得矩阵元抑制率（suppression rate）的封闭形式（closed-form）计算成为可能。发现矩阵元存在潜在的多尺度结构（multiscale structure），其特征由代数指数（algebraic exponents）的非解析涨落尺度依赖性（non-analytic fluctuation-scale dependence）所刻画。

Conclusion: 矩阵元在宏观系统中的分布不仅取决于宏观态参数，还普遍依赖于采样本征态所用系综的性质。这一发现揭示了传统微正则分析之外的、更丰富的系综依赖性结构，对深入理解ETH的适用范围和热化机制具有重要启示。

Abstract: The eigenstate thermalization hypothesis provides a framework for understanding thermalization in isolated quantum many-body systems by characterizing statistical properties of local observables in energy eigenstates. Here we demonstrate that distributions of matrix elements in macroscopic systems may depend not only on the macrostate parameters, such as the densities of local conserved charges, but generally also on the properties of ensembles used in sampling eigenstates. To this end, we depart from the conventional analysis of microcanonical windows and consider statistical ensembles with an adjustable scale parameter prescribing the magnitude of charge fluctuations. We specifically consider an integrable field theory that permits efficient numerical sampling of matrix elements and reliable extrapolation to the thermodynamic limit. Moreover, in this system, we identify a class of states that enables explicit closed-form computation of the suppression rate of matrix elements. Our findings reveal an underlying multiscale structure of matrix elements captured by a non-analytic fluctuation-scale dependence of algebraic exponents governing their statistical properties.

</details>


### [131] [Nonreciprocal McKean-Vlasov Equations: From Stationary Instabilities to Travelling Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07597)
*Arjun R,Pratyush Prakash Patra,A. V. Anil Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过引入和分析双物种非互易McKean-Vlasov方程，结合线性稳定性分析、弱非线性论证、伪谱模拟和Langevin粒子动力学，揭示了空间结构化的非互易相互作用如何控制集体有序的涌现机制，发现均匀弱非互易仅产生静态不稳定性，而空间调制的非互易可通过Hopf分岔产生驻波和行波态，并在粒子层面得到直接验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非互易相互作用（nonreciprocal interactions）打破了作用-反作用对称性，能够产生平衡自由能最小化无法描述的集体动力学，但空间结构化的非互易性如何控制有序态的涌现和本质尚不清楚，缺乏统一的连续描述框架。

Method: 推导了来源于随机相互作用粒子系统的双物种非互易McKean-Vlasov方程（nonreciprocal McKean-Vlasov equation）；综合运用线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）、弱非线性论证（weakly nonlinear arguments）、伪谱模拟（pseudo-spectral simulations）和Langevin粒子动力学模拟。

Result: 均匀弱非互易仅改变临界扩散阈值并产生静态不稳定性，无法产生持续时间依赖运动；空间调制非互易通过Hopf分岔（Hopf bifurcation）使均匀态失稳，产生驻波和行波态；识别了亚临界和超临界Hopf转变，行波可在弱非互易区域出现而无需显式的微观追逐规则；Langevin模拟证实这些振荡和行波态在粒子层面持续存在。

Conclusion: 非互易McKean-Vlasov方程为理解空间结构化非对称相互作用如何产生自组织运动、动力学相变（dynamical phase transitions）和非平衡集体有序提供了最小框架。

Abstract: Nonreciprocal interactions, in which action-reaction symmetry is broken, provide a powerful route to collective dynamics that cannot be captured by equilibrium free-energy minimisation. Here, we introduce and analyse a two-species nonreciprocal McKean-Vlasov equation derived from an underlying system of interacting stochastic particles. Combining linear stability analysis, weakly nonlinear arguments, pseudo-spectral simulations, and Langevin particle dynamics, we show that the structure of nonreciprocity controls the onset and nature of collective order. For spatially uniform weak nonreciprocity, asymmetry shifts the critical diffusion threshold but produces only stationary instabilities, indicating that uniform imbalance alone is insufficient to generate sustained time-dependent motion. In contrast, spatially modulated nonreciprocity fundamentally enriches the dynamics: depending on its symmetry and coupling to the interaction potential, the homogeneous state can lose stability through Hopf bifurcations, giving rise to standing and travelling wave states. We identify both subcritical and supercritical Hopf transitions, relate the selected patterns to Landau saturation coefficients, and show that travelling waves can emerge even in the weak-nonreciprocity regime without explicit microscopic run-and-chase rules. Direct Langevin simulations confirm that these oscillatory and travelling states persist at the particle level and are not artefacts of the continuum mean-field description. Our results establish nonreciprocal McKean-Vlasov equations as a minimal framework for understanding how spatially structured asymmetric interactions generate self-organized motion, dynamical phase transitions, and nonequilibrium collective order.

</details>


### [132] [Cluster Dynamics Stay Fast-Until Tricriticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07867)
*Minjun Jeon,Alexandros Vasilopoulos,Dong-Hee Kim,Víctor Martín-Mayor,Nikolaos G. Fytas*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 通过在二维Blume-Capel模型中进行混合团簇-局域更新方案的动力学标度研究，发现团簇蒙特卡洛算法（cluster Monte Carlo）在连续Ising型临界线上保持高效加速，但在三临界点（tricritical point）处加速失效，动态临界指数退化为局域更新值，其原因被追溯至空位（vacancy）的关联逾渗（correlated percolation）所引发的几何阻塞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决团簇蒙特卡洛算法在存在空位（vacancy）和多临界涨落（multicritical fluctuations）时是否能继续保持加速效果这一未决问题。

Method: 对二维Blume-Capel模型中的混合团簇-局域更新方案进行系统性的动力学标度（dynamic-scaling）研究。该模型展示了一条连续Ising型相变线，终止于一个三临界点（tricritical point）。

Result: 在整个临界线上，混合动力学保留了纯团簇更新的近最优效率。但在三临界点处，加速完全失效，动态临界指数（dynamic critical exponent）退化为局域更新值。这一失效被归因于空位的关联逾渗（correlated percolation），其产生的系统尺度几何结构阻碍了自旋扇区的非局域弛豫。

Conclusion: 三临界点处团簇加速存在根本性的几何限制，并确立空位逾渗（vacancy percolation）是控制混合蒙特卡洛动力学中动态普适性（dynamic universality）的机制。

Abstract: Cluster Monte Carlo algorithms are widely regarded as the most effective route to overcoming critical slowing down in lattice spin systems. Whether this acceleration persists in the presence of vacancies and multicritical fluctuations, however, remains unresolved. We address this question through a systematic dynamic-scaling study of hybrid cluster-local update schemes in the two-dimensional Blume-Capel model, which exhibits a line of continuous Ising-like transitions terminating at a tricritical point. Along the entire critical line, hybrid dynamics retain the near-optimal efficiency of pure cluster updates despite the presence of annealed vacancies. Strikingly, this acceleration collapses precisely at tricriticality, where the dynamic critical exponent reverts to the local-update value. We trace this breakdown to the correlated percolation of vacancies, whose emergent system-spanning geometry obstructs nonlocal relaxation in the spin sector. Our results identify a fundamental geometric limitation of cluster acceleration at tricriticality and establish vacancy percolation as the mechanism controlling dynamic universality in hybrid Monte Carlo dynamics.

</details>


### [133] [Mutual Linearity in Nonequilibrium Langevin Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07949)
*Jiming Zheng,Zhiyue Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在非平衡过阻尼朗之万系统（nonequilibrium overdamped Langevin systems）中建立了互线性理论（mutual linearity），揭示了连续系统中局部扰动下稳态密度与流观测量的线性关系，并将其推广至非稳态拉普拉斯域（Laplace domain），同时证明了该线性结构在离散与连续系统中的统一来源及其对有限宽度扰动的鲁棒性，并在F$_1$-ATP酶旋转马达模型中验证了该理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非平衡系统（nonequilibrium systems）对外部扰动的响应是物理学中的核心挑战，但目前缺乏统一的线性响应框架，尤其是在连续系统中对动态参数局部扰动下系统行为的理论描述尚不完善。

Method: 通过建立互线性理论（mutual linearity），分析过阻尼朗之万系统（overdamped Langevin systems）中动态参数在单点局部扰动下的稳态密度响应，并利用拉普拉斯域（Laplace domain）将理论扩展到非稳态弛豫过程（non-stationary relaxation processes）。

Result: 证明了在局部扰动下，任意两位置的稳态密度之间呈线性关系，且不同稳态流观测值（stationary state-current observables）之间亦存在互线性；揭示了离散与连续系统中的互线性源于相同的一维响应结构（one-dimensional response structure），并验证了互线性在有限宽度扰动（finite-width perturbations）下的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该工作为非平衡连续系统的响应控制与设计提供了理论框架，并在F$_1$-ATP酶旋转马达模型（F$_1$-ATPase rotary motor model）中成功应用，展示了互线性及其有限宽度鲁棒性的实际可行性。

Abstract: Understanding how nonequilibrium systems respond to perturbations is a central challenge in physics. In this work, we establish mutual linearity in nonequilibrium overdamped Langevin systems. This theory provides a framework for controlling and designing nonequilibrium responses in continuous systems. When a dynamical parameter is locally perturbed at a single position, the stationary densities at any two positions are linearly related. It further leads to mutual linearity among different stationary state-current observables. We also extend the mutual linearity to non-stationary relaxation processes in the Laplace domain. Our theory reveals that mutual linearity in both discrete and continuous systems originates from the same one-dimensional response structure. We further show that mutual linearity is robust under finite-width perturbations. As an application, we demonstrate the mutual linearity and its finite-width robustness in the F$_1$-ATPase rotary motor model.

</details>

Abstract: We show that for both QED and perturbative quantum gravity, finite-time Faddeev-Kulish dressings can be fully constrained by symmetry, and that this gives the unique choice which reproduces the classical memory effect. For gravity, we show that using this dressing to construct finite-time Fock spaces, as well as a carefully defined finite-time memory detector allows us to recover both the first order gravitational memory, as well as higher order Christodoulou contributions from the gravitational field. Conclusion: 本文构造的对偶关系同时展示了拓扑对称性与味对称性的交换特征，并可系统推广至具有一般秩、味数和Chern–Simons能级的$\mathcal{N}=2$辛SQCD理论。

Abstract: We propose a new class of infrared dualities relating three-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$ $USp(2N)$ Chern--Simons SQCD to planar Abelian quiver gauge theories. These dual descriptions are constructed via real mass deformations of established $\mathcal N=4$ mirror dualities between $\mathcal{N}=4$ $USp(2N)$ SQCD and unitary $D$-type quiver gauge theories. The resulting $\mathcal N=2$ dual pairs exhibit the characteristic exchange of topological and flavor symmetries. We provide nontrivial evidence for these dualities by matching $\mathbf{S}^3_b$ partition functions, superconformal indices, and gauge-invariant operator spectra. Furthermore, we systematically incorporate additional real mass deformations on both sides of the duality, allowing us to extend the construction to $\mathcal{N}=2$ symplectic SQCD with generic ranks, flavors, and Chern--Simons levels.

### [136] [A Semiclassical Diagnostic for Spacetime Emergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06780)
*Netta Engelhardt,Elliott Gesteau*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种半经典诊断方法，用于识别全息法则中时空涌现失败的案例，并评估“观测者规则”（observer rules）对此类失败的修复程度。该诊断基于一种称为“渐逝量子极值曲面”（evanescent quantum extremal surfaces）的几何对象，其特点是面积存在上限而非广义熵（generalized entropy）存在上限。文章进一步通过经典连通性与量子连通性之间的操作区分，解释了此类曲面的行为特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究表明，某些半经典时空无法通过传统全息规则（holography）实现涌现，这促使学者提出“观测者规则”以恢复时空涌现。本文旨在提供一种通用的半经典诊断手段，用于检测此类涌现失败的案例，并量化观测者规则的修复效果。

Method: 本文引入“渐逝量子极值曲面”作为诊断工具。不同于通常的量子极值曲面（QES），渐逝QES的判别依据是其面积存在上限，而非其广义熵存在上限。这一特征源于广义熵中面积项与体纠缠项（bulk entanglement term）之间解耦的约束关系。

Result: 渐逝QES的广义熵可能很大：尽管其面积项必须很小，但体纠缠项不受此限制。这一现象揭示了半经典引力（semiclassical gravity）中经典连通性与量子连通性之间的操作区分，等价于广义熵中两个求和项之间的区分。

Conclusion: 该诊断为识别全息法则中时空涌现的失败提供了新的几何判据，并阐明了观测者规则在恢复涌现过程中的作用机制。同时，对经典与量子连通性的区分深化了对广义熵结构的理解。

Abstract: Recent developments have shown that some semiclassical spacetimes cannot emerge from a traditional application of the rules of holography, prompting proposals for restoring their emergence with "observer rules". In this paper, we propose a general semiclassical diagnostic of such failures of emergence, and of the extent to which observer rules can fix them. Our diagnostic is the presence of certain "evanescent" quantum extremal surfaces, which are distinguished by an upper bound on their area rather than their generalized entropy. In particular, the generalized entropy of an evanescent QES may be large: even though its area term must be small, its bulk entanglement term is unconstrained. This feature is explained by an operational distinction between classical and quantum connectivity in semiclassical gravity, or equivalently between the two summands of the generalized entropy.

Abstract: We develop the foundations of Carrollian statistical mechanics by considering a system of interacting instantonic space-filling branes on a flat background, thereby providing the closest Carrollian analogue to the Galilean gas of interacting particles that underpins Boltzmann's collision theory. By adapting Boltzmann's statistical approach within this framework, we provide a first-principles microscopic derivation of the so-called Carrollian fluid equations, which were previously obtained as the vanishing-speed-of-light limit of relativistic conservation laws. We then use this analysis as a basis for formulating the first elements of Carrollian thermodynamics.

### [138] [Sharpened Dynamical Cobordism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06793)
*Andriana Makridou,Alejandro Javier Puga Gómez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“锐化版动态配边猜（Sharpened Dynamical Cobordism Conjecture）”，通过引入临界指数δ的允许范围R^ξ来判断奇点是否表示时空终结，并验证了该判据在多个弦论实例（如 massive IIA、O8-平面、特定黑洞解及D-膜分布）中的自洽性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始动态配边猜想（Dynamical Cobordism）用于刻画时空奇点能否被视为“终结于无（transition-to-nothing）”，但其判定条件不够精确。本文旨在提出一个更锐化的版本，通过指定物理结构ξ所对应的临界指数δ的允许范围R^ξ，从而更严格地区分真正的时空终结与由非平凡配边整体荷（cobordism global charge）所导致的障碍。

Method: 受Gubser判据（Gubser criterion for good singularities）启发，提出确定R^ξ的规则。将奇点分为两类：若δ∈R^ξ，则视为真正的“终结于无”构型；若δ∉R^ξ，则表明存在非平凡配边整体荷，与量子引力理论不兼容，可通过修改物理结构（如引入新自由度及相应的缺陷）来缓解。作为概念验证，显式展示了引入高阶规范场（higher-form gauge field）如何改变δ的允许范围。

Result: 在多个案例中验证了该猜想：massive IIA弦理论与O8-平面（O8-planes）的兼容性；Janis-Newman-Winicour及Garfinkle-Horowitz-Strominger黑洞解；以及某些D-膜（D-branes）的奇异分布。所有这些案例的结果均与预期一致。

Conclusion: 锐化版动态配边猜想能够更精确地判定奇点是否代表时空的终结，并在弦论背景下与已知结果保持一致，为量子引力中的奇点分类提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We propose a sharpened version of Dynamical Cobordism, where the physical structure $ξ$ of the theory in question determines an allowed range $R^ξ$ for the critical exponent $δ$. We interpret a singularity with $δ\in R^ξ$ as a true transition-to-nothing, i.e., a configuration ending spacetime, while a singularity with $δ\notin R^ξ$ indicates some obstruction to such a transition, i.e., the presence of a non-trivial cobordism global charge, which is incompatible with a theory of quantum gravity. In the spirit of the original Cobordism Conjecture, this apparent inconsistency of the theory can be alleviated via the modification of the structure, for instance by introducing new degrees of freedom and associated defects. Inspired by the Gubser criterion for good singularities, we propose a way to determine $R^ξ$. As a proof-of-concept we show explicitly how the introduction of a higher-form gauge field changes the allowed range of $δ$ compared to an EFT with only scalars. We test this sharpened version of Dynamical Cobordism against several examples, such as massive IIA string theory, where it is notably compatible with the presence of O8-planes; the Janis-Newman-Winicour and Garfinkle-Horowitz-Strominger black hole solutions; and certain singular distributions of D-branes. In all these cases, the Sharpened Dynamical Cobordism Conjecture leads to results consistent with our expectations.

</details>


### [139] [$G_2$ flux compactifications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06800)
*Aravind Aikot,Zheng Miao,George Tringas,Timm Wrase*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文系统地推导了将全部五种十维弦理论（string theory）在具有 $G_2$ 结构的七维流形上紧致化（compactification）后得到的三维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ 有效理论（effective theory），完整给出了标量势、动能项、轴子扇区（axionic sectors）、规范场、Stückelberg 耦合以及允许的几何与形式通量（form-flux）数据的模空间（moduli）依赖关系，为比较不同类型弦论的三维紧致化提供了统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前关于 $G_2$ 约化（reduction）的分析未完整纳入所有泛存在的场与通量。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立统一框架以系统地比较 IIA 型、IIB 型、I 型以及杂化（heterotic）弦论在三维紧致化中的有效理论。

Method: 通过在具有 $G_2$ 结构的七维流形上对全部五种十维弦理论进行通量紧致化（flux compactification），明确导出了三维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ 有效理论。推导明确包含了标量势、动能项、轴子扇区、规范场、Stückelberg 耦合以及几何与形式通量数据的完整模空间依赖性。

Result: 得到了所有五种十维弦理论在 $G_2$ 结构流形上紧致化至三维后的完整有效理论表达式。这些有效理论自然地组织在三维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ 超引力（supergravity）的实超势（real superpotential）框架下。

Conclusion: 该工作清晰地揭示了通量（fluxes）、挠率（torsion）、Chern–Simons 数据与模势（moduli potential）之间的内在关联，为不同弦论的三维约化提供了统一的比较基础。

Abstract: We derive the three-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ effective theories obtained by compactifying all five ten-dimensional string theories on generic seven-dimensional manifolds with $G_2$ structure. The resulting flux compactifications are worked out explicitly, including the full moduli dependence of the scalar potential, kinetic terms, axionic sectors, gauge fields, Stückelberg couplings, and the allowed geometric and form-flux data. Our results extend previous analyses by incorporating fields and fluxes that are generically present in $G_2$ reductions, and provide a unified framework for comparing type IIA, type IIB, type I and heterotic compactifications to three dimensions. In particular, the effective theories organize naturally in terms of the real superpotential formulation of three-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ supergravity, making the relation between fluxes, torsion, Chern--Simons data, and moduli potentials manifest.

### [140] [The Conformal Grassmannian: A Symplectic Bi-Grassmannian for $CFT_ 4$ Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06811)
*Aswini Bala,Sachin Jain,Dhruva K. S*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了四维共形场论（CFT₄）中Wightman关联函数的一种辛双格拉斯曼（symplectic bi-Grassmannian）表示形式。该形式利用Klein空间中的离壳旋量-螺旋性（spinor-helicity）变量，将Δ=2标量场和无迹对称守恒流的关联函数编码为一对n-平面（在2n维辛向量空间中）上的积分。该构造几何地体现了共形不变性、动量守恒和小群协变性，并推导了所有两点和三点函数。作为关键验证，该框架重现了⟨JJJ⟩和⟨TTT⟩的全部独立共形不变结构，且表达式比动量空间对应项更加紧凑，同时显式体现了杨-米尔斯与爱因斯坦引力的双拷贝（double copy）关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四维共形场论中关联函数的结构分析是量子场论的重要课题，但传统动量空间表示往往表达式冗长且结构不够透明。本文旨在发展一种更几何化、更紧凑的形式来描述CFT₄的Wightman关联函数，以便清晰揭示共形对称性、动量守恒、小群协变性以及杨-米尔斯与引力之间的双拷贝关系。

Method: 本文引入辛双格拉斯曼表示：在Klein空间中利用离壳旋量-螺旋性变量，将CFT₄关联函数表示为在2n维辛向量空间中一对n-平面上的积分。这些平面被约束为相互辛正交（mutually symplectically orthogonal），并与外运动学对齐。此外，还发展了一种螺旋性基（helicity-basis）重新表述，使各螺旋性分量的GL(1,R)和SL(2,R)权重得以显式化。

Result: 推导了涉及标量场、费米子、守恒流和能动张量的所有两点和三点函数。该构造成功再现了CFT₄中⟨JJJ⟩和⟨TTT⟩的全部独立共形不变结构，且表达式比传统动量空间形式更紧凑。此外，结果显式体现了杨-米尔斯⟨JJJ⟩与爱因斯坦引力⟨TTT⟩之间的双拷贝关系。

Conclusion: 所提出的辛双格拉斯曼形式为CFT₄关联函数提供了一种几何化且简洁的描述，不仅使共形对称性、动量守恒等对称性质更加透明，还自然地展现了规范理论和引力之间在关联函数层面的双拷贝结构。螺旋性基的引入为后续的扭量空间（twistor space）表述奠定了基础。

Abstract: We introduce a formalism for conformal field theory in four dimensions: a symplectic bi-Grassmannian representation of CFT$_4$ Wightman correlators. Working in Klein space with off-shell spinor-helicity variables, we show that correlators of $Δ= 2$ scalars and symmetric-traceless conserved currents are encoded by integrals over a pair of $n$-planes in a $2n$-dimensional symplectic vector space. These planes are constrained to be mutually symplectically orthogonal and aligned with the external kinematics. Conformal invariance, momentum conservation, and little-group covariance all follow geometrically from this structure. We derive all two- and three-point functions involving scalars, fermions, conserved currents, and stress tensors. As a non-trivial test, we show that the construction reproduces the full set of independent conformally invariant structures of $\langle JJJ\rangle$ and $\langle TTT\rangle$ in CFT$_4$. The resulting expressions are considerably more compact than their momentum-space counterparts. They also make manifest the double copy between Yang--Mills $\langle JJJ \rangle$ and Einstein-gravity $\langle TTT \rangle$. We further present a helicity-basis reformulation that makes the GL(1,R) and SL(2,R) weights of individual helicity components explicit. This basis also provides a natural starting point for a twistor-space formulation of the correlators.

### [141] [Quantum graviton scattering with definite helicities in the null surface formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06961)
*Carlos Kozameh,Gerardo Depaola*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在渐近平直时空的零曲面表述（NSF）中发展了引力的二阶量子微扰理论。所有动力学自由度均为零无穷远的辐射数据，无需体场或离壳传播子。推导了螺旋度分辨的Bondi剪切及对应的出算符，自然生成引力尾振幅和引力子散射振幅。该理论因中间引力子严格在壳且微扰能标受高斯抹平态抑制而具有微扰有限性，无需重整化或抵消项。其自然可观测量是天球面上的谱角分布，编码BMS超动量通量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统协变量子引力在离壳体传播子中产生紫外发散，且渐近态仅通过iε体方案间接定义。本文旨在构建一种基于零无穷远辐射数据的量子引力框架，从根本上避免上述发散问题。

Method: 采用零曲面表述（Null Surface Formulation, NSF），直接在零无穷远（null infinity）处开展工作，不引入体场或离壳传播子。推导了螺旋度分辨（helicity-resolved）的Bondi剪切与出算符（out-operators），并基于二阶量子微扰理论（second-order quantum perturbation theory）构建非线性引力子过程。

Result: 得到了需要相反入射螺旋度的引力尾振幅（gravitational tail amplitude），以及可分解为两个尾顶点通过一个在壳中间引力子连接的引力子散射振幅（graviton scattering amplitude）。在庞加莱极限下恢复了Weinberg树图振幅的s道贡献，交叉道出现在更高微扰阶。该理论具有微扰有限性（perturbatively finite），原因包括：中间引力子严格在壳，不产生虚体动量回路积分；高斯抹平（Gaussian-smeared）引力子态（Bondi质量相对于普朗克尺度很小）的抑制效应在微扰层级中递归传播，无需重整化（renormalization）或抵消项（counterterms）。自然可观测量是天球面（celestial sphere）上的谱角分布，编码BMS超动量通量而非普通庞加莱动量守恒。

Conclusion: 该NSF量子引力理论与协变微扰引力在结构上截然不同，其有限性源于在壳传播子与抹平态抑制而非传统紫外重整化。引力记忆（gravitational memory）、MHV螺旋度选择定则（MHV helicity selection rules）以及相干态经典极限（coherent-state classical limit）在同一框架内自然出现。

Abstract: We develop the second-order quantum perturbation theory of gravity in the Null Surface Formulation (NSF) of asymptotically flat spacetimes. In this framework all dynamical degrees of freedom are radiative data defined at null infinity; no bulk fields or off-shell propagators enter the construction. Working directly at null infinity, we derive the helicity-resolved Bondi shear and the corresponding out-operators governing nonlinear graviton processes. The formalism naturally generates a gravitational tail amplitude requiring opposite incoming helicities, and a graviton scattering amplitude that factorizes into two tail vertices connected by an on-shell intermediate graviton. Imposing the Poincare limit reproduces the s-channel contribution of the Weinberg tree-level amplitude, while the crossed channels are shown to arise at higher perturbative order. The theory is perturbatively finite for two independent reasons: all intermediate gravitons are strictly on-shell, so no loop integrals over virtual bulk momenta are generated; and the perturbative regime requires Gaussian-smeared graviton states (small Bondi mass relative to the Planck scale), whose suppression propagates recursively through the hierarchy, rendering all energy integrals absolutely convergent at every order without renormalization or counterterms. This finiteness is structurally distinct from the ultraviolet problem of covariant perturbative gravity, where divergences originate in off-shell bulk propagators and asymptotic states are defined only indirectly via an iε bulk prescription. The natural observables of the NSF are spectral-angular distributions on the celestial sphere, which encode BMS supermomentum flux rather than ordinary Poincare momentum conservation. Gravitational memory, MHV helicity selection rules, and the coherent-state classical limit arise naturally within the same framework.

### [142] [Real-Time Quantum Dynamics on the Fuzzy Sphere: Chaos and Entanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06985)
*S. Kürkcüoğlu,B. Özcan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本研究采用高斯态近似（Gaussian state approximation）分析模糊球面上两个玻色子场的矩阵模型的实时量子动力学，通过导出相关函数的耦合非线性微分方程、热态方程及李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent），证明量子动力学在有限温度下满足 Maldacena-Shenker-Stanford 混沌界，并在高温下趋近经典混沌区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解矩阵模型在模糊球面（fuzzy sphere）上的实时量子动力学（real-time quantum dynamics），特别关注其混沌（chaos）特征和纠缠动力学（entanglement dynamics），以检验量子混沌界（quantum chaos bound）的成立性。

Method: 基于哈密顿量形式（Hamiltonian formulation），利用 Wick 定理（Wick's theorem）导出关于单点和两点关联函数（one- and two-point correlation functions）的封闭耦合非线性微分方程组。通过最大化高斯态上的 von Neumann 熵（von Neumann entropy）求解代数自洽方程，确定协方差矩阵（covariance matrix）的辛谱（symplectic spectrum）。识别近热初始条件（near thermal initial conditions）并求解运动方程，计算最大李雅普诺夫指数（largest Lyapunov exponent）探测混沌，并通过划分希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）计算纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）分析纠缠动力学。

Result: 最大李雅普诺夫指数在有限温度下趋于零，表明量子动力学在所有温度下均满足 Maldacena-Shenker-Stanford 界（MSS bound），并在高温下趋近经典混沌区域。实时纠缠熵分析清晰展示了快速加扰（fast scrambling）特征。

Conclusion: 高斯态近似方法能有效捕捉模糊球面矩阵模型的量子混沌与纠缠动力学，且量子动力学严格遵循混沌界，系统在高温下表现出经典混沌行为和快速加扰特性。

Abstract: We study the real time quantum dynamics of a matrix model consisting two bosonic fields on the fuzzy sphere using the Gaussian state approximation. Starting from the Hamiltonian formulation and using Wick's theorem, we derive a closed set of coupled nonlinear differential equations governing the time evolution of the one- and two-point correlation functions. Thermal equation of state is found by maximizing the von Neumann entropy over Gaussian states and solving algebraic self-consistency equation(s) leading to a complete determination of the symplectic spectrum of the covariance matrix. We identify near thermal initial conditions and use them to solve the equations of motion and employ our findings to probe chaos by calculating the largest Lyapunov exponent at various temperatures. Our results demonstrate that the latter tends to zero at a finite temperature indicating that the quantum dynamics respect the Maldacena,Shenker,Stanford bound across all temperatures, while approaching toward the classically chaotic regime at high temperatures. Finally, we examine the entanglement dynamics of the model in real-time by considering a sequence of bipartitions of the Hilbert space and computing the entanglement entropy and clearly exhibit the fast scrambling features that emerge in due detail.

### [144] [Broken and restored: a holographic constraint for AdS vacua with orbifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07464)
*Filippo Revello,Vincent Van Hemelryck*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发现，具有大N全息对偶的弱耦合AdS真空必须满足三次耦合消失的一致性约束，但该约束在多种类型II AdS$_3$和AdS$_4$真空（包括尺度分离解和DGKT-CFI型模型）中被普遍违反。通过将轨形群扩展为适当的非阿贝尔群可以消除违规标量算符。结果表明，全息对偶的一致性对紧致化几何施加了非平凡限制，特别是O面不能缠绕不同同调类中的闭链。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前研究表明，具有大N全息对偶（large-$N$ holographic dual）的弱耦合AdS真空必须满足非平凡的相容性条件，即某些三次耦合必须为零，对应标量算符的（超）极值排列。本文旨在检验该约束在更广泛的类型II弦论真空中的有效性，并探索违反该约束时的修正可能性。

Method: 作者系统考察了源自$\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$和$\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$轨形（orbifold）的类型II AdS$_3$和AdS$_4$真空，包括尺度分离解（scale-separated solutions）和DGKT-CFI型模型。通过对比已知在DGKT场景中最简情形下成立的约束条件，检验这些更一般情形下的三次耦合是否为零，并尝试通过将轨形群扩展为合适的非阿贝尔群（non-abelian extension）来消除违规项。

Result: 约束条件在$\mathbb{Z}_3\times \mathbb{Z}_3$轨形上的DGKT场景中成立，但在$\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$和$\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$轨形的AdS$_3$和AdS$_4$真空（包括DGKT-CFI型模型）中被普遍违反。不过，在大多数情况下，通过将轨形群扩展为适当的非阿贝尔群，可以精确投影掉那些参与受约束三次耦合的标量算符，从而修复该问题。

Conclusion: 假设的全息对偶的一致性对紧致化几何（compactification geometry）施加了非平凡限制，特别地，O面（O-planes）不能缠绕在不同同调类（homology classes）的闭链上。

Abstract: It has been suggested that families of weakly-coupled AdS vacua with a large-$N$ holographic dual must satisfy non-trivial consistency requirements, which amount to the vanishing of certain cubic couplings, corresponding to (super-)extremal arrangements of scalar operators. While this constraint is known to hold in the simplest incarnation of the DGKT scenario in massive type IIA string theory, i.e. on the $\mathbb{Z}_3\times \mathbb{Z}_3$ orbifold, we find that it is generically violated for type II AdS$_3$ and AdS$_4$ vacua arising from $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ and $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifolds respectively, including scale-separated solutions and DGKT-CFI-type models. In most cases, however, this can be cured by enlarging the orbifold group to a suitable (non-abelian) extension that projects out precisely those scalar operators that would otherwise participate in the constrained cubic couplings. Our results suggest that consistency of the putative holographic dual imposes a non-trivial restriction on the compactification geometry, indicating in particular that O-planes cannot wrap cycles in distinct homology classes.

### [145] [Genus drop involving non-hyperelliptic curves in Feynman integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07729)
*Feiyu Yang,Jianyu Gong,Yang Zhang*

TL;DR: 本文重新表述了超椭圆费曼积分中由额外-对合机制引起的亏格下降现象，将其推广为代数曲线间无分歧双覆盖的特例，并证明该覆盖机制同样解释了三圈非超椭圆费曼图在亏格下降的同时伴随曲线类型变化的现象。此外，文章指出在特定框架下超椭圆情形中离散时空对称性的起源是显式的，并发现存在不表现出明显亏格下降的非超椭圆费曼积分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分析费曼积分（Feynman integrals）的函数类型对于理论和现象学研究都至关重要。此前工作（如Marzucca等人2024年）讨论了超椭圆费曼积分（hyperelliptic Feynman integrals）不同表示之间的亏格下降（genus drop）现象，本文旨在进一步阐明该现象的几何机制并推广到更一般的情形。

Method: 本文重新表述了额外-对合机制（extra-involution mechanism）作为代数曲线（algebraic curves）间无分歧双覆盖（unramified double covering）的一个特例，并以此覆盖机制分析亏格下降现象。研究还考察了特定框架下离散时空对称性（discrete spacetime symmetry）的起源。

Result: 证明无分歧双覆盖机制能够解释一类三圈费曼图（three-loop Feynman diagrams）中伴随曲线类型从非超椭圆（non-hyperelliptic）变为超椭圆（hyperelliptic）的亏格下降现象。在超椭圆情形中，离散时空对称性的起源在特定框架下是显式的。此外，发现存在不表现出明显亏格下降的非超椭圆费曼积分。

Conclusion: 无分歧双覆盖是亏格下降现象的统一几何解释机制。超椭圆情形中的亏格下降可归因于离散时空对称性，而非超椭圆情形则可能存在无显式亏格下降的例子，表明该现象具有更丰富的结构。

Abstract: For both theoretical and phenomenological studies, it is important to analyze the function types of Feynman integrals. The phenomenon of genus drop between different representations of hyperelliptic Feynman integrals was discussed in \cite{Marzucca2024Genusdrop}. In this paper, we reformulate the extra-involution mechanism of \cite{Marzucca2024Genusdrop} as a special case of an unramified double covering between algebraic curves, and show that this covering mechanism also explains genus drops accompanied by a curve-type change from non-hyperelliptic to hyperelliptic for a class of three-loop Feynman diagrams. We also demonstrate that within a specific framework, the origin of the discrete spacetime symmetry that leads to the genus drop in hyperelliptic cases is manifest. This work also points out that there exist non-hyperelliptic Feynman integrals that exhibit no apparent genus drop.

</details>


### [146] [Characterizing bulk properties of gapped phases by smeared boundary conformal field theories: Role of duality in unusual ordering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07734)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study the classification of the gapped phases or massive renormalization group (RG) flows dual to the massless RG flows under changing the sign of the coupling constants. Whereas our formalism is based on combining Higgs- or Nambu-Goldstone-type arguments with Cardy's smeared boundary conformal field theories (SBCFTs), several puzzling structures arise. More specifically, the established Higgs or Nambu-Goldstone type arguments on the duality imply that the natural basis for the gapped states should be constructed from a set of smeared Ishibashi states, which are unphysical in boundary critical phenomena. Hence, the module of the gapped phases can be outside of that of boundary critical phenomena, whereas one can still calculate characterizing quantities by applying SBCFTs to the models. For example, we demonstrate that the massive RG flow dual to the massless RG flow from the tricritical Ising model to the Ising model, one of the simplest massless RG flows, has this unusual structure. This can be regarded as a quantum field-theoretic analogue of order-disorder coexistence in lattice models. More generally, the resultant gapped phases usually spontaneously break non-group-like symmetry (or noninvertible symmetry). Our work provides systematic quantum field theoretic descriptions of such unusual phases with spontaneous symmetry breaking of non-group-like (or noninvertible) symmetries.

Method: 从 $\mathrm{AdS}_3$ 中 Virasoro 演化与径向坐标 $r \to e^{2\pi i} r$ 的解析延拓出发，将对数引力子构造为 $L_0$ 的广义本征态（generalized eigenstate），并沿着 $L_{-1}$ 生成的 $SL(2,\mathbb{R})_L$ 后裔塔（descendant tower）分析其 Jordan 结构。通过要求单值性相容的 Virasoro 流（monodromy-compatible Virasoro flow），重构完整的不可分解对数模（indecomposable logarithmic module）。

Abstract: We construct and analyze the logarithmic sector of chiral Topologically Massive Gravity (TMG) at the critical point $μ\ell = 1$ from the perspective of Virasoro evolution and radial monodromy in $\mathrm{AdS}_3$. This establishes a direct identification between the LCFT Jordan cell structure and a geometric monodromy operator acting in the bulk.
  We demonstrate that requiring monodromy-compatible Virasoro flow uniquely reconstructs the full indecomposable logarithmic module, including all descendant levels, and show explicit equivalence with the logarithmic graviton module previously obtained in the linearized analysis of chiral TMG. Through a direct comparison with the Dirac and Klein-Gordon equations, we provide a geometric explanation for the absence of Klein paradox and the Schwinger effect in the Salpeter equation. ### [150] [Undulating Conformal Boundaries in 3D Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08058)
*Weam Abou Hamdan,Chawakorn Maneerat*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了三维欧几里得引力在环面拓扑有限边界上的半经典热力学相空间，发现对于负宇宙学常数且特定曲率范围存在热力学上有利的非均匀解，并分析了不同边界极限下的行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在欧几里得符号（Euclidean signature）下考虑三维爱因斯坦引力，边界为固定共形类诱导度规和常数值外曲率迹K的环面。对零、正、负宇宙学常数Λ三种情形，解析确定包围局部平坦、de Sitter（dS₃）和Anti-de Sitter（AdS₃）空间不同区域的边界，并分析解的拓扑依赖性和自交性质。

Result: 发现解对环面的两个周期存在非平凡依赖，部分解存在自交。大多数鞍点比均匀边界解热不稳定或亚稳态，但在Λ<0且2<K|Λ|⁻¹/²<3/√2条件下，存在热力学上有利的非均匀解。对所有Λ值，均存在具有非可缩热圆（non-contractible thermal circle）和宏观熵的空间区域。

Conclusion: 在AdS₃边界极限、拉伸dS₃视界极限（stretched dS₃ horizon limit）以及经典弦（classical strings）重述框架下，进一步分析了该问题，指出非均匀解在特定参数范围内具有潜在热力学优势。

Abstract: We consider three-dimensional Einstein gravity in Euclidean signature with a finite boundary of torus topology endowed with an induced metric of fixed conformal class and a constant trace of extrinsic curvature $K$. For vanishing, positive, and negative cosmological constant $Λ$, we analytically determine boundaries enclosing different patches of locally flat, de Sitter (dS$_3$), and Anti-de Sitter (AdS$_3$) spaces. We find solutions that depend non-trivially on either cycle of the torus, noting that some of them exhibit self-intersections. Adapting the Gibbons-Hawking prescription of interpreting the Euclidean gravitational path integral as a thermal partition function, we explore the rich semi-classical thermodynamic phase space of the problem. While most saddles are found to be either thermally unstable or metastable compared to those with uniform boundaries, we find inhomogeneous solutions that are thermodynamically favourable in the case of $Λ< 0$ and $2<K|Λ|^{-1/2}<3/\sqrt{2}$. Moreover, for all values of $Λ$, there exist patches of space with a non-contractible thermal circle and a macroscopic entropy. We further analyse the problem in both the AdS$_3$ boundary limit and the stretched dS$_3$ horizon limit, and comment on a recasting of the problem in terms of classical strings.

### [151] [The two-flavor Schwinger model at 50: Solving Coleman's puzzles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08042)
*Gabriel Cuomo,Ross Dempsey,Andrei Katsevich,Igor R. Klebanov,Ilia V. Kochergin,Silviu S. Pufu,Benjamin T. Søgaard*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过解析计算与数值模拟，解决了Coleman在1976年关于双味Schwinger模型（two-flavor Schwinger model）提出的三个谜题，涉及电荷共轭对称性自发破缺、能级交叉以及同位旋破缺效应的大小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Coleman在1976年的论文"More about the massive Schwinger model"中通过阿贝尔玻色化（Abelian bosonization）阐明了双味Schwinger模型的许多物理性质，但在文末提出了三个未解决的谜题。本文旨在通过新的解析和数值计算解决这些谜题，从而深化对该模型的理解。

Method: 采用双圈重整化群（two-loop Renormalization Group）和可积性方法（integrability methods）进行解析分析，并在格点哈密顿量（lattice Hamiltonian）框架下进行数值计算。

Result: 在θ=π时，电荷共轭对称性（charge conjugation symmetry）自发破缺，且对于任意规范耦合g都不存在禁闭（confinement），弱耦合到强耦合之间存在平滑插值；强耦合区（m≪g）的质量隙（mass gap）行为为∼ m e^{-0.111 g^2/m^2}。在θ=0时，存在两个不同离散量子数的同位旋单态粒子（isosinglet particles）之间的能级交叉（level crossing）。此外，给出了强耦合下由不同费米子质量引起的同位旋破缺效应（isospin-breaking effects）的新估计。

Conclusion: 本文成功解决了Coleman提出的三个谜题，揭示了双味Schwinger模型在θ=π和θ=0时的相图结构和动力学行为，并通过解析与数值方法的一致性验证了分析结果。

Abstract: In his 1976 paper "More about the massive Schwinger model", Coleman introduced $1+1$-dimensional Quantum Electrodynamics coupled to two charged massive fermions. By applying Abelian bosonization, he elucidated much of the physics of this two-flavor Schwinger model, but he listed three puzzles at the end of his paper. We present new analytical and numerical calculations to solve Coleman's three puzzles and thereby deepen our understanding of this model. These puzzles pertain to the theory with equal fermion masses at $θ= 0$ and at $θ= π$, as well as the size of isospin-breaking effects when the fermion masses are unequal. For the puzzle at $θ= π$, the solution is related to the structure of the zero-temperature phase diagram arXiv:2305.04437: for equal fermion masses $m$, the model exhibits spontaneous breaking of charge conjugation symmetry and absence of confinement for any value of the gauge coupling $g$, so that there is a smooth interpolation from weak to strong coupling. Using two-loop Renormalization Group and integrability methods, we show that the mass gap behaves as $\sim m e^{-0.111 g^2/m^2}$ in the strong coupling regime $m\ll g$. Our numerical results using the lattice Hamiltonian are in good agreement with this behavior. For the puzzle at $θ= 0$, the solution is related to a level crossing between two isosinglet particles with different discrete quantum numbers; we demonstrate the necessity of such a crossing by comparing integrability and weak coupling calculations, and we also exhibit the crossing numerically. Finally, we provide a new estimate for the size of isospin-breaking effects caused by different fermion masses at strong coupling.

### [152] [Fermionic trace relations and supersymmetric indices at finite $N$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08085)
*Giorgos Eleftheriou,Ziming Ji,Sameer Murthy*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在 U(N) 伴随作用下，由费米子数加权的玻色型和费米型（Grassmann 值）矩阵的不变量，发现费米型矩阵的 2N 次幂为零导致大量新迹关系，且费米子模型中的迹关系可能使超对称指标随 N 减小而增大，与纯玻色模型相反。针对 N=4 SYM 理论中的 1/4-BPS 超对称指标，作者解析证明了指标与 N 无关，并基于此提出了极化 Cayley-Hamilton 恒等式和 Grassmann 矩阵不变量第二基本定理等代数结构的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超对称规范理论中的超对称指标（supersymmetric indices）可自然表示为 U(N) 矩阵模型，但费米型（Grassmann-valued）矩阵与玻色型矩阵在不变量结构上存在本质差异，这些差异对指标行为的影响尚待系统理解。

Method: 采用解析证明与实验数值研究相结合的方法，分析费米型矩阵的迹关系（trace relations）及其对超对称指标的影响，并考察 N=4 超对称杨-米尔斯（SYM）理论中 1/4-BPS 超对称指标的 N 依赖性。

Result: 发现 Grassmann 矩阵的 2N 次幂为零，由此产生大量新迹关系；费米子模型中迹关系可能导致超对称指标随 N 减小而增大；对于 N=4 SYM 的 1/4-BPS 指标，解析证明了其与 N 无关。

Conclusion: 基于观测结果，提出了极化 Cayley-Hamilton 恒等式（polarized Cayley-Hamilton identities）和 Grassmann 矩阵不变量第二基本定理（Second Fundamental Theorem of invariants）的类比猜想；给出了 N=4 SYM 中最一般超对称指标的多种（光滑和奇异）极限，并研究了它们随 N 变化的模式。

Abstract: We study invariants of bosonic and fermionic (Grassmann-valued) matrices under the adjoint action of $U(N)$, weighted by the fermion number. Such models naturally appear as the supersymmetric indices of supersymmetric gauge theories and are captured by $U(N)$ matrix models. We discuss two features of the fermionic models that are qualitatively different from bosonic models. Firstly, the $2N^\text{th}$ power of a Grassmann matrix vanishes, which gives rise to many new trace relations. Secondly, trace relations in models involving fermions could cause an increase in the supersymmetric index as $N$ decreases, in contrast with purely bosonic models. We focus on a simple model involving one fermion and one derivative that corresponds to a $\frac14$-BPS supersymmetric index in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM theory, in which we find that the index is independent of $N$. We prove this rank-independence analytically, and experimentally study the cancellations between bosonic and fermionic trace relations that lead to it. Based on these observations, we make some conjectures on resulting algebraic structures, including the analogue of the polarized Cayley-Hamilton identities and the Second Fundamental Theorem of invariants in the presence of Grassmann matrices. Finally, we present various (smooth and singular) limits of the most general supersymmetric index in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM theory, and study some patterns in their behavior as a function of $N$.
